\footnotesize\addtolength{\baselineskip}{-1ex}
\begin{list}{}{\setlength{\itemsep}{-\parsep}\setlength{\itemindent}{-\leftmargin}}
\item \NWtxtMacroDefBy\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}.
\item \NWtxtMacroRefIn\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}.
\end{list}
\vspace{-2ex}
\footnotesize\addtolength{\baselineskip}{-1ex}
\begin{list}{}{\setlength{\itemsep}{-\parsep}\setlength{\itemindent}{-\leftmargin}}
\item \NWtxtIdentsUsed\nobreak\  \verb@command_name@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}.\end{list}
\end{minipage}\\[4ex]
\end{flushleft}
The invocation name is conventionally passed in \verb|argv[0]|.
\begin{flushleft} \small
\begin{minipage}{\linewidth} \label{scrap22}
$\langle\,${\it Interpret command-line arguments}\nobreak\ {\footnotesize \NWtarget{nuweb?}{?}}$\,\rangle\equiv$
\vspace{-1ex}
\begin{list}{}{} \item
\mbox{}\verb@command_name = argv[0];@\\
\mbox{}\verb@@{\NWsep}
\end{list}
\vspace{-1ex}
\footnotesize\addtolength{\baselineskip}{-1ex}
\begin{list}{}{\setlength{\itemsep}{-\parsep}\setlength{\itemindent}{-\leftmargin}}
\item \NWtxtMacroDefBy\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}.
\item \NWtxtMacroRefIn\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}.
\end{list}
\vspace{-2ex}
\footnotesize\addtolength{\baselineskip}{-1ex}
\begin{list}{}{\setlength{\itemsep}{-\parsep}\setlength{\itemindent}{-\leftmargin}}
\item \NWtxtIdentsUsed\nobreak\  \verb@command_name@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}.\end{list}
\end{minipage}\\[4ex]
\end{flushleft}
We need to examine the remaining entries in \verb|argv|, looking for
command-line arguments.
\begin{flushleft} \small
\begin{minipage}{\linewidth} \label{scrap23}
$\langle\,${\it Interpret command-line arguments}\nobreak\ {\footnotesize \NWtarget{nuweb?}{?}}$\,\rangle\equiv$
\vspace{-1ex}
\begin{list}{}{} \item
\mbox{}\verb@while (arg < argc) {@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  char *s = argv[arg];@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  if (*s++ == '-') {@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    @\hbox{$\langle\,${\it Interpret the argument string \verb|s|}\nobreak\ {\footnotesize \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}}$\,\rangle$}\verb@@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    arg++;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    @\hbox{$\langle\,${\it Perhaps get the prepend path}\nobreak\ {\footnotesize \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}}$\,\rangle$}\verb@@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  }@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  else break;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@}@{\NWsep}
\end{list}
\vspace{-1ex}
\footnotesize\addtolength{\baselineskip}{-1ex}
\begin{list}{}{\setlength{\itemsep}{-\parsep}\setlength{\itemindent}{-\leftmargin}}
\item \NWtxtMacroDefBy\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}.
\item \NWtxtMacroRefIn\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}.
\end{list}
\end{minipage}\\[4ex]
\end{flushleft}
Several flags can be stacked behind a single minus sign; therefore,
we've got to loop through the string, handling them all.
\begin{flushleft} \small
\begin{minipage}{\linewidth} \label{scrap24}
$\langle\,${\it Interpret the argument string \verb|s|}\nobreak\ {\footnotesize \NWtarget{nuweb?}{?}}$\,\rangle\equiv$
\vspace{-1ex}
\begin{list}{}{} \item
\mbox{}\verb@{@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  char c = *s++;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  while (c) {@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    switch (c) {@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      case 'c': compare_flag = FALSE;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@                break;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      case 'd': dangling_flag = TRUE;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@                break;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      case 'n': number_flag = TRUE;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@                break;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      case 'o': output_flag = FALSE;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@                break;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      case 's': scrap_flag = FALSE;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@                break;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      case 't': tex_flag = FALSE;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@                break;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      case 'v': verbose_flag = TRUE;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@                break;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      case 'p': prepend_flag = TRUE;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@                break;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      case 'l': listings_flag = TRUE;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@                break;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      case 'r': hyperref_flag = TRUE;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@                break;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      case 'u': undefined_flag = TRUE;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@                break;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      case 'a': arglabels_flag = TRUE;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@                break;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      default:  fprintf(stderr, "%s: unexpected argument ignored.  ",@\\
\mbox{}\verb@                        command_name);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@                fprintf(stderr, "Usage is: %s [-clnortv] [-p path] file...\n",@\\
\mbox{}\verb@                        command_name);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@                break;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    }@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    c = *s++;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  }@\\
\mbox{}\verb@}@{\NWsep}
\end{list}
\vspace{-1ex}
\footnotesize\addtolength{\baselineskip}{-1ex}
\begin{list}{}{\setlength{\itemsep}{-\parsep}\setlength{\itemindent}{-\leftmargin}}
\item \NWtxtMacroRefIn\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}.
\end{list}
\vspace{-2ex}
\footnotesize\addtolength{\baselineskip}{-1ex}
\begin{list}{}{\setlength{\itemsep}{-\parsep}\setlength{\itemindent}{-\leftmargin}}
\item \NWtxtIdentsUsed\nobreak\  \verb@arglabels_flag@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}, \verb@command_name@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}, \verb@compare_flag@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}, \verb@dangling_flag@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}, \verb@FALSE@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}, \verb@fprintf@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}, \verb@hyperref_flag@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}, \verb@listings_flag@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}, \verb@number_flag@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}, \verb@output_flag@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}, \verb@scrap_flag@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}, \verb@stderr@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}, \verb@tex_flag@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}, \verb@TRUE@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}, \verb@undefined_flag@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}, \verb@verbose_flag@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}.\end{list}
\end{minipage}\\[4ex]
\end{flushleft}
\begin{flushleft} \small
\begin{minipage}{\linewidth} \label{scrap25}
$\langle\,${\it Perhaps get the prepend path}\nobreak\ {\footnotesize \NWtarget{nuweb?}{?}}$\,\rangle\equiv$
\vspace{-1ex}
\begin{list}{}{} \item
\mbox{}\verb@if (prepend_flag)@\\
\mbox{}\verb@{@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  dirpath = argv[arg++];@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  prepend_flag = FALSE;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@}@\\
\mbox{}\verb@@{\NWsep}
\end{list}
\vspace{-1ex}
\footnotesize\addtolength{\baselineskip}{-1ex}
\begin{list}{}{\setlength{\itemsep}{-\parsep}\setlength{\itemindent}{-\leftmargin}}
\item \NWtxtMacroRefIn\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}.
\end{list}
\vspace{-2ex}
\footnotesize\addtolength{\baselineskip}{-1ex}
\begin{list}{}{\setlength{\itemsep}{-\parsep}\setlength{\itemindent}{-\leftmargin}}
\item \NWtxtIdentsUsed\nobreak\  \verb@FALSE@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}.\end{list}
\end{minipage}\\[4ex]
\end{flushleft}
In order to be able to process files in foreign languages we
set the locale information. \texttt{isgraph()} and friends need
this (see Section~\ref{names}).
Try to read \texttt{LC\_CTYPE} from the environment. Use \texttt{LC\_ALL}
if that fails. Don't set the locale if reading \texttt{LC\_ALL} fails, too.
Print a warning if setting the program's locale failes.
\begin{flushleft} \small
\begin{minipage}{\linewidth} \label{scrap26}
$\langle\,${\it Set locale information}\nobreak\ {\footnotesize \NWtarget{nuweb?}{?}}$\,\rangle\equiv$
\vspace{-1ex}
\begin{list}{}{} \item
\mbox{}\verb@@\\
\mbox{}\verb@{@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  /* try to get locale information */@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  char *s=getenv("LC_CTYPE");@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  if (s==NULL) s=getenv("LC_ALL");@\\
\mbox{}\verb@@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  /* set it */@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  if (s!=NULL)@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    if(setlocale(LC_CTYPE, s)==NULL)@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      fprintf(stderr, "Setting locale failed\n");@\\
\mbox{}\verb@}@\\
\mbox{}\verb@@{\NWsep}
\end{list}
\vspace{-1ex}
\footnotesize\addtolength{\baselineskip}{-1ex}
\begin{list}{}{\setlength{\itemsep}{-\parsep}\setlength{\itemindent}{-\leftmargin}}
\item \NWtxtMacroRefIn\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}.
\end{list}
\vspace{-2ex}
\footnotesize\addtolength{\baselineskip}{-1ex}
\begin{list}{}{\setlength{\itemsep}{-\parsep}\setlength{\itemindent}{-\leftmargin}}
\item \NWtxtIdentsDefed\nobreak\  \verb@getenv@\nobreak\ \NWtxtIdentsNotUsed, \verb@setlocale@\nobreak\ \NWtxtIdentsNotUsed.\end{list}
\vspace{-2ex}
\footnotesize\addtolength{\baselineskip}{-1ex}
\begin{list}{}{\setlength{\itemsep}{-\parsep}\setlength{\itemindent}{-\leftmargin}}
\item \NWtxtIdentsUsed\nobreak\  \verb@fprintf@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}, \verb@stderr@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}.\end{list}
\end{minipage}\\[4ex]
\end{flushleft}
\subsection{File Names}

We expect at least one file name. While a missing file name might be
ignored without causing any problems, we take the opportunity to report
the usage convention.
\begin{flushleft} \small
\begin{minipage}{\linewidth} \label{scrap27}
$\langle\,${\it Process the remaining arguments (file names)}\nobreak\ {\footnotesize \NWtarget{nuweb?}{?}}$\,\rangle\equiv$
\vspace{-1ex}
\begin{list}{}{} \item
\mbox{}\verb@{@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  if (arg >= argc) {@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    fprintf(stderr, "%s: expected a file name.  ", command_name);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    fprintf(stderr, "Usage is: %s [-clnortv] [-p path] file-name...\n", command_name);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    exit(-1);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  }@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  do {@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    @\hbox{$\langle\,${\it Handle the file name in \verb|argv[arg]|}\nobreak\ {\footnotesize \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}}$\,\rangle$}\verb@@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    arg++;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  } while (arg < argc);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@}@{\NWsep}
\end{list}
\vspace{-1ex}
\footnotesize\addtolength{\baselineskip}{-1ex}
\begin{list}{}{\setlength{\itemsep}{-\parsep}\setlength{\itemindent}{-\leftmargin}}
\item \NWtxtMacroRefIn\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}.
\end{list}
\vspace{-2ex}
\footnotesize\addtolength{\baselineskip}{-1ex}
\begin{list}{}{\setlength{\itemsep}{-\parsep}\setlength{\itemindent}{-\leftmargin}}
\item \NWtxtIdentsUsed\nobreak\  \verb@command_name@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}, \verb@exit@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}, \verb@fprintf@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}, \verb@stderr@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}.\end{list}
\end{minipage}\\[4ex]
\end{flushleft}
\newpage
\noindent
The code to handle a particular file name is rather more tedious than
the actual processing of the file. A file name may be an arbitrarily
complicated path name, with an optional extension. If no extension is
present, we add \verb|.w| as a default. The extended path name will be
kept in a local variable \verb|source_name|. The resulting documentation
file will be written in the current directory; its name will be kept
in the variable \verb|tex_name|.
\begin{flushleft} \small
\begin{minipage}{\linewidth} \label{scrap28}
$\langle\,${\it Handle the file name in \verb|argv[arg]|}\nobreak\ {\footnotesize \NWtarget{nuweb?}{?}}$\,\rangle\equiv$
\vspace{-1ex}
\begin{list}{}{} \item
\mbox{}\verb@{@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  char source_name[FILENAME_MAX];@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  char tex_name[FILENAME_MAX];@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  char aux_name[FILENAME_MAX];@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  @\hbox{$\langle\,${\it Build \verb|source_name| and \verb|tex_name|}\nobreak\ {\footnotesize \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}}$\,\rangle$}\verb@@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  @\hbox{$\langle\,${\it Process a file}\nobreak\ {\footnotesize \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}}$\,\rangle$}\verb@@\\
\mbox{}\verb@}@{\NWsep}
\end{list}
\vspace{-1ex}
\footnotesize\addtolength{\baselineskip}{-1ex}
\begin{list}{}{\setlength{\itemsep}{-\parsep}\setlength{\itemindent}{-\leftmargin}}
\item \NWtxtMacroRefIn\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}.
\end{list}
\vspace{-2ex}
\footnotesize\addtolength{\baselineskip}{-1ex}
\begin{list}{}{\setlength{\itemsep}{-\parsep}\setlength{\itemindent}{-\leftmargin}}
\item \NWtxtIdentsUsed\nobreak\  \verb@source_name@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}.\end{list}
\end{minipage}\\[4ex]
\end{flushleft}
I bump the pointer \verb|p| through all the characters in \verb|argv[arg]|,
copying all the characters into \verb|source_name| (via the pointer
\verb|q|). 

At each slash, I update \verb|trim| to point just past the
slash in \verb|source_name|. The effect is that \verb|trim| will point
at the file name without any leading directory specifications.

The pointer \verb|dot| is made to point at the file name extension, if
present. If there is no extension, we add \verb|.w| to the source name.
In any case, we create the \verb|tex_name| from \verb|trim|, taking
care to get the correct extension.  The \verb|html_flag| is set in
this scrap.
\begin{flushleft} \small
\begin{minipage}{\linewidth} \label{scrap29}
$\langle\,${\it Build \verb|source_name| and \verb|tex_name|}\nobreak\ {\footnotesize \NWtarget{nuweb?}{?}}$\,\rangle\equiv$
\vspace{-1ex}
\begin{list}{}{} \item
\mbox{}\verb@{@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  char *p = argv[arg];@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  char *q = source_name;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  char *trim = q;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  char *dot = NULL;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  char c = *p++;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  while (c) {@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    *q++ = c;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    if (PATH_SEP(c)) {@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      trim = q;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      dot = NULL;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    }@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    else if (c == '.')@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      dot = q - 1;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    c = *p++;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  }@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  *q = '\0';@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  if (dot) {@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    *dot = '\0'; /* produce HTML when the file extension is ".hw" */@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    html_flag = dot[1] == 'h' && dot[2] == 'w' && dot[3] == '\0';@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    sprintf(tex_name, "%s%s%s.tex", dirpath, path_sep, trim);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    sprintf(aux_name, "%s%s%s.aux", dirpath, path_sep, trim);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    *dot = '.';@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  }@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  else {@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    sprintf(tex_name, "%s%s%s.tex", dirpath, path_sep, trim);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    sprintf(aux_name, "%s%s%s.aux", dirpath, path_sep, trim);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    *q++ = '.';@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    *q++ = 'w';@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    *q = '\0';@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  }@\\
\mbox{}\verb@}@{\NWsep}
\end{list}
\vspace{-1ex}
\footnotesize\addtolength{\baselineskip}{-1ex}
\begin{list}{}{\setlength{\itemsep}{-\parsep}\setlength{\itemindent}{-\leftmargin}}
\item \NWtxtMacroRefIn\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}.
\end{list}
\vspace{-2ex}
\footnotesize\addtolength{\baselineskip}{-1ex}
\begin{list}{}{\setlength{\itemsep}{-\parsep}\setlength{\itemindent}{-\leftmargin}}
\item \NWtxtIdentsUsed\nobreak\  \verb@html_flag@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}, \verb@source_name@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}.\end{list}
\end{minipage}\\[4ex]
\end{flushleft}
Now that we're finally ready to process a file, it's not really too
complex.  We bundle most of the work into four routines \verb|pass1|
(see Section~\ref{pass-one}), \verb|write_tex| (see
Section~\ref{latex-file}), \verb|write_html| (see
Section~\ref{html-file}), and \verb|write_files| (see
Section~\ref{output-files}). After we're finished with a
particular file, we must remember to release its storage (see
Section~\ref{memory-management}).  The sequential numbering of scraps
is forced when generating HTML.
\begin{flushleft} \small
\begin{minipage}{\linewidth} \label{scrap30}
$\langle\,${\it Process a file}\nobreak\ {\footnotesize \NWtarget{nuweb?}{?}}$\,\rangle\equiv$
\vspace{-1ex}
\begin{list}{}{} \item
\mbox{}\verb@{@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  pass1(source_name);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  current_sector = 1;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  if (tex_flag) {@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    if (html_flag) {@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      int saved_number_flag = number_flag; @\\
\mbox{}\verb@      number_flag = TRUE;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      collect_numbers(aux_name);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      write_html(source_name, tex_name, 0/*Dummy */);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      number_flag = saved_number_flag;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    }@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    else {@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      collect_numbers(aux_name);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      write_tex(source_name, tex_name);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    }@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  }@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  if (output_flag)@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    write_files(file_names);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  arena_free();@\\
\mbox{}\verb@}@{\NWsep}
\end{list}
\vspace{-1ex}
\footnotesize\addtolength{\baselineskip}{-1ex}
\begin{list}{}{\setlength{\itemsep}{-\parsep}\setlength{\itemindent}{-\leftmargin}}
\item \NWtxtMacroRefIn\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}.
\end{list}
\vspace{-2ex}
\footnotesize\addtolength{\baselineskip}{-1ex}
\begin{list}{}{\setlength{\itemsep}{-\parsep}\setlength{\itemindent}{-\leftmargin}}
\item \NWtxtIdentsUsed\nobreak\  \verb@arena_free@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}, \verb@collect_numbers@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}, \verb@current_sector@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}, \verb@file_names@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}, \verb@html_flag@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}, \verb@number_flag@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}, \verb@output_flag@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}, \verb@pass1@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}, \verb@source_name@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}, \verb@tex_flag@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}, \verb@TRUE@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}, \verb@write_files@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}, \verb@write_html@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}, \verb@write_tex@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}.\end{list}
\end{minipage}\\[4ex]
\end{flushleft}
\newpage
\section{Pass One} \label{pass-one}

During the first pass, we scan the file, recording the definitions of
each macro and file and accumulating all the scraps. 

\begin{flushleft} \small
\begin{minipage}{\linewidth} \label{scrap31}
$\langle\,${\it Function prototypes}\nobreak\ {\footnotesize \NWtarget{nuweb?}{?}}$\,\rangle\equiv$
\vspace{-1ex}
\begin{list}{}{} \item
\mbox{}\verb@extern void pass1();@\\
\mbox{}\verb@@{\NWsep}
\end{list}
\vspace{-1ex}
\footnotesize\addtolength{\baselineskip}{-1ex}
\begin{list}{}{\setlength{\itemsep}{-\parsep}\setlength{\itemindent}{-\leftmargin}}
\item \NWtxtMacroDefBy\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}.
\item \NWtxtMacroRefIn\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}.
\end{list}
\vspace{-2ex}
\footnotesize\addtolength{\baselineskip}{-1ex}
\begin{list}{}{\setlength{\itemsep}{-\parsep}\setlength{\itemindent}{-\leftmargin}}
\item \NWtxtIdentsUsed\nobreak\  \verb@pass1@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}.\end{list}
\end{minipage}\\[4ex]
\end{flushleft}
The routine \verb|pass1| takes a single argument, the name of the
source file. It opens the file, then initializes the scrap structures
(see Section~\ref{scraps}) and the roots of the file-name tree, the
macro-name tree, and the tree of user-specified index entries (see 
Section~\ref{names}). After completing all the
necessary preparation, we make a pass over the file, filling in all
our data structures. Next, we seach all the scraps for references to
the user-specified index entries. Finally, we must reverse all the
cross-reference lists accumulated while scanning the scraps.
\begin{flushleft} \small
\begin{minipage}{\linewidth} \label{scrap32}
\verb@"pass1.c"@\nobreak\ {\footnotesize \NWtarget{nuweb?}{?} }$\equiv$
\vspace{-1ex}
\begin{list}{}{} \item
\mbox{}\verb@void pass1(file_name)@\\
\mbox{}\verb@     char *file_name;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@{@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  if (verbose_flag)@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    fprintf(stderr, "reading %s\n", file_name);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  source_open(file_name);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  init_scraps();@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  macro_names = NULL;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  file_names = NULL;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  user_names = NULL;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  @\hbox{$\langle\,${\it Scan the source file, looking for at-sequences}\nobreak\ {\footnotesize \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}}$\,\rangle$}\verb@@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  if (tex_flag)@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    search();@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  @\hbox{$\langle\,${\it Reverse cross-reference lists}\nobreak\ {\footnotesize \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}}$\,\rangle$}\verb@@\\
\mbox{}\verb@}@\\
\mbox{}\verb@@{\NWsep}
\end{list}
\vspace{-1ex}
\footnotesize\addtolength{\baselineskip}{-1ex}
\begin{list}{}{\setlength{\itemsep}{-\parsep}\setlength{\itemindent}{-\leftmargin}}
\item \NWtxtFileDefBy\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}.
\end{list}
\vspace{-2ex}
\footnotesize\addtolength{\baselineskip}{-1ex}
\begin{list}{}{\setlength{\itemsep}{-\parsep}\setlength{\itemindent}{-\leftmargin}}
\item \NWtxtIdentsDefed\nobreak\  \verb@pass1@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}.\end{list}
\vspace{-2ex}
\footnotesize\addtolength{\baselineskip}{-1ex}
\begin{list}{}{\setlength{\itemsep}{-\parsep}\setlength{\itemindent}{-\leftmargin}}
\item \NWtxtIdentsUsed\nobreak\  \verb@file_names@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}, \verb@fprintf@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}, \verb@init_scraps@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}, \verb@macro_names@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}, \verb@search@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}, \verb@source_open@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}, \verb@stderr@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}, \verb@tex_flag@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}, \verb@user_names@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}, \verb@verbose_flag@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}.\end{list}
\end{minipage}\\[4ex]
\end{flushleft}
The only thing we look for in the first pass are the command
sequences. All ordinary text is skipped entirely.
\begin{flushleft} \small
\begin{minipage}{\linewidth} \label{scrap33}
$\langle\,${\it Scan the source file, looking for at-sequences}\nobreak\ {\footnotesize \NWtarget{nuweb?}{?}}$\,\rangle\equiv$
\vspace{-1ex}
\begin{list}{}{} \item
\mbox{}\verb@{@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  int c = source_get();@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  while (c != EOF) {@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    if (c == nw_char)@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      @\hbox{$\langle\,${\it Scan at-sequence}\nobreak\ {\footnotesize \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}}$\,\rangle$}\verb@@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    c = source_get();@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  }@\\
\mbox{}\verb@}@{\NWsep}
\end{list}
\vspace{-1ex}
\footnotesize\addtolength{\baselineskip}{-1ex}
\begin{list}{}{\setlength{\itemsep}{-\parsep}\setlength{\itemindent}{-\leftmargin}}
\item \NWtxtMacroRefIn\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}.
\end{list}
\vspace{-2ex}
\footnotesize\addtolength{\baselineskip}{-1ex}
\begin{list}{}{\setlength{\itemsep}{-\parsep}\setlength{\itemindent}{-\leftmargin}}
\item \NWtxtIdentsUsed\nobreak\  \verb@nw_char@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}, \verb@source_get@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}.\end{list}
\end{minipage}\\[4ex]
\end{flushleft}
Only four of the at-sequences are interesting during the first pass.
We skip past others immediately; warning if unexpected sequences are
discovered.
\begin{flushleft} \small
\begin{minipage}{\linewidth} \label{scrap34}
$\langle\,${\it Scan at-sequence}\nobreak\ {\footnotesize \NWtarget{nuweb?}{?}}$\,\rangle\equiv$
\vspace{-1ex}
\begin{list}{}{} \item
\mbox{}\verb@{@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  c = source_get();@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  switch (c) {@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    case 'r':@\\
\mbox{}\verb@          c = source_get();@\\
\mbox{}\verb@          nw_char = c;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@          update_delimit_scrap();@\\
\mbox{}\verb@          break;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    case 'O':@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    case 'o': @\hbox{$\langle\,${\it Build output file definition}\nobreak\ {\footnotesize \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}}$\,\rangle$}\verb@@\\
\mbox{}\verb@              break;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    case 'D':@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    case 'd': @\hbox{$\langle\,${\it Build macro definition}\nobreak\ {\footnotesize \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}}$\,\rangle$}\verb@@\\
\mbox{}\verb@              break;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    case 's':@\\
\mbox{}\verb@              @\hbox{$\langle\,${\it Step to next sector}\nobreak\ {\footnotesize \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}}$\,\rangle$}\verb@@\\
\mbox{}\verb@              break;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    case '(':@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    case '[':@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    case '{': @\hbox{$\langle\,${\it Skip over an in-text scrap}\nobreak\ {\footnotesize \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}}$\,\rangle$}\verb@@\\
\mbox{}\verb@              break;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    case 'x': @\\
\mbox{}\verb@    case 'u':@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    case 'm':@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    case 'f': /* ignore during this pass */@\\
\mbox{}\verb@              break;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    default:  if (c==nw_char) /* ignore during this pass */@\\
\mbox{}\verb@                break;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@              fprintf(stderr,@\\
\mbox{}\verb@                      "%s: unexpected %c sequence ignored (%s, line %d)\n",@\\
\mbox{}\verb@                      command_name, nw_char, source_name, source_line);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@              break;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  }@\\
\mbox{}\verb@}@{\NWsep}
\end{list}
\vspace{-1ex}
\footnotesize\addtolength{\baselineskip}{-1ex}
\begin{list}{}{\setlength{\itemsep}{-\parsep}\setlength{\itemindent}{-\leftmargin}}
\item \NWtxtMacroRefIn\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}.
\end{list}
\vspace{-2ex}
\footnotesize\addtolength{\baselineskip}{-1ex}
\begin{list}{}{\setlength{\itemsep}{-\parsep}\setlength{\itemindent}{-\leftmargin}}
\item \NWtxtIdentsUsed\nobreak\  \verb@command_name@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}, \verb@fprintf@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}, \verb@nw_char@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}, \verb@source_get@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}, \verb@source_line@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}, \verb@source_name@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}, \verb@stderr@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}, \verb@update_delimit_scrap@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}.\end{list}
\end{minipage}\\[4ex]
\end{flushleft}
\begin{flushleft} \small
\begin{minipage}{\linewidth} \label{scrap35}
$\langle\,${\it Step to next sector}\nobreak\ {\footnotesize \NWtarget{nuweb?}{?}}$\,\rangle\equiv$
\vspace{-1ex}
\begin{list}{}{} \item
\mbox{}\verb@@\\
\mbox{}\verb@current_sector += 1;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@do@\\
\mbox{}\verb@   c = source_get();@\\
\mbox{}\verb@while (isspace(c));@\\
\mbox{}\verb@@{\NWsep}
\end{list}
\vspace{-1ex}
\footnotesize\addtolength{\baselineskip}{-1ex}
\begin{list}{}{\setlength{\itemsep}{-\parsep}\setlength{\itemindent}{-\leftmargin}}
\item \NWtxtMacroRefIn\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}.
\end{list}
\vspace{-2ex}
\footnotesize\addtolength{\baselineskip}{-1ex}
\begin{list}{}{\setlength{\itemsep}{-\parsep}\setlength{\itemindent}{-\leftmargin}}
\item \NWtxtIdentsUsed\nobreak\  \verb@current_sector@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}, \verb@isspace@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}, \verb@source_get@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}.\end{list}
\end{minipage}\\[4ex]
\end{flushleft}
\begin{flushleft} \small
\begin{minipage}{\linewidth} \label{scrap36}
$\langle\,${\it Global variable declarations}\nobreak\ {\footnotesize \NWtarget{nuweb?}{?}}$\,\rangle\equiv$
\vspace{-1ex}
\begin{list}{}{} \item
\mbox{}\verb@unsigned char current_sector;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@@{\NWsep}
\end{list}
\vspace{-1ex}
\footnotesize\addtolength{\baselineskip}{-1ex}
\begin{list}{}{\setlength{\itemsep}{-\parsep}\setlength{\itemindent}{-\leftmargin}}
\item \NWtxtMacroDefBy\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}.
\item \NWtxtMacroRefIn\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}.
\end{list}
\vspace{-2ex}
\footnotesize\addtolength{\baselineskip}{-1ex}
\begin{list}{}{\setlength{\itemsep}{-\parsep}\setlength{\itemindent}{-\leftmargin}}
\item \NWtxtIdentsDefed\nobreak\  \verb@current_sector@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}.\end{list}
\end{minipage}\\[4ex]
\end{flushleft}
\begin{flushleft} \small
\begin{minipage}{\linewidth} \label{scrap37}
$\langle\,${\it Global variable definitions}\nobreak\ {\footnotesize \NWtarget{nuweb?}{?}}$\,\rangle\equiv$
\vspace{-1ex}
\begin{list}{}{} \item
\mbox{}\verb@unsigned char current_sector = 1;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@@{\NWsep}
\end{list}
\vspace{-1ex}
\footnotesize\addtolength{\baselineskip}{-1ex}
\begin{list}{}{\setlength{\itemsep}{-\parsep}\setlength{\itemindent}{-\leftmargin}}
\item \NWtxtMacroDefBy\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}.
\item \NWtxtMacroRefIn\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}.
\end{list}
\vspace{-2ex}
\footnotesize\addtolength{\baselineskip}{-1ex}
\begin{list}{}{\setlength{\itemsep}{-\parsep}\setlength{\itemindent}{-\leftmargin}}
\item \NWtxtIdentsUsed\nobreak\  \verb@current_sector@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}.\end{list}
\end{minipage}\\[4ex]
\end{flushleft}
\subsection{Accumulating Definitions}

There are three steps required to handle a definition:
\begin{enumerate}
  \item Build an entry for the name so we can look it up later.
  \item Collect the scrap and save it in the table of scraps.
  \item Attach the scrap to the name.
\end{enumerate}
We go through the same steps for both file names and macro names.
\begin{flushleft} \small
\begin{minipage}{\linewidth} \label{scrap38}
$\langle\,${\it Build output file definition}\nobreak\ {\footnotesize \NWtarget{nuweb?}{?}}$\,\rangle\equiv$
\vspace{-1ex}
\begin{list}{}{} \item
\mbox{}\verb@{@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  Name *name = collect_file_name(); /* returns a pointer to the name entry */@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  int scrap = collect_scrap();      /* returns an index to the scrap */@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  @\hbox{$\langle\,${\it Add \verb|scrap| to \verb|name|'s definition list}\nobreak\ {\footnotesize \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}}$\,\rangle$}\verb@@\\
\mbox{}\verb@}@{\NWsep}
\end{list}
\vspace{-1ex}
\footnotesize\addtolength{\baselineskip}{-1ex}
\begin{list}{}{\setlength{\itemsep}{-\parsep}\setlength{\itemindent}{-\leftmargin}}
\item \NWtxtMacroRefIn\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}.
\end{list}
\vspace{-2ex}
\footnotesize\addtolength{\baselineskip}{-1ex}
\begin{list}{}{\setlength{\itemsep}{-\parsep}\setlength{\itemindent}{-\leftmargin}}
\item \NWtxtIdentsUsed\nobreak\  \verb@collect_file_name@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}, \verb@collect_scrap@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}, \verb@Name@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}.\end{list}
\end{minipage}\\[4ex]
\end{flushleft}
\begin{flushleft} \small
\begin{minipage}{\linewidth} \label{scrap39}
$\langle\,${\it Build macro definition}\nobreak\ {\footnotesize \NWtarget{nuweb?}{?}}$\,\rangle\equiv$
\vspace{-1ex}
\begin{list}{}{} \item
\mbox{}\verb@{@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  Name *name = collect_macro_name();@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  int scrap = collect_scrap();@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  @\hbox{$\langle\,${\it Add \verb|scrap| to \verb|name|'s definition list}\nobreak\ {\footnotesize \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}}$\,\rangle$}\verb@@\\
\mbox{}\verb@}@{\NWsep}
\end{list}
\vspace{-1ex}
\footnotesize\addtolength{\baselineskip}{-1ex}
\begin{list}{}{\setlength{\itemsep}{-\parsep}\setlength{\itemindent}{-\leftmargin}}
\item \NWtxtMacroRefIn\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}.
\end{list}
\vspace{-2ex}
\footnotesize\addtolength{\baselineskip}{-1ex}
\begin{list}{}{\setlength{\itemsep}{-\parsep}\setlength{\itemindent}{-\leftmargin}}
\item \NWtxtIdentsUsed\nobreak\  \verb@collect_macro_name@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}, \verb@collect_scrap@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}, \verb@Name@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}.\end{list}
\end{minipage}\\[4ex]
\end{flushleft}
Since a file or macro may be defined by many scraps, we maintain them
in a simple linked list. The list is actually built in reverse order,
with each new definition being added to the head of the list.
\begin{flushleft} \small
\begin{minipage}{\linewidth} \label{scrap40}
$\langle\,${\it Add \verb|scrap| to \verb|name|'s definition list}\nobreak\ {\footnotesize \NWtarget{nuweb?}{?}}$\,\rangle\equiv$
\vspace{-1ex}
\begin{list}{}{} \item
\mbox{}\verb@{@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  Scrap_Node *def = (Scrap_Node *) arena_getmem(sizeof(Scrap_Node));@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  def->scrap = scrap;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  def->next = name->defs;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  name->defs = def;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@}@{\NWsep}
\end{list}
\vspace{-1ex}
\footnotesize\addtolength{\baselineskip}{-1ex}
\begin{list}{}{\setlength{\itemsep}{-\parsep}\setlength{\itemindent}{-\leftmargin}}
\item \NWtxtMacroRefIn\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}.
\end{list}
\vspace{-2ex}
\footnotesize\addtolength{\baselineskip}{-1ex}
\begin{list}{}{\setlength{\itemsep}{-\parsep}\setlength{\itemindent}{-\leftmargin}}
\item \NWtxtIdentsUsed\nobreak\  \verb@arena_getmem@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}, \verb@Scrap_Node@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}.\end{list}
\end{minipage}\\[4ex]
\end{flushleft}
\begin{flushleft} \small
\begin{minipage}{\linewidth} \label{scrap41}
$\langle\,${\it Skip over an in-text scrap}\nobreak\ {\footnotesize \NWtarget{nuweb?}{?}}$\,\rangle\equiv$
\vspace{-1ex}
\begin{list}{}{} \item
\mbox{}\verb@@\\
\mbox{}\verb@{@\\
\mbox{}\verb@@\\
\mbox{}\verb@   int c;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@   while ((c = source_get()) != EOF) {@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      if (c == nw_char)@\\
\mbox{}\verb@         @\hbox{$\langle\,${\it Skip over at-sign or go to skipped}\nobreak\ {\footnotesize \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}}$\,\rangle$}\verb@@\\
\mbox{}\verb@   }@\\
\mbox{}\verb@   fprintf(stderr, "%s: unexpected EOF in text at (%s, %d)\n",@\\
\mbox{}\verb@                    command_name, source_name, source_line);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@   exit(-1);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@@\\
\mbox{}\verb@skipped:@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  ;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@}@\\
\mbox{}\verb@@{\NWsep}
\end{list}
\vspace{-1ex}
\footnotesize\addtolength{\baselineskip}{-1ex}
\begin{list}{}{\setlength{\itemsep}{-\parsep}\setlength{\itemindent}{-\leftmargin}}
\item \NWtxtMacroRefIn\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}.
\end{list}
\vspace{-2ex}
\footnotesize\addtolength{\baselineskip}{-1ex}
\begin{list}{}{\setlength{\itemsep}{-\parsep}\setlength{\itemindent}{-\leftmargin}}
\item \NWtxtIdentsUsed\nobreak\  \verb@command_name@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}, \verb@exit@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}, \verb@fprintf@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}, \verb@nw_char@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}, \verb@source_get@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}, \verb@source_line@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}, \verb@source_name@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}, \verb@stderr@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}.\end{list}
\end{minipage}\\[4ex]
\end{flushleft}
\begin{flushleft} \small
\begin{minipage}{\linewidth} \label{scrap42}
$\langle\,${\it Skip over at-sign or go to skipped}\nobreak\ {\footnotesize \NWtarget{nuweb?}{?}}$\,\rangle\equiv$
\vspace{-1ex}
\begin{list}{}{} \item
\mbox{}\verb@@\\
\mbox{}\verb@{@\\
\mbox{}\verb@   c = source_get();@\\
\mbox{}\verb@   switch (c) {@\\
\mbox{}\verb@     case '}': case ']': case ')':@\\
\mbox{}\verb@        goto skipped;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@     case 'x': case '|': case ',': case '<':@\\
\mbox{}\verb@     case '>': case '%': case '1': case '2':@\\
\mbox{}\verb@     case '3': case '4': case '5': case '6':@\\
\mbox{}\verb@     case '7': case '8': case '9': case '_':@\\
\mbox{}\verb@     case 'f': case '#': case '+': case '-':@\\
\mbox{}\verb@        break;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@     default:@\\
\mbox{}\verb@        if (c != nw_char) {@\\
\mbox{}\verb@           fprintf(stderr, "%s: unexpected %c%c in text at (%s, %d)\n",@\\
\mbox{}\verb@                           command_name, nw_char, c, source_name, source_line);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@           exit(-1);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@        }@\\
\mbox{}\verb@        break;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@   }@\\
\mbox{}\verb@}@\\
\mbox{}\verb@@{\NWsep}
\end{list}
\vspace{-1ex}
\footnotesize\addtolength{\baselineskip}{-1ex}
\begin{list}{}{\setlength{\itemsep}{-\parsep}\setlength{\itemindent}{-\leftmargin}}
\item \NWtxtMacroRefIn\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}.
\end{list}
\vspace{-2ex}
\footnotesize\addtolength{\baselineskip}{-1ex}
\begin{list}{}{\setlength{\itemsep}{-\parsep}\setlength{\itemindent}{-\leftmargin}}
\item \NWtxtIdentsUsed\nobreak\  \verb@command_name@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}, \verb@exit@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}, \verb@fprintf@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}, \verb@nw_char@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}, \verb@source_get@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}, \verb@source_line@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}, \verb@source_name@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}, \verb@stderr@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}.\end{list}
\end{minipage}\\[4ex]
\end{flushleft}
\subsection{Fixing the Cross References}

Since the definition and reference lists for each name are accumulated
in reverse order, we take the time at the end of \verb|pass1| to
reverse them all so they'll be simpler to print out prettily.
The code for \verb|reverse_lists| appears in Section~\ref{names}.
\begin{flushleft} \small
\begin{minipage}{\linewidth} \label{scrap43}
$\langle\,${\it Reverse cross-reference lists}\nobreak\ {\footnotesize \NWtarget{nuweb?}{?}}$\,\rangle\equiv$
\vspace{-1ex}
\begin{list}{}{} \item
\mbox{}\verb@{@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  reverse_lists(file_names);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  reverse_lists(macro_names);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  reverse_lists(user_names);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@}@{\NWsep}
\end{list}
\vspace{-1ex}
\footnotesize\addtolength{\baselineskip}{-1ex}
\begin{list}{}{\setlength{\itemsep}{-\parsep}\setlength{\itemindent}{-\leftmargin}}
\item \NWtxtMacroRefIn\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}.
\end{list}
\vspace{-2ex}
\footnotesize\addtolength{\baselineskip}{-1ex}
\begin{list}{}{\setlength{\itemsep}{-\parsep}\setlength{\itemindent}{-\leftmargin}}
\item \NWtxtIdentsUsed\nobreak\  \verb@file_names@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}, \verb@macro_names@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}, \verb@reverse_lists@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}, \verb@user_names@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}.\end{list}
\end{minipage}\\[4ex]
\end{flushleft}
\subsection{Dealing with macro parameters}

Macro parameters were added on later in nuweb's development.
There still is not, for example, an index of macro parameters.
We need a data type to keep track of macro parameters.

Parameter lists will be chained; each one pointing to the one corresponding
to the inocation anteceding the current one.

\begin{flushleft} \small
\begin{minipage}{\linewidth} \label{scrap44}
\verb@"scraps.c"@\nobreak\ {\footnotesize \NWtarget{nuweb?}{?} }$\equiv$
\vspace{-1ex}
\begin{list}{}{} \item
\mbox{}\verb@typedef struct Param { int p[10]; struct Param* parent;} *Parameters;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@@{\NWsep}
\end{list}
\vspace{-1ex}
\footnotesize\addtolength{\baselineskip}{-1ex}
\begin{list}{}{\setlength{\itemsep}{-\parsep}\setlength{\itemindent}{-\leftmargin}}
\item \NWtxtFileDefBy\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}.
\end{list}
\vspace{-2ex}
\footnotesize\addtolength{\baselineskip}{-1ex}
\begin{list}{}{\setlength{\itemsep}{-\parsep}\setlength{\itemindent}{-\leftmargin}}
\item \NWtxtIdentsDefed\nobreak\  \verb@Parameters@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}.\end{list}
\end{minipage}\\[4ex]
\end{flushleft}
When we are copying a scrap to the output, we can then pull
the $n$th string from the \verb|Parameters| list when we
see an \verb|@1| \verb|@2|, etc.

\begin{flushleft} \small
\begin{minipage}{\linewidth} \label{scrap45}
$\langle\,${\it Handle macro parameter substitution}\nobreak\ {\footnotesize \NWtarget{nuweb?}{?}}$\,\rangle\equiv$
\vspace{-1ex}
\begin{list}{}{} \item
\mbox{}\verb@@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    case '1': case '2': case '3':@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    case '4': case '5': case '6':@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    case '7': case '8': case '9':@\\
\mbox{}\verb@              if ( parameters && parameters->p[c - '1'] ) {@\\
\mbox{}\verb@                Scrap_Node param_defs;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@                param_defs.scrap = parameters->p[c - '1'];@\\
\mbox{}\verb@                param_defs.next = 0;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@                write_scraps(file, spelling, &param_defs, global_indent + indent,@\\
\mbox{}\verb@                          indent_chars, debug_flag, tab_flag, indent_flag, @\\
\mbox{}\verb@                                parameters? parameters->parent : 0);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@              } else {@\\
\mbox{}\verb@                /* ZZZ need error message here */@\\
\mbox{}\verb@              }@\\
\mbox{}\verb@              break;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@@{\NWsep}
\end{list}
\vspace{-1ex}
\footnotesize\addtolength{\baselineskip}{-1ex}
\begin{list}{}{\setlength{\itemsep}{-\parsep}\setlength{\itemindent}{-\leftmargin}}
\item \NWtxtMacroRefIn\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}.
\end{list}
\vspace{-2ex}
\footnotesize\addtolength{\baselineskip}{-1ex}
\begin{list}{}{\setlength{\itemsep}{-\parsep}\setlength{\itemindent}{-\leftmargin}}
\item \NWtxtIdentsUsed\nobreak\  \verb@Scrap_Node@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}, \verb@write_scraps@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}.\end{list}
\end{minipage}\\[4ex]
\end{flushleft}
Now onto actually parsing macro parameters from a call.
We start off checking for macro parameters, an \verb|@(| sequence 
followed by parameters separated by \verb|@,| sequences, and
terminated by a \verb|@)| sequence.

We collect separate scraps for each parameter, and write the
scrap numbers down in the text. For example, if the file has:
\begin{verbatim}
   @<foo @( param1 @, param2 @)@>
\end{verbatim}
we actually make new scraps, say 10 and 11, for param1 and param2, 
and write in the collected scrap:
\begin{verbatim}
   @<foo @(10@,11@)@>
\end{verbatim}

\begin{flushleft} \small
\begin{minipage}{\linewidth} \label{scrap46}
$\langle\,${\it Save macro parameters}\nobreak\ {\footnotesize \NWtarget{nuweb?}{?}}$\,\rangle\equiv$
\vspace{-1ex}
\begin{list}{}{} \item
\mbox{}\verb@{@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  int param_scrap;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  char param_buf[10];@\\
\mbox{}\verb@@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  push(nw_char, &writer);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  push('(', &writer);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  do {@\\
\mbox{}\verb@@\\
\mbox{}\verb@     param_scrap = collect_scrap();@\\
\mbox{}\verb@     sprintf(param_buf, "%d", param_scrap);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@     pushs(param_buf, &writer);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@     push(nw_char, &writer);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@     push(scrap_ended_with, &writer);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@     @\hbox{$\langle\,${\it Add current scrap to \verb|name|'s uses}\nobreak\ {\footnotesize \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}}$\,\rangle$}\verb@@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  } while( scrap_ended_with == ',' );@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  do@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    c = source_get();@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  while( ' ' == c );@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  if (c == nw_char) {@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    c = source_get();@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  }@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  if (c != '>') {@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    /* ZZZ print error */;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  }@\\
\mbox{}\verb@}@{\NWsep}
\end{list}
\vspace{-1ex}
\footnotesize\addtolength{\baselineskip}{-1ex}
\begin{list}{}{\setlength{\itemsep}{-\parsep}\setlength{\itemindent}{-\leftmargin}}
\item \NWtxtMacroRefIn\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}.
\end{list}
\vspace{-2ex}
\footnotesize\addtolength{\baselineskip}{-1ex}
\begin{list}{}{\setlength{\itemsep}{-\parsep}\setlength{\itemindent}{-\leftmargin}}
\item \NWtxtIdentsUsed\nobreak\  \verb@collect_scrap@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}, \verb@nw_char@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}, \verb@push@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}, \verb@pushs@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}, \verb@source_get@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}.\end{list}
\end{minipage}\\[4ex]
\end{flushleft}
If we get inside, we have at least one parameter, which will be at
the beginning of the parms buffer, and we prime the pump with the
first character.

\begin{flushleft} \small
\begin{minipage}{\linewidth} \label{scrap47}
$\langle\,${\it Check for macro parameters}\nobreak\ {\footnotesize \NWtarget{nuweb?}{?}}$\,\rangle\equiv$
\vspace{-1ex}
\begin{list}{}{} \item
\mbox{}\verb@@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  if (c == '(') {@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    Parameters res = arena_getmem(sizeof(struct Param));@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    int *p2 = res->p;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    int count = 0;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    int scrapnum;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    res->parent = 0;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    while( c && c != ')' ) {@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      scrapnum = 0;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      c = pop(manager);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      while( '0' <= c && c <= '9' ) {@\\
\mbox{}\verb@        scrapnum = scrapnum  * 10 + c - '0';@\\
\mbox{}\verb@        c = pop(manager);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      }@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      if ( c == nw_char ) {@\\
\mbox{}\verb@        c = pop(manager);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      }@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      *p2++ = scrapnum;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      count++;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    }@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    while (count < 10) {@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      *p2++ = 0;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      count++;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    }@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    while( c && c != nw_char ) {@\\
\mbox{}\verb@        c = pop(manager);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    }@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    if ( c == nw_char ) {@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      c = pop(manager);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    }@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    *parameters = res;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  }@\\
\mbox{}\verb@else@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  {@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    Parameters res = arena_getmem(sizeof(*res));@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    int *p2 = res->p;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    int count = 0;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    res->parent = 0;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    @\\
\mbox{}\verb@    while (count < 10) {@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      *p2++ = 0;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      count++;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    }@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    *parameters = res;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  }@\\
\mbox{}\verb@@{\NWsep}
\end{list}
\vspace{-1ex}
\footnotesize\addtolength{\baselineskip}{-1ex}
\begin{list}{}{\setlength{\itemsep}{-\parsep}\setlength{\itemindent}{-\leftmargin}}
\item \NWtxtMacroRefIn\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}.
\end{list}
\vspace{-2ex}
\footnotesize\addtolength{\baselineskip}{-1ex}
\begin{list}{}{\setlength{\itemsep}{-\parsep}\setlength{\itemindent}{-\leftmargin}}
\item \NWtxtIdentsUsed\nobreak\  \verb@arena_getmem@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}, \verb@nw_char@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}, \verb@Parameters@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}, \verb@pop@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}.\end{list}
\end{minipage}\\[4ex]
\end{flushleft}
These are used in \verb|write_tex| and \verb|write_html| to output the
argument list for a macro.

\begin{flushleft} \small
\begin{minipage}{\linewidth} \label{scrap48}
$\langle\,${\it Format macro parameters}\nobreak\ {\footnotesize \NWtarget{nuweb?}{?}}$\,\rangle\equiv$
\vspace{-1ex}
\begin{list}{}{} \item
\mbox{}\verb@@\\
\mbox{}\verb@   char sep;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@@\\
\mbox{}\verb@   sep = '(';@\\
\mbox{}\verb@   do {@\\
\mbox{}\verb@     fputc(sep,file);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@@\\
\mbox{}\verb@     fputs("{\\footnotesize ", file);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@     if (arglabels_flag)     @\\
\mbox{}\verb@       write_single_scrap_ref(file, scraps + 1);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@     fprintf(file, "\\label{scrap%d}\n", scraps + 1);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@     fputs(" }", file);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@@\\
\mbox{}\verb@     source_last = '{';@\\
\mbox{}\verb@     copy_scrap(file, TRUE);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@@\\
\mbox{}\verb@     ++scraps;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@@\\
\mbox{}\verb@     sep = ',';@\\
\mbox{}\verb@   } while ( source_last != ')' && source_last != EOF );@\\
\mbox{}\verb@   fputs(" ) ",file);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@   do @\\
\mbox{}\verb@     c = source_get();@\\
\mbox{}\verb@   while(c != nw_char && c != EOF);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@   if (c == nw_char) {@\\
\mbox{}\verb@     c = source_get();@\\
\mbox{}\verb@   }@\\
\mbox{}\verb@@{\NWsep}
\end{list}
\vspace{-1ex}
\footnotesize\addtolength{\baselineskip}{-1ex}
\begin{list}{}{\setlength{\itemsep}{-\parsep}\setlength{\itemindent}{-\leftmargin}}
\item \NWtxtMacroRefIn\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}.
\end{list}
\vspace{-2ex}
\footnotesize\addtolength{\baselineskip}{-1ex}
\begin{list}{}{\setlength{\itemsep}{-\parsep}\setlength{\itemindent}{-\leftmargin}}
\item \NWtxtIdentsUsed\nobreak\  \verb@arglabels_flag@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}, \verb@copy_scrap@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}, \verb@fprintf@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}, \verb@fputs@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}, \verb@nw_char@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}, \verb@scraps@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}, \verb@source_get@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}, \verb@source_last@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}, \verb@TRUE@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}, \verb@write_single_scrap_ref@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}.\end{list}
\end{minipage}\\[4ex]
\end{flushleft}
\begin{flushleft} \small
\begin{minipage}{\linewidth} \label{scrap49}
$\langle\,${\it Format HTML macro parameters}\nobreak\ {\footnotesize \NWtarget{nuweb?}{?}}$\,\rangle\equiv$
\vspace{-1ex}
\begin{list}{}{} \item
\mbox{}\verb@@\\
\mbox{}\verb@   char sep;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@@\\
\mbox{}\verb@   sep = '(';@\\
\mbox{}\verb@   fputs("\\begin{rawhtml}", file);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@   do {@\\
\mbox{}\verb@@\\
\mbox{}\verb@     fputc(sep,file);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@     @\\
\mbox{}\verb@     fprintf(file, "%d <A NAME=\"#nuweb%d\"></A>", scraps, scraps);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@@\\
\mbox{}\verb@     source_last = '{';@\\
\mbox{}\verb@     copy_scrap(file, TRUE);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@@\\
\mbox{}\verb@     ++scraps;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@     sep = ',';@\\
\mbox{}\verb@@\\
\mbox{}\verb@   } while ( source_last != ')' && source_last != EOF );@\\
\mbox{}\verb@   fputs(" ) ",file);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@   do @\\
\mbox{}\verb@     c = source_get();@\\
\mbox{}\verb@   while(c != nw_char && c != EOF);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@   if (c == nw_char) {@\\
\mbox{}\verb@     c = source_get();@\\
\mbox{}\verb@   }@\\
\mbox{}\verb@   fputs("\\end{rawhtml}", file);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@@{\NWsep}
\end{list}
\vspace{-1ex}
\footnotesize\addtolength{\baselineskip}{-1ex}
\begin{list}{}{\setlength{\itemsep}{-\parsep}\setlength{\itemindent}{-\leftmargin}}
\item \NWtxtMacroRefIn\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}.
\end{list}
\vspace{-2ex}
\footnotesize\addtolength{\baselineskip}{-1ex}
\begin{list}{}{\setlength{\itemsep}{-\parsep}\setlength{\itemindent}{-\leftmargin}}
\item \NWtxtIdentsUsed\nobreak\  \verb@copy_scrap@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}, \verb@fprintf@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}, \verb@fputs@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}, \verb@nw_char@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}, \verb@scraps@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}, \verb@source_get@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}, \verb@source_last@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}, \verb@TRUE@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}.\end{list}
\end{minipage}\\[4ex]
\end{flushleft}
\section{Writing the Latex File} \label{latex-file}

The second pass (invoked via a call to \verb|write_tex|) copies most of
the text from the source file straight into a \verb|.tex| file.
Definitions are formatted slightly and cross-reference information is
printed out.

Note that all the formatting is handled in this section.
If you don't like the format of definitions or indices or whatever,
it'll be in this section somewhere. Similarly, if someone wanted to
modify nuweb to work with a different typesetting system, this would
be the place to look.

\begin{flushleft} \small
\begin{minipage}{\linewidth} \label{scrap50}
$\langle\,${\it Function prototypes}\nobreak\ {\footnotesize \NWtarget{nuweb?}{?}}$\,\rangle\equiv$
\vspace{-1ex}
\begin{list}{}{} \item
\mbox{}\verb@extern void write_tex();@\\
\mbox{}\verb@@{\NWsep}
\end{list}
\vspace{-1ex}
\footnotesize\addtolength{\baselineskip}{-1ex}
\begin{list}{}{\setlength{\itemsep}{-\parsep}\setlength{\itemindent}{-\leftmargin}}
\item \NWtxtMacroDefBy\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}.
\item \NWtxtMacroRefIn\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}.
\end{list}
\vspace{-2ex}
\footnotesize\addtolength{\baselineskip}{-1ex}
\begin{list}{}{\setlength{\itemsep}{-\parsep}\setlength{\itemindent}{-\leftmargin}}
\item \NWtxtIdentsUsed\nobreak\  \verb@write_tex@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}.\end{list}
\end{minipage}\\[4ex]
\end{flushleft}
We need a few local function declarations before we get into the body
of \verb|write_tex|.

\begin{flushleft} \small
\begin{minipage}{\linewidth} \label{scrap51}
\verb@"latex.c"@\nobreak\ {\footnotesize \NWtarget{nuweb?}{?} }$\equiv$
\vspace{-1ex}
\begin{list}{}{} \item
\mbox{}\verb@static void copy_scrap();             /* formats the body of a scrap */@\\
\mbox{}\verb@static void print_scrap_numbers();      /* formats a list of scrap numbers */@\\
\mbox{}\verb@static void format_entry();             /* formats an index entry */@\\
\mbox{}\verb@static void format_user_entry();@\\
\mbox{}\verb@@{\NWsep}
\end{list}
\vspace{-1ex}
\footnotesize\addtolength{\baselineskip}{-1ex}
\begin{list}{}{\setlength{\itemsep}{-\parsep}\setlength{\itemindent}{-\leftmargin}}
\item \NWtxtFileDefBy\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}.
\end{list}
\vspace{-2ex}
\footnotesize\addtolength{\baselineskip}{-1ex}
\begin{list}{}{\setlength{\itemsep}{-\parsep}\setlength{\itemindent}{-\leftmargin}}
\item \NWtxtIdentsUsed\nobreak\  \verb@copy_scrap@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}, \verb@format_entry@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}, \verb@format_user_entry@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}, \verb@print_scrap_numbers@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}.\end{list}
\end{minipage}\\[4ex]
\end{flushleft}
The routine \verb|write_tex| takes two file names as parameters: the
name of the web source file and the name of the \verb|.tex| output file.
\begin{flushleft} \small
\begin{minipage}{\linewidth} \label{scrap52}
\verb@"latex.c"@\nobreak\ {\footnotesize \NWtarget{nuweb?}{?} }$\equiv$
\vspace{-1ex}
\begin{list}{}{} \item
\mbox{}\verb@void write_tex(file_name, tex_name)@\\
\mbox{}\verb@     char *file_name;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@     char *tex_name;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@{@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  FILE *tex_file = fopen(tex_name, "w");@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  if (tex_file) {@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    if (verbose_flag)@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      fprintf(stderr, "writing %s\n", tex_name);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    source_open(file_name);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    @\hbox{$\langle\,${\it Write LaTeX limbo definitions}\nobreak\ {\footnotesize \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}}$\,\rangle$}\verb@@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    @\hbox{$\langle\,${\it Copy \verb|source_file| into \verb|tex_file|}\nobreak\ {\footnotesize \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}}$\,\rangle$}\verb@@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    fclose(tex_file);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  }@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  else@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    fprintf(stderr, "%s: can't open %s\n", command_name, tex_name);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@}@\\
\mbox{}\verb@@{\NWsep}
\end{list}
\vspace{-1ex}
\footnotesize\addtolength{\baselineskip}{-1ex}
\begin{list}{}{\setlength{\itemsep}{-\parsep}\setlength{\itemindent}{-\leftmargin}}
\item \NWtxtFileDefBy\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}.
\end{list}
\vspace{-2ex}
\footnotesize\addtolength{\baselineskip}{-1ex}
\begin{list}{}{\setlength{\itemsep}{-\parsep}\setlength{\itemindent}{-\leftmargin}}
\item \NWtxtIdentsDefed\nobreak\  \verb@write_tex@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}.\end{list}
\vspace{-2ex}
\footnotesize\addtolength{\baselineskip}{-1ex}
\begin{list}{}{\setlength{\itemsep}{-\parsep}\setlength{\itemindent}{-\leftmargin}}
\item \NWtxtIdentsUsed\nobreak\  \verb@command_name@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}, \verb@fclose@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}, \verb@FILE@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}, \verb@fopen@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}, \verb@fprintf@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}, \verb@source_open@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}, \verb@stderr@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}, \verb@verbose_flag@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}.\end{list}
\end{minipage}\\[4ex]
\end{flushleft}
Now that the \verb|\NW...| macros are used, it seems convenient
to write default definitions for those macros so that source files
need not define anything new. If a user wants to change any of 
the macros (to use hyperref or to write in some language other than
english) he or she can redefine the commands.
\begin{flushleft} \small
\begin{minipage}{\linewidth} \label{scrap53}
$\langle\,${\it Write LaTeX limbo definitions}\nobreak\ {\footnotesize \NWtarget{nuweb?}{?}}$\,\rangle\equiv$
\vspace{-1ex}
\begin{list}{}{} \item
\mbox{}\verb@if (hyperref_flag == TRUE) {@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  fputs("\\newcommand{\\NWtarget}[2]{\\hypertarget{#1}{#2}}\n", tex_file);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  fputs("\\newcommand{\\NWlink}[2]{\\hyperlink{#1}{#2}}\n", tex_file);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@} else {@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  fputs("\\newcommand{\\NWtarget}[2]{#2}\n", tex_file);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  fputs("\\newcommand{\\NWlink}[2]{#2}\n", tex_file);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@}@\\
\mbox{}\verb@@\\
\mbox{}\verb@fputs("\\newcommand{\\NWtxtMacroDefBy}{Macro defined by}\n", tex_file);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@fputs("\\newcommand{\\NWtxtMacroRefIn}{Macro referenced in}\n", tex_file);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@fputs("\\newcommand{\\NWtxtMacroNoRef}{Macro never referenced}\n", tex_file);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@fputs("\\newcommand{\\NWtxtDefBy}{Defined by}\n", tex_file);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@fputs("\\newcommand{\\NWtxtRefIn}{Referenced in}\n", tex_file);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@fputs("\\newcommand{\\NWtxtNoRef}{Not referenced}\n", tex_file);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@fputs("\\newcommand{\\NWtxtFileDefBy}{File defined by}\n", tex_file);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@fputs("\\newcommand{\\NWtxtIdentsUsed}{Uses:}\n", tex_file);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@fputs("\\newcommand{\\NWtxtIdentsNotUsed}{Never used}\n", tex_file);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@fputs("\\newcommand{\\NWtxtIdentsDefed}{Defines:}\n", tex_file);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@fputs("\\newcommand{\\NWsep}{${\\diamond}$}\n", tex_file);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@@{\NWsep}
\end{list}
\vspace{-1ex}
\footnotesize\addtolength{\baselineskip}{-1ex}
\begin{list}{}{\setlength{\itemsep}{-\parsep}\setlength{\itemindent}{-\leftmargin}}
\item \NWtxtMacroRefIn\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}.
\end{list}
\vspace{-2ex}
\footnotesize\addtolength{\baselineskip}{-1ex}
\begin{list}{}{\setlength{\itemsep}{-\parsep}\setlength{\itemindent}{-\leftmargin}}
\item \NWtxtIdentsUsed\nobreak\  \verb@fputs@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}, \verb@hyperref_flag@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}, \verb@TRUE@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}, \verb@Uses@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}.\end{list}
\end{minipage}\\[4ex]
\end{flushleft}
We make our second (and final) pass through the source web, this time
copying characters straight into the \verb|.tex| file. However, we keep
an eye peeled for \verb|@|~characters, which signal a command sequence.

\begin{flushleft} \small
\begin{minipage}{\linewidth} \label{scrap54}
$\langle\,${\it Copy \verb|source_file| into \verb|tex_file|}\nobreak\ {\footnotesize \NWtarget{nuweb?}{?}}$\,\rangle\equiv$
\vspace{-1ex}
\begin{list}{}{} \item
\mbox{}\verb@{@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  int c = source_get();@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  while (c != EOF) {@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    if (c == nw_char)@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      {@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      @\hbox{$\langle\,${\it Interpret at-sequence}\nobreak\ {\footnotesize \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}}$\,\rangle$}\verb@@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      }@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    else {@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      putc(c, tex_file);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      c = source_get();@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    }@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  }@\\
\mbox{}\verb@}@{\NWsep}
\end{list}
\vspace{-1ex}
\footnotesize\addtolength{\baselineskip}{-1ex}
\begin{list}{}{\setlength{\itemsep}{-\parsep}\setlength{\itemindent}{-\leftmargin}}
\item \NWtxtMacroRefIn\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}.
\end{list}
\vspace{-2ex}
\footnotesize\addtolength{\baselineskip}{-1ex}
\begin{list}{}{\setlength{\itemsep}{-\parsep}\setlength{\itemindent}{-\leftmargin}}
\item \NWtxtIdentsUsed\nobreak\  \verb@nw_char@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}, \verb@putc@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}, \verb@source_get@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}.\end{list}
\end{minipage}\\[4ex]
\end{flushleft}
\begin{flushleft} \small
\begin{minipage}{\linewidth} \label{scrap55}
$\langle\,${\it Interpret at-sequence}\nobreak\ {\footnotesize \NWtarget{nuweb?}{?}}$\,\rangle\equiv$
\vspace{-1ex}
\begin{list}{}{} \item
\mbox{}\verb@{@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  int big_definition = FALSE;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  c = source_get();@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  switch (c) {@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    case 'r':@\\
\mbox{}\verb@          c = source_get();@\\
\mbox{}\verb@          nw_char = c;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@          update_delimit_scrap();@\\
\mbox{}\verb@          break;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    case 'O': big_definition = TRUE;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    case 'o': @\hbox{$\langle\,${\it Write output file definition}\nobreak\ {\footnotesize \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}}$\,\rangle$}\verb@@\\
\mbox{}\verb@              break;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    case 'D': big_definition = TRUE;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    case 'd': @\hbox{$\langle\,${\it Write macro definition}\nobreak\ {\footnotesize \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}}$\,\rangle$}\verb@@\\
\mbox{}\verb@              break;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    case 's':@\\
\mbox{}\verb@              @\hbox{$\langle\,${\it Step to next sector}\nobreak\ {\footnotesize \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}}$\,\rangle$}\verb@@\\
\mbox{}\verb@              break;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    case '{':@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    case '[':@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    case '(': @\hbox{$\langle\,${\it Write in-text scrap}\nobreak\ {\footnotesize \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}}$\,\rangle$}\verb@@\\
\mbox{}\verb@              break;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    case 'x': @\hbox{$\langle\,${\it Copy label from source into}\nobreak\ ({\footnotesize \label{scrap56}
 }\mbox{}\verb@tex_file@ ) {\footnotesize \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}}$\,\rangle$}\verb@@\\
\mbox{}\verb@              break;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    case 'f': @\hbox{$\langle\,${\it Write index of file names}\nobreak\ {\footnotesize \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}}$\,\rangle$}\verb@@\\
\mbox{}\verb@              break;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    case 'm': @\hbox{$\langle\,${\it Write index of macro names}\nobreak\ {\footnotesize \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}}$\,\rangle$}\verb@@\\
\mbox{}\verb@              break;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    case 'u': @\hbox{$\langle\,${\it Write index of user-specified names}\nobreak\ {\footnotesize \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}}$\,\rangle$}\verb@@\\
\mbox{}\verb@              break;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    default:  @\\
\mbox{}\verb@          if (c==nw_char)@\\
\mbox{}\verb@            putc(c, tex_file); @\\
\mbox{}\verb@          c = source_get();@\\
\mbox{}\verb@              break;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  }@\\
\mbox{}\verb@}@{\NWsep}
\end{list}
\vspace{-1ex}
\footnotesize\addtolength{\baselineskip}{-1ex}
\begin{list}{}{\setlength{\itemsep}{-\parsep}\setlength{\itemindent}{-\leftmargin}}
\item \NWtxtMacroRefIn\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}.
\end{list}
\end{minipage}\\[4ex]
\end{flushleft}
\subsection{Formatting Definitions}

We go through a fair amount of effort to format a file definition.
I've derived most of the \LaTeX\ commands experimentally; it's quite
likely that an expert could do a better job. The \LaTeX\ for
the previous macro definition should look like this (perhaps modulo
the scrap references):
{\small
\begin{verbatim}
\begin{flushleft} \small
\begin{minipage}{\linewidth} \label{scrap37}
$\langle$Interpret at-sequence {\footnotesize 18}$\rangle\equiv$
\vspace{-1ex}
\begin{list}{}{} \item
\mbox{}\verb@{@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  int big_definition = FALSE;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  c = source_get();@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  switch (c) {@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    case 'O': big_definition = TRUE;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    case 'o': @$\langle$Write output file definition {\footnotesize 19a}$\rangle$\verb@@\\
\end{verbatim}
\vdots
\begin{verbatim}
\mbox{}\verb@    case '@{\tt @}\verb@': putc(c, tex_file);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    default:  c = source_get();@\\
\mbox{}\verb@              break;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  }@\\
\mbox{}\verb@}@$\diamond$
\end{list}
\vspace{-1ex}
\footnotesize\addtolength{\baselineskip}{-1ex}
\begin{list}{}{\setlength{\itemsep}{-\parsep}\setlength{\itemindent}{-\leftmargin}}
\item Macro referenced in scrap 17b.
\end{list}
\end{minipage}\\[4ex]
\end{flushleft}
\end{verbatim}}

\noindent
The {\em flushleft\/} environment is used to avoid \LaTeX\ warnings
about underful lines. The {\em minipage\/} environment is used to
avoid page breaks in the middle of scraps. The {\em verb\/} command
allows arbitrary characters to be printed (however, note the special
handling of the \verb|@| case in the switch statement).

Macro and file definitions are formatted nearly identically.
I've factored the common parts out into separate scraps.

\begin{flushleft} \small
\begin{minipage}{\linewidth} \label{scrap57}
$\langle\,${\it Write output file definition}\nobreak\ {\footnotesize \NWtarget{nuweb?}{?}}$\,\rangle\equiv$
\vspace{-1ex}
\begin{list}{}{} \item
\mbox{}\verb@{@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  Name *name = collect_file_name();@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  @\hbox{$\langle\,${\it Begin the scrap environment}\nobreak\ {\footnotesize \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}}$\,\rangle$}\verb@@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  fprintf(tex_file, "\\verb%c\"%s\"%c\\nobreak\\ {\\footnotesize ", nw_char, name->spelling, nw_char);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  fputs("\\NWtarget{nuweb", tex_file);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  write_single_scrap_ref(tex_file, scraps);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  fputs("}{", tex_file);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  write_single_scrap_ref(tex_file, scraps);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  fputs("}", tex_file);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  fputs(" }$\\equiv$\n", tex_file);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  @\hbox{$\langle\,${\it Fill in the middle of the scrap environment}\nobreak\ {\footnotesize \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}}$\,\rangle$}\verb@@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  if ( scrap_flag ) {@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    @\hbox{$\langle\,${\it Write file defs}\nobreak\ {\footnotesize \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}}$\,\rangle$}\verb@@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  }@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  @\hbox{$\langle\,${\it Finish the scrap environment}\nobreak\ {\footnotesize \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}}$\,\rangle$}\verb@@\\
\mbox{}\verb@}@{\NWsep}
\end{list}
\vspace{-1ex}
\footnotesize\addtolength{\baselineskip}{-1ex}
\begin{list}{}{\setlength{\itemsep}{-\parsep}\setlength{\itemindent}{-\leftmargin}}
\item \NWtxtMacroRefIn\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}.
\end{list}
\vspace{-2ex}
\footnotesize\addtolength{\baselineskip}{-1ex}
\begin{list}{}{\setlength{\itemsep}{-\parsep}\setlength{\itemindent}{-\leftmargin}}
\item \NWtxtIdentsUsed\nobreak\  \verb@collect_file_name@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}, \verb@fprintf@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}, \verb@fputs@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}, \verb@Name@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}, \verb@nw_char@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}, \verb@scraps@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}, \verb@scrap_flag@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}, \verb@write_single_scrap_ref@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}.\end{list}
\end{minipage}\\[4ex]
\end{flushleft}
I don't format a macro name at all specially, figuring the programmer
might want to use italics or bold face in the midst of the name.

\begin{flushleft} \small
\begin{minipage}{\linewidth} \label{scrap58}
$\langle\,${\it Write macro definition}\nobreak\ {\footnotesize \NWtarget{nuweb?}{?}}$\,\rangle\equiv$
\vspace{-1ex}
\begin{list}{}{} \item
\mbox{}\verb@{@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  Name *name = collect_macro_name();@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  @\hbox{$\langle\,${\it Begin the scrap environment}\nobreak\ {\footnotesize \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}}$\,\rangle$}\verb@@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  fprintf(tex_file, "$\\langle\\,${\\it %s}\\nobreak\\ {\\footnotesize ", name->spelling);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  fputs("\\NWtarget{nuweb", tex_file);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  write_single_scrap_ref(tex_file, scraps);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  fputs("}{", tex_file);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  write_single_scrap_ref(tex_file, scraps);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  fputs("}", tex_file);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  fputs("}$\\,\\rangle\\equiv$\n", tex_file);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  @\hbox{$\langle\,${\it Fill in the middle of the scrap environment}\nobreak\ {\footnotesize \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}}$\,\rangle$}\verb@@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  @\hbox{$\langle\,${\it Write macro defs}\nobreak\ {\footnotesize \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}}$\,\rangle$}\verb@@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  @\hbox{$\langle\,${\it Write macro refs}\nobreak\ {\footnotesize \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}}$\,\rangle$}\verb@@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  @\hbox{$\langle\,${\it Finish the scrap environment}\nobreak\ {\footnotesize \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}}$\,\rangle$}\verb@@\\
\mbox{}\verb@}@{\NWsep}
\end{list}
\vspace{-1ex}
\footnotesize\addtolength{\baselineskip}{-1ex}
\begin{list}{}{\setlength{\itemsep}{-\parsep}\setlength{\itemindent}{-\leftmargin}}
\item \NWtxtMacroRefIn\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}.
\end{list}
\vspace{-2ex}
\footnotesize\addtolength{\baselineskip}{-1ex}
\begin{list}{}{\setlength{\itemsep}{-\parsep}\setlength{\itemindent}{-\leftmargin}}
\item \NWtxtIdentsUsed\nobreak\  \verb@collect_macro_name@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}, \verb@fprintf@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}, \verb@fputs@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}, \verb@Name@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}, \verb@scraps@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}, \verb@write_single_scrap_ref@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}.\end{list}
\end{minipage}\\[4ex]
\end{flushleft}
\begin{flushleft} \small
\begin{minipage}{\linewidth} \label{scrap59}
$\langle\,${\it Begin the scrap environment}\nobreak\ {\footnotesize \NWtarget{nuweb?}{?}}$\,\rangle\equiv$
\vspace{-1ex}
\begin{list}{}{} \item
\mbox{}\verb@{@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  fputs("\\begin{flushleft} \\small", tex_file);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  if (!big_definition)@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    fputs("\n\\begin{minipage}{\\linewidth}", tex_file);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  fprintf(tex_file, " \\label{scrap%d}\n", scraps);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@}@{\NWsep}
\end{list}
\vspace{-1ex}
\footnotesize\addtolength{\baselineskip}{-1ex}
\begin{list}{}{\setlength{\itemsep}{-\parsep}\setlength{\itemindent}{-\leftmargin}}
\item \NWtxtMacroRefIn\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}.
\end{list}
\vspace{-2ex}
\footnotesize\addtolength{\baselineskip}{-1ex}
\begin{list}{}{\setlength{\itemsep}{-\parsep}\setlength{\itemindent}{-\leftmargin}}
\item \NWtxtIdentsUsed\nobreak\  \verb@fprintf@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}, \verb@fputs@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}, \verb@scraps@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}.\end{list}
\end{minipage}\\[4ex]
\end{flushleft}
The interesting things here are the $\diamond$ inserted at the end of
each scrap and the various spacing commands. The diamond helps to
clearly indicate the end of a scrap. The spacing commands were derived
empirically; they may be adjusted to taste.

\begin{flushleft} \small
\begin{minipage}{\linewidth} \label{scrap60}
$\langle\,${\it Fill in the middle of the scrap environment}\nobreak\ {\footnotesize \NWtarget{nuweb?}{?}}$\,\rangle\equiv$
\vspace{-1ex}
\begin{list}{}{} \item
\mbox{}\verb@{@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  fputs("\\vspace{-1ex}\n\\begin{list}{}{} \\item\n", tex_file);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  copy_scrap(tex_file, TRUE);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  fputs("{\\NWsep}\n\\end{list}\n", tex_file);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@}@{\NWsep}
\end{list}
\vspace{-1ex}
\footnotesize\addtolength{\baselineskip}{-1ex}
\begin{list}{}{\setlength{\itemsep}{-\parsep}\setlength{\itemindent}{-\leftmargin}}
\item \NWtxtMacroRefIn\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}.
\end{list}
\vspace{-2ex}
\footnotesize\addtolength{\baselineskip}{-1ex}
\begin{list}{}{\setlength{\itemsep}{-\parsep}\setlength{\itemindent}{-\leftmargin}}
\item \NWtxtIdentsUsed\nobreak\  \verb@copy_scrap@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}, \verb@fputs@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}, \verb@TRUE@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}.\end{list}
\end{minipage}\\[4ex]
\end{flushleft}
\newpage
\noindent
We've got one last spacing command, controlling the amount of white
space after a scrap.

Note also the whitespace eater. I use it to remove any blank lines
that appear after a scrap in the source file. This way, text following
a scrap will not be indented. Again, this is a matter of personal taste.

\begin{flushleft} \small
\begin{minipage}{\linewidth} \label{scrap61}
$\langle\,${\it Finish the scrap environment}\nobreak\ {\footnotesize \NWtarget{nuweb?}{?}}$\,\rangle\equiv$
\vspace{-1ex}
\begin{list}{}{} \item
\mbox{}\verb@{@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  format_defs_refs(tex_file, scraps);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  format_uses_refs(tex_file, scraps++);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  if (!big_definition)@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    fputs("\\end{minipage}\\\\[4ex]\n", tex_file);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  fputs("\\end{flushleft}\n", tex_file);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  do@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    c = source_get();@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  while (isspace(c));@\\
\mbox{}\verb@}@{\NWsep}
\end{list}
\vspace{-1ex}
\footnotesize\addtolength{\baselineskip}{-1ex}
\begin{list}{}{\setlength{\itemsep}{-\parsep}\setlength{\itemindent}{-\leftmargin}}
\item \NWtxtMacroRefIn\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}.
\end{list}
\vspace{-2ex}
\footnotesize\addtolength{\baselineskip}{-1ex}
\begin{list}{}{\setlength{\itemsep}{-\parsep}\setlength{\itemindent}{-\leftmargin}}
\item \NWtxtIdentsUsed\nobreak\  \verb@format_defs_refs@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}, \verb@format_uses_refs@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}, \verb@fputs@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}, \verb@isspace@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}, \verb@scraps@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}, \verb@source_get@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}.\end{list}
\end{minipage}\\[4ex]
\end{flushleft}
\begin{flushleft} \small
\begin{minipage}{\linewidth} \label{scrap62}
$\langle\,${\it Write in-text scrap}\nobreak\ {\footnotesize \NWtarget{nuweb?}{?}}$\,\rangle\equiv$
\vspace{-1ex}
\begin{list}{}{} \item
\mbox{}\verb@copy_scrap(tex_file, FALSE);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@c = source_get();@\\
\mbox{}\verb@@{\NWsep}
\end{list}
\vspace{-1ex}
\footnotesize\addtolength{\baselineskip}{-1ex}
\begin{list}{}{\setlength{\itemsep}{-\parsep}\setlength{\itemindent}{-\leftmargin}}
\item \NWtxtMacroRefIn\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}.
\end{list}
\vspace{-2ex}
\footnotesize\addtolength{\baselineskip}{-1ex}
\begin{list}{}{\setlength{\itemsep}{-\parsep}\setlength{\itemindent}{-\leftmargin}}
\item \NWtxtIdentsUsed\nobreak\  \verb@copy_scrap@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}, \verb@FALSE@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}, \verb@source_get@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}.\end{list}
\end{minipage}\\[4ex]
\end{flushleft}
\subsubsection{Formatting Cross References}

\begin{flushleft} \small
\begin{minipage}{\linewidth} \label{scrap63}
$\langle\,${\it Write file defs}\nobreak\ {\footnotesize \NWtarget{nuweb?}{?}}$\,\rangle\equiv$
\vspace{-1ex}
\begin{list}{}{} \item
\mbox{}\verb@{@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  if (name->defs->next) {@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    fputs("\\vspace{-1ex}\n", tex_file);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    fputs("\\footnotesize\\addtolength{\\baselineskip}{-1ex}\n", tex_file);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    fputs("\\begin{list}{}{\\setlength{\\itemsep}{-\\parsep}", tex_file);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    fputs("\\setlength{\\itemindent}{-\\leftmargin}}\n", tex_file);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    fputs("\\item \\NWtxtFileDefBy\\ ", tex_file);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    print_scrap_numbers(tex_file, name->defs);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    fputs("\\end{list}\n", tex_file);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  }@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  else@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    fputs("\\vspace{-2ex}\n", tex_file);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@}@{\NWsep}
\end{list}
\vspace{-1ex}
\footnotesize\addtolength{\baselineskip}{-1ex}
\begin{list}{}{\setlength{\itemsep}{-\parsep}\setlength{\itemindent}{-\leftmargin}}
\item \NWtxtMacroRefIn\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}.
\end{list}
\vspace{-2ex}
\footnotesize\addtolength{\baselineskip}{-1ex}
\begin{list}{}{\setlength{\itemsep}{-\parsep}\setlength{\itemindent}{-\leftmargin}}
\item \NWtxtIdentsUsed\nobreak\  \verb@fputs@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}, \verb@print_scrap_numbers@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}.\end{list}
\end{minipage}\\[4ex]
\end{flushleft}
\begin{flushleft} \small
\begin{minipage}{\linewidth} \label{scrap64}
$\langle\,${\it Write macro defs}\nobreak\ {\footnotesize \NWtarget{nuweb?}{?}}$\,\rangle\equiv$
\vspace{-1ex}
\begin{list}{}{} \item
\mbox{}\verb@{@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  fputs("\\vspace{-1ex}\n", tex_file);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  fputs("\\footnotesize\\addtolength{\\baselineskip}{-1ex}\n", tex_file);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  fputs("\\begin{list}{}{\\setlength{\\itemsep}{-\\parsep}", tex_file);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  fputs("\\setlength{\\itemindent}{-\\leftmargin}}\n", tex_file);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  if (name->defs->next) {@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    fputs("\\item \\NWtxtMacroDefBy\\ ", tex_file);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    print_scrap_numbers(tex_file, name->defs);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  }@\\
\mbox{}\verb@}@{\NWsep}
\end{list}
\vspace{-1ex}
\footnotesize\addtolength{\baselineskip}{-1ex}
\begin{list}{}{\setlength{\itemsep}{-\parsep}\setlength{\itemindent}{-\leftmargin}}
