\end{list}
\vspace{-2ex}
\footnotesize\addtolength{\baselineskip}{-1ex}
\begin{list}{}{\setlength{\itemsep}{-\parsep}\setlength{\itemindent}{-\leftmargin}}
\item \NWtxtIdentsUsed\nobreak\  \verb@fputs@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}, \verb@print_scrap_numbers@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}.\end{list}
\end{minipage}\\[4ex]
\end{flushleft}
\begin{flushleft} \small
\begin{minipage}{\linewidth} \label{scrap65}
$\langle\,${\it Write macro refs}\nobreak\ {\footnotesize \NWtarget{nuweb?}{?}}$\,\rangle\equiv$
\vspace{-1ex}
\begin{list}{}{} \item
\mbox{}\verb@{@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  if (name->uses) {@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    if (name->uses->next) {@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      fputs("\\item \\NWtxtMacroRefIn\\ ", tex_file);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      print_scrap_numbers(tex_file, name->uses);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    }@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    else {@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      fputs("\\item \\NWtxtMacroRefIn\\ ", tex_file);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      fputs("\\NWlink{nuweb", tex_file);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      write_single_scrap_ref(tex_file, name->uses->scrap);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      fputs("}{", tex_file);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      write_single_scrap_ref(tex_file, name->uses->scrap);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      fputs("}", tex_file);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      fputs(".\n", tex_file);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    }@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  }@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  else {@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    fputs("\\item {\\NWtxtMacroNoRef}.\n", tex_file);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    fprintf(stderr, "%s: <%s> never referenced.\n",@\\
\mbox{}\verb@            command_name, name->spelling);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  }@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  fputs("\\end{list}\n", tex_file);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@}@{\NWsep}
\end{list}
\vspace{-1ex}
\footnotesize\addtolength{\baselineskip}{-1ex}
\begin{list}{}{\setlength{\itemsep}{-\parsep}\setlength{\itemindent}{-\leftmargin}}
\item \NWtxtMacroRefIn\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}.
\end{list}
\vspace{-2ex}
\footnotesize\addtolength{\baselineskip}{-1ex}
\begin{list}{}{\setlength{\itemsep}{-\parsep}\setlength{\itemindent}{-\leftmargin}}
\item \NWtxtIdentsUsed\nobreak\  \verb@command_name@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}, \verb@fprintf@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}, \verb@fputs@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}, \verb@print_scrap_numbers@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}, \verb@stderr@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}, \verb@write_single_scrap_ref@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}.\end{list}
\end{minipage}\\[4ex]
\end{flushleft}
\begin{flushleft} \small
\begin{minipage}{\linewidth} \label{scrap66}
\verb@"latex.c"@\nobreak\ {\footnotesize \NWtarget{nuweb?}{?} }$\equiv$
\vspace{-1ex}
\begin{list}{}{} \item
\mbox{}\verb@static void print_scrap_numbers(tex_file, scraps)@\\
\mbox{}\verb@     FILE *tex_file;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@     Scrap_Node *scraps;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@{@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  int page;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  fputs("\\NWlink{nuweb", tex_file);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  write_scrap_ref(tex_file, scraps->scrap, -1, &page);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  fputs("}{", tex_file);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  write_scrap_ref(tex_file, scraps->scrap, TRUE, &page);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  fputs("}", tex_file);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  scraps = scraps->next;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  while (scraps) {@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    fputs("\\NWlink{nuweb", tex_file);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    write_scrap_ref(tex_file, scraps->scrap, -1, &page);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    fputs("}{", tex_file);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    write_scrap_ref(tex_file, scraps->scrap, FALSE, &page);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    scraps = scraps->next;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    fputs("}", tex_file);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  }@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  fputs(".\n", tex_file);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@}@\\
\mbox{}\verb@@{\NWsep}
\end{list}
\vspace{-1ex}
\footnotesize\addtolength{\baselineskip}{-1ex}
\begin{list}{}{\setlength{\itemsep}{-\parsep}\setlength{\itemindent}{-\leftmargin}}
\item \NWtxtFileDefBy\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}.
\end{list}
\vspace{-2ex}
\footnotesize\addtolength{\baselineskip}{-1ex}
\begin{list}{}{\setlength{\itemsep}{-\parsep}\setlength{\itemindent}{-\leftmargin}}
\item \NWtxtIdentsDefed\nobreak\  \verb@print_scrap_numbers@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}.\end{list}
\vspace{-2ex}
\footnotesize\addtolength{\baselineskip}{-1ex}
\begin{list}{}{\setlength{\itemsep}{-\parsep}\setlength{\itemindent}{-\leftmargin}}
\item \NWtxtIdentsUsed\nobreak\  \verb@FALSE@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}, \verb@FILE@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}, \verb@fputs@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}, \verb@scraps@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}, \verb@Scrap_Node@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}, \verb@TRUE@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}, \verb@write_scrap_ref@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}.\end{list}
\end{minipage}\\[4ex]
\end{flushleft}
\subsubsection{Formatting a Scrap}

We add a \verb|\mbox{}| at the beginning of each line to avoid
problems with older versions of \TeX.
This is the only place we really care whether a scrap is
delimited with \verb|@{...@}|, \verb|@[...@]|, or \verb|@(...@)|,
and we base our output sequences on that.

We have an array \texttt{delimit\_scrap} where we store our strings
that perform the formatting for one line of a scrap. Upon
initialisation we copy our strings from the source
\texttt{orig\_delimit\_scrap} to it to have the strings writeable. We
might change the strings later when we encounter the command to change
the `nuweb character'.

\begin{flushleft} \small
\begin{minipage}{\linewidth} \label{scrap67}
\verb@"latex.c"@\nobreak\ {\footnotesize \NWtarget{nuweb?}{?} }$\equiv$
\vspace{-1ex}
\begin{list}{}{} \item
\mbox{}\verb@static char *orig_delimit_scrap[3][5] = {@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  /* {} mode: begin, end, insert nw_char, prefix, suffix */@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  { "\\verb@{\tt @}\verb@", "@{\tt @}\verb@", "@{\tt @}\verb@{\\tt @{\tt @}\verb@}\\verb@{\tt @}\verb@", "\\mbox{}", "\\\\" },@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  /* [] mode: begin, end, insert nw_char, prefix, suffix */@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  { "", "", "@{\tt @}\verb@", "", "" },@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  /* () mode: begin, end, insert nw_char, prefix, suffix */@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  { "$", "$", "@{\tt @}\verb@", "", "" },@\\
\mbox{}\verb@};@\\
\mbox{}\verb@@\\
\mbox{}\verb@static char *delimit_scrap[3][5];@\\
\mbox{}\verb@@{\NWsep}
\end{list}
\vspace{-1ex}
\footnotesize\addtolength{\baselineskip}{-1ex}
\begin{list}{}{\setlength{\itemsep}{-\parsep}\setlength{\itemindent}{-\leftmargin}}
\item \NWtxtFileDefBy\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}.
\end{list}
\vspace{-2ex}
\footnotesize\addtolength{\baselineskip}{-1ex}
\begin{list}{}{\setlength{\itemsep}{-\parsep}\setlength{\itemindent}{-\leftmargin}}
\item \NWtxtIdentsUsed\nobreak\  \verb@delimit_scrap@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}, \verb@nw_char@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}.\end{list}
\end{minipage}\\[4ex]
\end{flushleft}
The function \texttt{initialise\_delimit\_scrap\_array} does the
copying. If we want to have the listings package \index{listings package}
do the formatting we have to replace only two of those strings: the
\texttt{verb} command has to be replaced by the package's \texttt{lstinline}
command.

\begin{flushleft} \small
\begin{minipage}{\linewidth} \label{scrap68}
\verb@"latex.c"@\nobreak\ {\footnotesize \NWtarget{nuweb?}{?} }$\equiv$
\vspace{-1ex}
\begin{list}{}{} \item
\mbox{}\verb@void initialise_delimit_scrap_array() {@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  int i,j;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  for(i = 0; i < 3; i++) {@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    for(j = 0; j < 5; j++) {@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      if((delimit_scrap[i][j] = strdup(orig_delimit_scrap[i][j])) == NULL) {@\\
\mbox{}\verb@        fprintf(stderr, "Not enough memory for string allocation\n");@\\
\mbox{}\verb@        exit(EXIT_FAILURE);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      }@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    }@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  }@\\
\mbox{}\verb@@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  /* replace verb by lstinline */@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  if (listings_flag == TRUE) {@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    free(delimit_scrap[0][0]);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    if((delimit_scrap[0][0]=strdup("\\lstinline@{\tt @}\verb@")) == NULL) {@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      fprintf(stderr, "Not enough memory for string allocation\n");@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      exit(EXIT_FAILURE);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    }@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    free(delimit_scrap[0][2]);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    if((delimit_scrap[0][2]=strdup("@{\tt @}\verb@{\\tt @{\tt @}\verb@}\\lstinline@{\tt @}\verb@")) == NULL) {@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      fprintf(stderr, "Not enough memory for string allocation\n");@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      exit(EXIT_FAILURE);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    }@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  }@\\
\mbox{}\verb@}@\\
\mbox{}\verb@@{\NWsep}
\end{list}
\vspace{-1ex}
\footnotesize\addtolength{\baselineskip}{-1ex}
\begin{list}{}{\setlength{\itemsep}{-\parsep}\setlength{\itemindent}{-\leftmargin}}
\item \NWtxtFileDefBy\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}.
\end{list}
\vspace{-2ex}
\footnotesize\addtolength{\baselineskip}{-1ex}
\begin{list}{}{\setlength{\itemsep}{-\parsep}\setlength{\itemindent}{-\leftmargin}}
\item \NWtxtIdentsUsed\nobreak\  \verb@delimit_scrap@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}, \verb@exit@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}, \verb@fprintf@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}, \verb@listings_flag@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}, \verb@stderr@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}, \verb@TRUE@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}.\end{list}
\end{minipage}\\[4ex]
\end{flushleft}
\begin{flushleft} \small
\begin{minipage}{\linewidth} \label{scrap69}
$\langle\,${\it Function prototypes}\nobreak\ {\footnotesize \NWtarget{nuweb?}{?}}$\,\rangle\equiv$
\vspace{-1ex}
\begin{list}{}{} \item
\mbox{}\verb@void initialise_delimit_scrap_array(void);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@@{\NWsep}
\end{list}
\vspace{-1ex}
\footnotesize\addtolength{\baselineskip}{-1ex}
\begin{list}{}{\setlength{\itemsep}{-\parsep}\setlength{\itemindent}{-\leftmargin}}
\item \NWtxtMacroDefBy\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}.
\item \NWtxtMacroRefIn\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}.
\end{list}
\end{minipage}\\[4ex]
\end{flushleft}
\begin{flushleft} \small
\begin{minipage}{\linewidth} \label{scrap70}
\verb@"latex.c"@\nobreak\ {\footnotesize \NWtarget{nuweb?}{?} }$\equiv$
\vspace{-1ex}
\begin{list}{}{} \item
\mbox{}\verb@int scrap_type = 0;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@@\\
\mbox{}\verb@static void copy_scrap(file, prefix)@\\
\mbox{}\verb@     FILE *file;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@     int prefix;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@{@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  int indent = 0;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  int c;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  if (source_last == '{') scrap_type = 0;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  if (source_last == '[') scrap_type = 1;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  if (source_last == '(') scrap_type = 2;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  c = source_get();@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  if (prefix) fputs(delimit_scrap[scrap_type][3], file);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  fputs(delimit_scrap[scrap_type][0], file);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  while (1) {@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    switch (c) {@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      case '\n': fputs(delimit_scrap[scrap_type][1], file);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@                 if (prefix) fputs(delimit_scrap[scrap_type][4], file);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@                 fputs("\n", file);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@                 if (prefix) fputs(delimit_scrap[scrap_type][3], file);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@                 fputs(delimit_scrap[scrap_type][0], file);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@                 indent = 0;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@                 break;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      case '\t': @\hbox{$\langle\,${\it Expand tab into spaces}\nobreak\ {\footnotesize \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}}$\,\rangle$}\verb@@\\
\mbox{}\verb@                 break;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      default:   @\\
\mbox{}\verb@         if (c==nw_char)@\\
\mbox{}\verb@           {@\\
\mbox{}\verb@             @\hbox{$\langle\,${\it Check at-sequence for end-of-scrap}\nobreak\ {\footnotesize \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}}$\,\rangle$}\verb@@\\
\mbox{}\verb@             break;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@           }           @\\
\mbox{}\verb@         putc(c, file);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@                 indent++;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@                 break;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    }@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    c = source_get();@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  }@\\
\mbox{}\verb@}@\\
\mbox{}\verb@@{\NWsep}
\end{list}
\vspace{-1ex}
\footnotesize\addtolength{\baselineskip}{-1ex}
\begin{list}{}{\setlength{\itemsep}{-\parsep}\setlength{\itemindent}{-\leftmargin}}
\item \NWtxtFileDefBy\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}.
\end{list}
\vspace{-2ex}
\footnotesize\addtolength{\baselineskip}{-1ex}
\begin{list}{}{\setlength{\itemsep}{-\parsep}\setlength{\itemindent}{-\leftmargin}}
\item \NWtxtIdentsDefed\nobreak\  \verb@copy_scrap@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}, \verb@delimit_scrap@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}, \verb@scrap_type@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}.\end{list}
\vspace{-2ex}
\footnotesize\addtolength{\baselineskip}{-1ex}
\begin{list}{}{\setlength{\itemsep}{-\parsep}\setlength{\itemindent}{-\leftmargin}}
\item \NWtxtIdentsUsed\nobreak\  \verb@FILE@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}, \verb@fputs@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}, \verb@nw_char@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}, \verb@putc@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}, \verb@source_get@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}, \verb@source_last@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}.\end{list}
\end{minipage}\\[4ex]
\end{flushleft}
When we encouter the command to change the `nuweb character' we call
this function. It updates the scrap formatting directives accordingly.

\begin{flushleft} \small
\begin{minipage}{\linewidth} \label{scrap71}
\verb@"latex.c"@\nobreak\ {\footnotesize \NWtarget{nuweb?}{?} }$\equiv$
\vspace{-1ex}
\begin{list}{}{} \item
\mbox{}\verb@void update_delimit_scrap()@\\
\mbox{}\verb@{@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  static int been_here_before = 0;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  /* {}-mode begin */@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  if (listings_flag == TRUE) {@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    delimit_scrap[0][0][10] = nw_char;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  } else {@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    delimit_scrap[0][0][5] = nw_char;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  }@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  /* {}-mode end */@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  delimit_scrap[0][1][0] = nw_char;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  /* {}-mode insert nw_char */@\\
\mbox{}\verb@@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  delimit_scrap[0][2][0] = nw_char;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  delimit_scrap[0][2][6] = nw_char;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  if (listings_flag == TRUE) {@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    delimit_scrap[0][2][18] = nw_char;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  } else {@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    delimit_scrap[0][2][13] = nw_char;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  }  @\\
\mbox{}\verb@@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  /* []-mode insert nw_char */@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  delimit_scrap[1][2][0] = nw_char;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  /* ()-mode insert nw_char */@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  delimit_scrap[2][2][0] = nw_char;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@}@\\
\mbox{}\verb@@{\NWsep}
\end{list}
\vspace{-1ex}
\footnotesize\addtolength{\baselineskip}{-1ex}
\begin{list}{}{\setlength{\itemsep}{-\parsep}\setlength{\itemindent}{-\leftmargin}}
\item \NWtxtFileDefBy\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}.
\end{list}
\vspace{-2ex}
\footnotesize\addtolength{\baselineskip}{-1ex}
\begin{list}{}{\setlength{\itemsep}{-\parsep}\setlength{\itemindent}{-\leftmargin}}
\item \NWtxtIdentsDefed\nobreak\  \verb@update_delimit_scrap@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}.\end{list}
\vspace{-2ex}
\footnotesize\addtolength{\baselineskip}{-1ex}
\begin{list}{}{\setlength{\itemsep}{-\parsep}\setlength{\itemindent}{-\leftmargin}}
\item \NWtxtIdentsUsed\nobreak\  \verb@delimit_scrap@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}, \verb@listings_flag@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}, \verb@nw_char@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}, \verb@TRUE@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}.\end{list}
\end{minipage}\\[4ex]
\end{flushleft}
\begin{flushleft} \small

\begin{flushleft} \small
\begin{minipage}{\linewidth} \label{scrap73}
$\langle\,${\it Expand tab into spaces}\nobreak\ {\footnotesize \NWtarget{nuweb?}{?}}$\,\rangle\equiv$
\vspace{-1ex}
\begin{list}{}{} \item
\mbox{}\verb@{@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  int delta = 3 - (indent % 3);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  indent += delta;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  while (delta > 0) {@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    putc(' ', file);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    delta--;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  }@\\
\mbox{}\verb@}@{\NWsep}
\end{list}
\vspace{-1ex}
\footnotesize\addtolength{\baselineskip}{-1ex}

\item \NWtxtIdentsUsed\nobreak\  \verb@putc@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}.\end{list}
\end{minipage}\\[4ex]
\end{flushleft}
\begin{flushleft} \small
\begin{minipage}{\linewidth} \label{scrap74}
$\langle\,${\it Check at-sequence for end-of-scrap}\nobreak\ {\footnotesize \NWtarget{nuweb?}{?}}$\,\rangle\equiv$
\vspace{-1ex}
\begin{list}{}{} \item
\mbox{}\verb@{@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  c = source_get();@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  switch (c) {@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    case 'x': @\hbox{$\langle\,${\it Copy label from source into}\nobreak\ ({\footnotesize \label{scrap75}
 }\mbox{}\verb@file@ ) {\footnotesize \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}}$\,\rangle$}\verb@@\\
\mbox{}\verb@              break;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    case '+':@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    case '-':@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    case '|': @\hbox{$\langle\,${\it Skip over index entries}\nobreak\ {\footnotesize \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}}$\,\rangle$}\verb@@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    case ',':@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    case ')':@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    case ']':@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    case '}': fputs(delimit_scrap[scrap_type][1], file);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@              return;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    case '<': @\hbox{$\langle\,${\it Format macro name}\nobreak\ {\footnotesize \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}}$\,\rangle$}\verb@@\\
\mbox{}\verb@              break;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    case '%': @\hbox{$\langle\,${\it Skip commented-out code}\nobreak\ {\footnotesize \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}}$\,\rangle$}\verb@@\\
\mbox{}\verb@              break;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    case '_': @\hbox{$\langle\,${\it Bold Keyword}\nobreak\ {\footnotesize \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}}$\,\rangle$}\verb@@\\
\mbox{}\verb@              break;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    case 'f': @\hbox{$\langle\,${\it Italic "file name"}\nobreak\ {\footnotesize \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}}$\,\rangle$}\verb@@\\
\mbox{}\verb@              break;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    case '1': case '2': case '3': @\\
\mbox{}\verb@    case '4': case '5': case '6': @\\
\mbox{}\verb@    case '7': case '8': case '9': @\\
\mbox{}\verb@              fputs(delimit_scrap[scrap_type][1], file);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@              fputc(nw_char, file);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@              fputc(c,   file);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@              fputs(delimit_scrap[scrap_type][0], file);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@              break;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    default:  @\\
\mbox{}\verb@          if (c==nw_char)@\\
\mbox{}\verb@            {@\\
\mbox{}\verb@              fputs(delimit_scrap[scrap_type][2], file);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@              break;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@            }@\\
\mbox{}\verb@          /* ignore these since pass1 will have warned about them */@\\
\mbox{}\verb@              break;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  }@\\
\mbox{}\verb@}@{\NWsep}
\end{list}
\vspace{-1ex}
\footnotesize\addtolength{\baselineskip}{-1ex}
\begin{list}{}{\setlength{\itemsep}{-\parsep}\setlength{\itemindent}{-\leftmargin}}
\item \NWtxtMacroRefIn\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}.
\end{list}
\end{minipage}\\[4ex]
\end{flushleft}
\begin{flushleft} \small
\begin{minipage}{\linewidth} \label{scrap76}
$\langle\,${\it Copy label from source into}\nobreak\ {\footnotesize \NWtarget{nuweb?}{?}}$\,\rangle\equiv$
\vspace{-1ex}
\begin{list}{}{} \item
\mbox{}\verb@{@\\
\mbox{}\verb@   @\hbox{$\langle\,${\it Get label from}\nobreak\ ({\footnotesize \label{scrap77}
 }\mbox{}\verb@source_get()@ ) {\footnotesize \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}}$\,\rangle$}\verb@@\\
\mbox{}\verb@   write_label(label_name, @@1\verb@);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@}@{\NWsep}
\end{list}
\vspace{-1ex}
\footnotesize\addtolength{\baselineskip}{-1ex}
\begin{list}{}{\setlength{\itemsep}{-\parsep}\setlength{\itemindent}{-\leftmargin}}
\item \NWtxtMacroRefIn\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}.
\end{list}
\vspace{-2ex}
\footnotesize\addtolength{\baselineskip}{-1ex}
\begin{list}{}{\setlength{\itemsep}{-\parsep}\setlength{\itemindent}{-\leftmargin}}
\item \NWtxtIdentsUsed\nobreak\  \verb@source_get@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}.\end{list}
\end{minipage}\\[4ex]
\end{flushleft}
There's no need to check for errors here, since we will have already
pointed out any during the first pass.
\begin{flushleft} \small
\begin{minipage}{\linewidth} \label{scrap78}
$\langle\,${\it Skip over index entries}\nobreak\ {\footnotesize \NWtarget{nuweb?}{?}}$\,\rangle\equiv$
\vspace{-1ex}
\begin{list}{}{} \item
\mbox{}\verb@{@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  do {@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    do@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      c = source_get();@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    while (c != nw_char);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    c = source_get();@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  } while (c != '}' && c != ']' && c != ')' );@\\
\mbox{}\verb@}@{\NWsep}
\end{list}
\vspace{-1ex}
\footnotesize\addtolength{\baselineskip}{-1ex}

\mbox{}\verb@  do {@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      fputc(c, file);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      c = source_get();@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  } while (c != nw_char);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  c = source_get();@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  fprintf(file, "}");@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  fputs(delimit_scrap[scrap_type][0], file);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@}@{\NWsep}

$\langle\,${\it Format macro name}\nobreak\ {\footnotesize \NWtarget{nuweb?}{?}}$\,\rangle\equiv$
\vspace{-1ex}
\begin{list}{}{} \item
\mbox{}\verb@{@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  Name *name = collect_scrap_name();@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  fputs(delimit_scrap[scrap_type][1],file);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  if (prefix)@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    fputs("\\hbox{", file);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  fprintf(file, "$\\langle\\,${\\it %s}\\nobreak\\ ", name->spelling);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  if (scrap_name_has_parameters) {@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    @\hbox{$\langle\,${\it Format macro parameters}\nobreak\ {\footnotesize \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}}$\,\rangle$}\verb@@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  }@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  fprintf(file, "{\\footnotesize ");@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  if (name->defs)@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    @\hbox{$\langle\,${\it Write abbreviated definition list}\nobreak\ {\footnotesize \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}}$\,\rangle$}\verb@@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  else {@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    putc('?', file);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    fprintf(stderr, "%s: never defined <%s>\n",@\\
\mbox{}\verb@            command_name, name->spelling);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  }@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  fputs("}$\\,\\rangle$", file);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  if (prefix)@\\
\mbox{}\verb@     fputs("}", file);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  fputs(delimit_scrap[scrap_type][0], file);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@}@{\NWsep}
\end{list}

\subsection{Generating the Indices}

\begin{flushleft} \small
\begin{minipage}{\linewidth} \label{scrap84}
$\langle\,${\it Write index of file names}\nobreak\ {\footnotesize \NWtarget{nuweb?}{?}}$\,\rangle\equiv$
\vspace{-1ex}
\begin{list}{}{} \item
\mbox{}\verb@{@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  if (file_names) {@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    fputs("\n{\\small\\begin{list}{}{\\setlength{\\itemsep}{-\\parsep}",@\\
\mbox{}\verb@          tex_file);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    fputs("\\setlength{\\itemindent}{-\\leftmargin}}\n", tex_file);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    format_entry(file_names, tex_file, TRUE, 0);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    fputs("\\end{list}}", tex_file);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  }@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  c = source_get();@\\
\mbox{}\verb@}@{\NWsep}
\end{list}
\vspace{-1ex}
\footnotesize\addtolength{\baselineskip}{-1ex}
\begin{list}{}{\setlength{\itemsep}{-\parsep}\setlength{\itemindent}{-\leftmargin}}

\end{list}

\end{minipage}\\[4ex]

\begin{flushleft} \small
\begin{minipage}{\linewidth} \label{scrap85}
$\langle\,${\it Write index of macro names}\nobreak\ {\footnotesize \NWtarget{nuweb?}{?}}$\,\rangle\equiv$
\vspace{-1ex}
\begin{list}{}{} \item
\mbox{}\verb@{@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  if (macro_names) {@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    unsigned char sector = current_sector;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    int c = source_get();@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    if (c == '+')@\\
\mbox{}\verb@       sector = 0;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    else@\\
\mbox{}\verb@       source_ungetc(&c);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    fputs("\n{\\small\\begin{list}{}{\\setlength{\\itemsep}{-\\parsep}",@\\
\mbox{}\verb@          tex_file);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    fputs("\\setlength{\\itemindent}{-\\leftmargin}}\n", tex_file);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    format_entry(macro_names, tex_file, FALSE, sector);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    fputs("\\end{list}}", tex_file);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  }@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  c = source_get();@\\
\mbox{}\verb@}@{\NWsep}
\end{list}

\begin{flushleft} \small
\begin{minipage}{\linewidth} \label{scrap86}

\vspace{-1ex}
\begin{list}{}{} \item
\mbox{}\verb@static void format_entry(name, tex_file, file_flag, sector)@\\
\mbox{}\verb@     Name *name;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@     FILE *tex_file;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@     int file_flag;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@     unsigned char sector;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@{@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  while (name) {@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    format_entry(name->llink, tex_file, file_flag, sector);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    @\hbox{$\langle\,${\it Format an index entry}\nobreak\ {\footnotesize \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}}$\,\rangle$}\verb@@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    name = name->rlink;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  }@\\
\mbox{}\verb@}@\\
\mbox{}\verb@@{\NWsep}
\end{list}

\mbox{}\verb@  }@\\

\mbox{}\verb@    fprintf(tex_file, "$\\langle\\,$%s\\nobreak\\ {\\footnotesize ", name->spelling);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    @\hbox{$\langle\,${\it Write defining scrap numbers}\nobreak\ {\footnotesize \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}}$\,\rangle$}\verb@@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    fputs("}$\\,\\rangle$ ", tex_file);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    @\hbox{$\langle\,${\it Write referencing scrap numbers}\nobreak\ {\footnotesize \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}}$\,\rangle$}\verb@@\\

\begin{flushleft} \small
\begin{minipage}{\linewidth} \label{scrap88}
$\langle\,${\it Write file's defining scrap numbers}\nobreak\ {\footnotesize \NWtarget{nuweb?}{?}}$\,\rangle\equiv$
\vspace{-1ex}
\begin{list}{}{} \item

\mbox{}\verb@  Scrap_Node *p = name->defs;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  fputs("{\\footnotesize {\\NWtxtDefBy}", tex_file);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  if (p->next) {@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    /* fputs("s ", tex_file); */@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      putc(' ', tex_file);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    print_scrap_numbers(tex_file, p);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  }@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  else {@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    putc(' ', tex_file);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    fputs("\\NWlink{nuweb", tex_file);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    write_single_scrap_ref(tex_file, p->scrap);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    fputs("}{", tex_file);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    write_single_scrap_ref(tex_file, p->scrap);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    fputs("}", tex_file);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    putc('.', tex_file);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  }@\\

\begin{flushleft} \small
\begin{minipage}{\linewidth} \label{scrap89}
$\langle\,${\it Write defining scrap numbers}\nobreak\ {\footnotesize \NWtarget{nuweb?}{?}}$\,\rangle\equiv$
\vspace{-1ex}
\begin{list}{}{} \item
\mbox{}\verb@{@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  Scrap_Node *p = name->defs;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  if (p) {@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    int page;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    fputs("\\NWlink{nuweb", tex_file);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    write_scrap_ref(tex_file, p->scrap, -1, &page);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    fputs("}{", tex_file);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    write_scrap_ref(tex_file, p->scrap, TRUE, &page);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    fputs("}", tex_file);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    p = p->next;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    while (p) {@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      fputs("\\NWlink{nuweb", tex_file);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      write_scrap_ref(tex_file, p->scrap, -1, &page);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      fputs("}{", tex_file);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      write_scrap_ref(tex_file, p->scrap, FALSE, &page);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      fputs("}", tex_file);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      p = p->next;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    }@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  }@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  else@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    putc('?', tex_file);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@}@{\NWsep}
\end{list}
\vspace{-1ex}
\footnotesize\addtolength{\baselineskip}{-1ex}
\begin{list}{}{\setlength{\itemsep}{-\parsep}\setlength{\itemindent}{-\leftmargin}}
\item \NWtxtMacroRefIn\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}.
\end{list}
\vspace{-2ex}
\footnotesize\addtolength{\baselineskip}{-1ex}
\begin{list}{}{\setlength{\itemsep}{-\parsep}\setlength{\itemindent}{-\leftmargin}}
\item \NWtxtIdentsUsed\nobreak\  \verb@FALSE@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}, \verb@fputs@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}, \verb@putc@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}, \verb@Scrap_Node@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}, \verb@TRUE@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}, \verb@write_scrap_ref@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}.\end{list}
\end{minipage}\\[4ex]
\end{flushleft}
\begin{flushleft} \small
\begin{minipage}{\linewidth} \label{scrap90}
$\langle\,${\it Write referencing scrap numbers}\nobreak\ {\footnotesize \NWtarget{nuweb?}{?}}$\,\rangle\equiv$
\vspace{-1ex}
\begin{list}{}{} \item
\mbox{}\verb@{@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  Scrap_Node *p = name->uses;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  fputs("{\\footnotesize ", tex_file);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  if (p) {@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    fputs("{\\NWtxtRefIn}", tex_file);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    if (p->next) {@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      /* fputs("s ", tex_file); */@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      putc(' ', tex_file);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      print_scrap_numbers(tex_file, p);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    }@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    else {@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      putc(' ', tex_file);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      fputs("\\NWlink{nuweb", tex_file);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      write_single_scrap_ref(tex_file, p->scrap);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      fputs("}{", tex_file);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      write_single_scrap_ref(tex_file, p->scrap);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      fputs("}", tex_file);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      putc('.', tex_file);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    }@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  }@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  else@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    fputs("{\\NWtxtNoRef}.", tex_file);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  putc('}', tex_file);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@}@{\NWsep}
\end{list}
\vspace{-1ex}
\footnotesize\addtolength{\baselineskip}{-1ex}
\begin{list}{}{\setlength{\itemsep}{-\parsep}\setlength{\itemindent}{-\leftmargin}}
\item \NWtxtMacroRefIn\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}.
\end{list}
\vspace{-2ex}
\footnotesize\addtolength{\baselineskip}{-1ex}
\begin{list}{}{\setlength{\itemsep}{-\parsep}\setlength{\itemindent}{-\leftmargin}}
\item \NWtxtIdentsUsed\nobreak\  \verb@fputs@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}, \verb@print_scrap_numbers@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}, \verb@putc@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}, \verb@Scrap_Node@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}, \verb@write_single_scrap_ref@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}.\end{list}
\end{minipage}\\[4ex]
\end{flushleft}
\begin{flushleft} \small
\begin{minipage}{\linewidth} \label{scrap91}
\verb@"latex.c"@\nobreak\ {\footnotesize \NWtarget{nuweb?}{?} }$\equiv$
\vspace{-1ex}
\begin{list}{}{} \item
\mbox{}\verb@int has_sector(name, sector)@\\
\mbox{}\verb@Name * name;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@unsigned char sector;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@{@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  while(name) {@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    if (name->sector == sector)@\\
\mbox{}\verb@       return TRUE;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    if (has_sector(name->llink, sector))@\\
\mbox{}\verb@       return TRUE;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@     name = name->rlink;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@   }@\\
\mbox{}\verb@   return FALSE;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@}@\\
\mbox{}\verb@@{\NWsep}
\end{list}
\vspace{-1ex}
\footnotesize\addtolength{\baselineskip}{-1ex}
\begin{list}{}{\setlength{\itemsep}{-\parsep}\setlength{\itemindent}{-\leftmargin}}
\item \NWtxtFileDefBy\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}.
\end{list}
\vspace{-2ex}
\footnotesize\addtolength{\baselineskip}{-1ex}
\begin{list}{}{\setlength{\itemsep}{-\parsep}\setlength{\itemindent}{-\leftmargin}}
\item \NWtxtIdentsUsed\nobreak\  \verb@FALSE@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}, \verb@Name@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}, \verb@TRUE@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}.\end{list}
\end{minipage}\\[4ex]
\end{flushleft}
\begin{flushleft} \small
\begin{minipage}{\linewidth} \label{scrap92}
$\langle\,${\it Write index of user-specified names}\nobreak\ {\footnotesize \NWtarget{nuweb?}{?}}$\,\rangle\equiv$
\vspace{-1ex}
\begin{list}{}{} \item
\mbox{}\verb@{@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    unsigned char sector = current_sector;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    c = source_get();@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    if (c == '+') {@\\
\mbox{}\verb@       sector = 0;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@       c = source_get();@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    }@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    if (has_sector(user_names, sector)) {@\\
\mbox{}\verb@       fputs("\n{\\small\\begin{list}{}{\\setlength{\\itemsep}{-\\parsep}",@\\
\mbox{}\verb@             tex_file);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@       fputs("\\setlength{\\itemindent}{-\\leftmargin}}\n", tex_file);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@         format_user_entry(user_names, tex_file, sector);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@       fputs("\\end{list}}", tex_file);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    }@\\
\mbox{}\verb@}@{\NWsep}
\end{list}
\vspace{-1ex}
\footnotesize\addtolength{\baselineskip}{-1ex}
\begin{list}{}{\setlength{\itemsep}{-\parsep}\setlength{\itemindent}{-\leftmargin}}
\item \NWtxtMacroRefIn\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}.
\end{list}
\vspace{-2ex}
\footnotesize\addtolength{\baselineskip}{-1ex}
\begin{list}{}{\setlength{\itemsep}{-\parsep}\setlength{\itemindent}{-\leftmargin}}
\item \NWtxtIdentsUsed\nobreak\  \verb@current_sector@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}, \verb@format_user_entry@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}, \verb@fputs@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}, \verb@source_get@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}, \verb@user_names@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}.\end{list}
\end{minipage}\\[4ex]
\end{flushleft}
\begin{flushleft} \small
\begin{minipage}{\linewidth} \label{scrap93}
\verb@"latex.c"@\nobreak\ {\footnotesize \NWtarget{nuweb?}{?} }$\equiv$
\vspace{-1ex}
\begin{list}{}{} \item
\mbox{}\verb@static void format_user_entry(name, tex_file, sector)@\\
\mbox{}\verb@     Name *name;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@     FILE *tex_file;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@     unsigned char sector;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@{@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  while (name) {@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    format_user_entry(name->llink, tex_file, sector);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    @\hbox{$\langle\,${\it Format a user index entry}\nobreak\ {\footnotesize \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}}$\,\rangle$}\verb@@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    name = name->rlink;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  }@\\
\mbox{}\verb@}@\\
\mbox{}\verb@@{\NWsep}
\end{list}
\vspace{-1ex}
\footnotesize\addtolength{\baselineskip}{-1ex}

\end{list}

\vspace{-2ex}
\footnotesize\addtolength{\baselineskip}{-1ex}
\begin{list}{}{\setlength{\itemsep}{-\parsep}\setlength{\itemindent}{-\leftmargin}}
\item \NWtxtIdentsUsed\nobreak\  \verb@FILE@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}, \verb@Name@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}.\end{list}
\end{minipage}\\[4ex]
\end{flushleft}
\begin{flushleft} \small \label{scrap94}
$\langle\,${\it Format a user index entry}\nobreak\ {\footnotesize \NWtarget{nuweb?}{?}}$\,\rangle\equiv$
\vspace{-1ex}
\begin{list}{}{} \item
\mbox{}\verb@if (name->sector == sector){@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  Scrap_Node *uses = name->uses;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  if ( uses || dangling_flag ) {@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    int page;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    Scrap_Node *defs = name->defs;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    fprintf(tex_file, "\\item \\verb%c%s%c: ", nw_char,name->spelling,nw_char);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    if (!uses) {@\\
\mbox{}\verb@        fputs("(\\underline{", tex_file);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@        fputs("\\NWlink{nuweb", tex_file);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@        write_single_scrap_ref(tex_file, defs->scrap);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@        fputs("}{", tex_file);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@        write_single_scrap_ref(tex_file, defs->scrap);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@        fputs("})}", tex_file);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@        page = -2;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@        defs = defs->next;        @\\
\mbox{}\verb@    }@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    else@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      if (uses->scrap < defs->scrap) {    @\\
\mbox{}\verb@      fputs("\\NWlink{nuweb", tex_file);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      write_scrap_ref(tex_file, uses->scrap, -1, &page);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      fputs("}{", tex_file);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      write_scrap_ref(tex_file, uses->scrap, TRUE, &page);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      fputs("}", tex_file);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      uses = uses->next;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    }@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    else {@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      if (defs->scrap == uses->scrap)@\\
\mbox{}\verb@        uses = uses->next;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      fputs("\\underline{", tex_file);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      fputs("\\NWlink{nuweb", tex_file);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      write_single_scrap_ref(tex_file, defs->scrap);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      fputs("}{", tex_file);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      write_single_scrap_ref(tex_file, defs->scrap);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      fputs("}}", tex_file);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      page = -2;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      defs = defs->next;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    }@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    while (uses || defs) {@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      if (uses && (!defs || uses->scrap < defs->scrap)) {@\\
\mbox{}\verb@        fputs("\\NWlink{nuweb", tex_file);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@        write_scrap_ref(tex_file, uses->scrap, -1, &page);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@        fputs("}{", tex_file);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@        write_scrap_ref(tex_file, uses->scrap, FALSE, &page);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@        fputs("}", tex_file);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@        uses = uses->next;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      }@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      else {@\\
\mbox{}\verb@        if (uses && defs->scrap == uses->scrap)@\\
\mbox{}\verb@          uses = uses->next;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@        fputs(", \\underline{", tex_file);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@@\\
\mbox{}\verb@        fputs("\\NWlink{nuweb", tex_file);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@        write_single_scrap_ref(tex_file, defs->scrap);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@        fputs("}{", tex_file);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@        write_single_scrap_ref(tex_file, defs->scrap);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@        fputs("}", tex_file);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@ @\\
\mbox{}\verb@        putc('}', tex_file);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@        page = -2;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@        defs = defs->next;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      }@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    }@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    fputs(".\n", tex_file);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  }@\\
\mbox{}\verb@}@{\NWsep}
\end{list}
\vspace{-1ex}
\footnotesize\addtolength{\baselineskip}{-1ex}
\begin{list}{}{\setlength{\itemsep}{-\parsep}\setlength{\itemindent}{-\leftmargin}}
\item \NWtxtMacroRefIn\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}.
\end{list}
\vspace{-2ex}
\footnotesize\addtolength{\baselineskip}{-1ex}
\begin{list}{}{\setlength{\itemsep}{-\parsep}\setlength{\itemindent}{-\leftmargin}}
\item \NWtxtIdentsUsed\nobreak\  \verb@dangling_flag@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}, \verb@FALSE@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}, \verb@fprintf@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}, \verb@fputs@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}, \verb@nw_char@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}, \verb@putc@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}, \verb@Scrap_Node@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}, \verb@TRUE@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}, \verb@write_scrap_ref@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}, \verb@write_single_scrap_ref@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}.\end{list}
\end{flushleft}
\section{Writing the LaTeX File with HTML Scraps} \label{html-file} 

The HTML generated is patterned closely upon the {\LaTeX} generated in
the previous section.\footnote{\relax While writing this section, I
tried to follow Preston's style as displayed in
Section~\ref{latex-file}---J. D. R.}  When a file name ends in
\verb|.hw|, the second pass (invoked via a call to \verb|write_html|)
copies most of the text from the source file straight into a
\verb|.tex| file.  Definitions are formatted slightly and
cross-reference information is printed out.

\begin{flushleft} \small
\begin{minipage}{\linewidth} \label{scrap95}
$\langle\,${\it Function prototypes}\nobreak\ {\footnotesize \NWtarget{nuweb?}{?}}$\,\rangle\equiv$
\vspace{-1ex}
\begin{list}{}{} \item
\mbox{}\verb@extern void write_html();@\\
\mbox{}\verb@@{\NWsep}
\end{list}
\vspace{-1ex}
\footnotesize\addtolength{\baselineskip}{-1ex}
\begin{list}{}{\setlength{\itemsep}{-\parsep}\setlength{\itemindent}{-\leftmargin}}
\item \NWtxtMacroDefBy\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}.
\item \NWtxtMacroRefIn\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}.
\end{list}
\vspace{-2ex}
\footnotesize\addtolength{\baselineskip}{-1ex}
\begin{list}{}{\setlength{\itemsep}{-\parsep}\setlength{\itemindent}{-\leftmargin}}
\item \NWtxtIdentsUsed\nobreak\  \verb@write_html@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}.\end{list}
\end{minipage}\\[4ex]
\end{flushleft}
We need a few local function declarations before we get into the body
of \verb|write_html|.

\begin{flushleft} \small
\begin{minipage}{\linewidth} \label{scrap96}
\verb@"html.c"@\nobreak\ {\footnotesize \NWtarget{nuweb?}{?} }$\equiv$
\vspace{-1ex}
\begin{list}{}{} \item
\mbox{}\verb@static void copy_scrap();               /* formats the body of a scrap */@\\
\mbox{}\verb@static void display_scrap_ref();        /* formats a scrap reference */@\\
\mbox{}\verb@static void display_scrap_numbers();    /* formats a list of scrap numbers */@\\
\mbox{}\verb@static void print_scrap_numbers();      /* pluralizes scrap formats list */@\\
\mbox{}\verb@static void format_entry();             /* formats an index entry */@\\
\mbox{}\verb@static void format_user_entry();@\\
\mbox{}\verb@@{\NWsep}
\end{list}
\vspace{-1ex}
\footnotesize\addtolength{\baselineskip}{-1ex}
\begin{list}{}{\setlength{\itemsep}{-\parsep}\setlength{\itemindent}{-\leftmargin}}
\item \NWtxtFileDefBy\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}.
\end{list}
\vspace{-2ex}
\footnotesize\addtolength{\baselineskip}{-1ex}
\begin{list}{}{\setlength{\itemsep}{-\parsep}\setlength{\itemindent}{-\leftmargin}}
\item \NWtxtIdentsUsed\nobreak\  \verb@copy_scrap@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}, \verb@display_scrap_numbers@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}, \verb@display_scrap_ref@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}, \verb@format_entry@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}, \verb@format_user_entry@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}, \verb@print_scrap_numbers@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}.\end{list}
\end{minipage}\\[4ex]
\end{flushleft}
The routine \verb|write_html| takes two file names as parameters: the
name of the web source file and the name of the \verb|.tex| output file.
\begin{flushleft} \small
\begin{minipage}{\linewidth} \label{scrap97}
\verb@"html.c"@\nobreak\ {\footnotesize \NWtarget{nuweb?}{?} }$\equiv$
\vspace{-1ex}
\begin{list}{}{} \item
\mbox{}\verb@void write_html(file_name, html_name)@\\
\mbox{}\verb@     char *file_name;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@     char *html_name;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@{@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  FILE *html_file = fopen(html_name, "w");@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  FILE *tex_file = html_file;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  @\hbox{$\langle\,${\it Write LaTeX limbo definitions}\nobreak\ {\footnotesize \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}}$\,\rangle$}\verb@@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  if (html_file) {@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    if (verbose_flag)@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      fprintf(stderr, "writing %s\n", html_name);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    source_open(file_name);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    @\hbox{$\langle\,${\it Copy \verb|source_file| into \verb|html_file|}\nobreak\ {\footnotesize \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}}$\,\rangle$}\verb@@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    fclose(html_file);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  }@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  else@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    fprintf(stderr, "%s: can't open %s\n", command_name, html_name);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@}@\\
\mbox{}\verb@@{\NWsep}
\end{list}
\vspace{-1ex}
\footnotesize\addtolength{\baselineskip}{-1ex}
\begin{list}{}{\setlength{\itemsep}{-\parsep}\setlength{\itemindent}{-\leftmargin}}
\item \NWtxtFileDefBy\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}.
\end{list}
\vspace{-2ex}
\footnotesize\addtolength{\baselineskip}{-1ex}
\begin{list}{}{\setlength{\itemsep}{-\parsep}\setlength{\itemindent}{-\leftmargin}}
\item \NWtxtIdentsDefed\nobreak\  \verb@write_html@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}.\end{list}
\vspace{-2ex}
\footnotesize\addtolength{\baselineskip}{-1ex}
\begin{list}{}{\setlength{\itemsep}{-\parsep}\setlength{\itemindent}{-\leftmargin}}
\item \NWtxtIdentsUsed\nobreak\  \verb@command_name@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}, \verb@fclose@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}, \verb@FILE@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}, \verb@fopen@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}, \verb@fprintf@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}, \verb@source_open@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}, \verb@stderr@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}, \verb@verbose_flag@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}.\end{list}
\end{minipage}\\[4ex]
\end{flushleft}
We make our second (and final) pass through the source web, this time
copying characters straight into the \verb|.tex| file. However, we keep
an eye peeled for \verb|@|~characters, which signal a command sequence.

\begin{flushleft} \small
\begin{minipage}{\linewidth} \label{scrap98}
$\langle\,${\it Copy \verb|source_file| into \verb|html_file|}\nobreak\ {\footnotesize \NWtarget{nuweb?}{?}}$\,\rangle\equiv$
\vspace{-1ex}
\begin{list}{}{} \item
\mbox{}\verb@{@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  int c = source_get();@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  while (c != EOF) {@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    if (c == nw_char)@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      @\hbox{$\langle\,${\it Interpret HTML at-sequence}\nobreak\ {\footnotesize \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}}$\,\rangle$}\verb@@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    else {@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      putc(c, html_file);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      c = source_get();@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    }@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  }@\\
\mbox{}\verb@}@{\NWsep}
\end{list}
\vspace{-1ex}
\footnotesize\addtolength{\baselineskip}{-1ex}
\begin{list}{}{\setlength{\itemsep}{-\parsep}\setlength{\itemindent}{-\leftmargin}}
\item \NWtxtMacroRefIn\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}.
\end{list}
\vspace{-2ex}
\footnotesize\addtolength{\baselineskip}{-1ex}
\begin{list}{}{\setlength{\itemsep}{-\parsep}\setlength{\itemindent}{-\leftmargin}}
\item \NWtxtIdentsUsed\nobreak\  \verb@nw_char@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}, \verb@putc@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}, \verb@source_get@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}.\end{list}
\end{minipage}\\[4ex]
\end{flushleft}
\begin{flushleft} \small
\begin{minipage}{\linewidth} \label{scrap99}
$\langle\,${\it Interpret HTML at-sequence}\nobreak\ {\footnotesize \NWtarget{nuweb?}{?}}$\,\rangle\equiv$
\vspace{-1ex}
\begin{list}{}{} \item
\mbox{}\verb@{@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  c = source_get();@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  switch (c) {@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    case 'r':@\\
\mbox{}\verb@          c = source_get();@\\
\mbox{}\verb@          nw_char = c;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@          update_delimit_scrap();@\\
\mbox{}\verb@          break;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    case 'O': @\\
\mbox{}\verb@    case 'o': @\hbox{$\langle\,${\it Write HTML output file definition}\nobreak\ {\footnotesize \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}}$\,\rangle$}\verb@@\\
\mbox{}\verb@              break;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    case 'D': @\\
\mbox{}\verb@    case 'd': @\hbox{$\langle\,${\it Write HTML macro definition}\nobreak\ {\footnotesize \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}}$\,\rangle$}\verb@@\\
\mbox{}\verb@              break;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    case 'f': @\hbox{$\langle\,${\it Write HTML index of file names}\nobreak\ {\footnotesize \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}}$\,\rangle$}\verb@@\\
\mbox{}\verb@              break;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    case 'm': @\hbox{$\langle\,${\it Write HTML index of macro names}\nobreak\ {\footnotesize \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}}$\,\rangle$}\verb@@\\
\mbox{}\verb@              break;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    case 'u': @\hbox{$\langle\,${\it Write HTML index of user-specified names}\nobreak\ {\footnotesize \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}}$\,\rangle$}\verb@@\\
\mbox{}\verb@              break;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    default:  @\\
\mbox{}\verb@          if (c==nw_char)@\\
\mbox{}\verb@            putc(c, html_file);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@          c = source_get();@\\
\mbox{}\verb@              break;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  }@\\
\mbox{}\verb@}@{\NWsep}
\end{list}
\vspace{-1ex}
\footnotesize\addtolength{\baselineskip}{-1ex}
\begin{list}{}{\setlength{\itemsep}{-\parsep}\setlength{\itemindent}{-\leftmargin}}
\item \NWtxtMacroRefIn\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}.
\end{list}
\vspace{-2ex}
\footnotesize\addtolength{\baselineskip}{-1ex}
\begin{list}{}{\setlength{\itemsep}{-\parsep}\setlength{\itemindent}{-\leftmargin}}
\item \NWtxtIdentsUsed\nobreak\  \verb@nw_char@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}, \verb@putc@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}, \verb@source_get@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}, \verb@update_delimit_scrap@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}.\end{list}
\end{minipage}\\[4ex]
\end{flushleft}
\subsection{Formatting Definitions}

We go through only a little amount of effort to format a definition.
The HTML for the previous macro definition should look like this
(perhaps modulo the scrap references):

\begin{verbatim}
<pre>
<a name="nuweb68">&lt;Interpret HTML at-sequence 68&gt;</a> =
{
  c = source_get();
  switch (c) {
    case 'O': 
    case 'o': &lt;Write HTML output file definition <a href="#nuweb69">69</a>&gt;
              break;
    case 'D': 
    case 'd': &lt;Write HTML macro definition <a href="#nuweb71">71</a>&gt;
              break;
    case 'f': &lt;Write HTML index of file names <a href="#nuweb86">86</a>&gt;
              break;
    case 'm': &lt;Write HTML index of macro names <a href="#nuweb87">87</a>&gt;
              break;
    case 'u': &lt;Write HTML index of user-specified names <a href="#nuweb93">93</a>&gt;
              break;
    default:  
         if (c==nw_char)
           putc(c, html_file);
         c = source_get();
              break;
  }
}&lt;&gt;</pre>
Macro referenced in scrap <a href="#nuweb67">67</a>.
<br>
\end{verbatim}

Macro and file definitions are formatted nearly identically.
I've factored the common parts out into separate scraps.

I don't format a macro name at all specially, figuring the programmer
might want to use italics or bold face in the midst of the name.  Note
that in this implementation, programmers may only use directives in
macro names that are recognized in preformatted text elements (PRE).

Modification 2001--02--15.: I'm interpreting the macro name
as regular LaTex, so that any formatting can be used in it. To use
HTML formatting, the \verb|rawhtml| environment should be used.

\begin{flushleft} \small
\begin{minipage}{\linewidth} \label{scrap103}

\mbox{}\verb@  fputs(name->spelling, html_file);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  fputs("\\begin{rawhtml} ", html_file);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  write_single_scrap_ref(html_file, scraps);@\\

\mbox{}\verb@@{\NWsep}

\subsubsection{Formatting a Scrap}

We must translate HTML special keywords into entities in scraps.

\begin{flushleft} \small
\begin{minipage}{\linewidth} \label{scrap113}
\verb@"html.c"@\nobreak\ {\footnotesize \NWtarget{nuweb?}{?} }$\equiv$
\vspace{-1ex}
\begin{list}{}{} \item
\mbox{}\verb@static void copy_scrap(file, prefix)@\\
\mbox{}\verb@     FILE *file;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@{@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  int indent = 0;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  int c = source_get();@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  while (1) {@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    switch (c) {@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      case '<' : fputs("&lt;", file);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@                 indent++;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@                 break;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      case '>' : fputs("&gt;", file);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@                 indent++;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@                 break;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      case '&' : fputs("&amp;", file);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@                 indent++;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@                 break;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      case '\n': fputc(c, file);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@                 indent = 0;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@                 break;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      case '\t': @\hbox{$\langle\,${\it Expand tab into spaces}\nobreak\ {\footnotesize \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}}$\,\rangle$}\verb@@\\
\mbox{}\verb@                 break;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      default:   @\\
\mbox{}\verb@         if (c==nw_char)@\\
\mbox{}\verb@           {@\\
\mbox{}\verb@             @\hbox{$\langle\,${\it Check HTML at-sequence for end-of-scrap}\nobreak\ {\footnotesize \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}}$\,\rangle$}\verb@@\\
\mbox{}\verb@             break;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@           }@\\
\mbox{}\verb@         putc(c, file);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@                 indent++;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@                 break;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    }@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    c = source_get();@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  }@\\
\mbox{}\verb@}@\\
\mbox{}\verb@@{\NWsep}
\end{list}
\vspace{-1ex}
\footnotesize\addtolength{\baselineskip}{-1ex}
\begin{list}{}{\setlength{\itemsep}{-\parsep}\setlength{\itemindent}{-\leftmargin}}
\item \NWtxtFileDefBy\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}.
\end{list}
\vspace{-2ex}
\footnotesize\addtolength{\baselineskip}{-1ex}
\begin{list}{}{\setlength{\itemsep}{-\parsep}\setlength{\itemindent}{-\leftmargin}}

\begin{flushleft} \small
\begin{minipage}{\linewidth} \label{scrap114}
$\langle\,${\it Check HTML at-sequence for end-of-scrap}\nobreak\ {\footnotesize \NWtarget{nuweb?}{?}}$\,\rangle\equiv$
\vspace{-1ex}
\begin{list}{}{} \item
\mbox{}\verb@{@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  c = source_get();@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  switch (c) {@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    case '+':@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    case '-':@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    case '|': @\hbox{$\langle\,${\it Skip over index entries}\nobreak\ {\footnotesize \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}}$\,\rangle$}\verb@@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    case ',': @\\
\mbox{}\verb@    case '}': @\\
\mbox{}\verb@    case ']': @\\
\mbox{}\verb@    case ')': return;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    case '_': @\hbox{$\langle\,${\it Write HTML bold tag or end}\nobreak\ {\footnotesize \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}}$\,\rangle$}\verb@@\\
\mbox{}\verb@              break;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    case '1': case '2': case '3': @\\
\mbox{}\verb@    case '4': case '5': case '6': @\\
\mbox{}\verb@    case '7': case '8': case '9': @\\
\mbox{}\verb@              fputc(nw_char, file);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@              fputc(c,   file);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@              break;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    case '<': @\hbox{$\langle\,${\it Format HTML macro name}\nobreak\ {\footnotesize \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}}$\,\rangle$}\verb@@\\
\mbox{}\verb@              break;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    case '%': @\hbox{$\langle\,${\it Skip commented-out code}\nobreak\ {\footnotesize \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}}$\,\rangle$}\verb@@\\
\mbox{}\verb@              break;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    default:  @\\
\mbox{}\verb@         if (c==nw_char)@\\
\mbox{}\verb@           {@\\
\mbox{}\verb@             fputc(c, file);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@             break;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@           }@\\
\mbox{}\verb@          /* ignore these since pass1 will have warned about them */@\\
\mbox{}\verb@              break;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  }@\\
\mbox{}\verb@}@{\NWsep}
\end{list}
\vspace{-1ex}
\footnotesize\addtolength{\baselineskip}{-1ex}
\begin{list}{}{\setlength{\itemsep}{-\parsep}\setlength{\itemindent}{-\leftmargin}}
\item \NWtxtMacroRefIn\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}.
\end{list}
\vspace{-2ex}
\footnotesize\addtolength{\baselineskip}{-1ex}
\begin{list}{}{\setlength{\itemsep}{-\parsep}\setlength{\itemindent}{-\leftmargin}}
\item \NWtxtIdentsUsed\nobreak\  \verb@nw_char@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}, \verb@pass1@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}, \verb@source_get@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}.\end{list}
\end{minipage}\\[4ex]
\end{flushleft}
There's no need to check for errors here, since we will have already
pointed out any during the first pass.

\begin{flushleft} \small
\begin{minipage}{\linewidth} \label{scrap126}
\verb@"html.c"@\nobreak\ {\footnotesize \NWtarget{nuweb?}{?} }$\equiv$
\vspace{-1ex}
\begin{list}{}{} \item

\mbox{}\verb@     Name *name;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@     FILE *html_file;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@{@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  while (name) {@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    format_user_entry(name->llink, html_file, sector);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    @\hbox{$\langle\,${\it Format a user HTML index entry}\nobreak\ {\footnotesize \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}}$\,\rangle$}\verb@@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    name = name->rlink;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  }@\\
\mbox{}\verb@}@\\
\mbox{}\verb@@{\NWsep}
\end{list}

\end{flushleft}
\begin{flushleft} \small
\begin{minipage}{\linewidth} \label{scrap127}
$\langle\,${\it Format a user HTML index entry}\nobreak\ {\footnotesize \NWtarget{nuweb?}{?}}$\,\rangle\equiv$
\vspace{-1ex}
\begin{list}{}{} \item
\mbox{}\verb@{@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  Scrap_Node *uses = name->uses;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  if (uses) {@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    Scrap_Node *defs = name->defs;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    fprintf(html_file, "<dt><code>%s</code>:\n<dd> ", name->spelling);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    if (uses->scrap < defs->scrap) {@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      display_scrap_ref(html_file, uses->scrap);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      uses = uses->next;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    }@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    else {@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      if (defs->scrap == uses->scrap)@\\
\mbox{}\verb@        uses = uses->next;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      fputs("<strong>", html_file);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      display_scrap_ref(html_file, defs->scrap);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      fputs("</strong>", html_file);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      defs = defs->next;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    }@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    while (uses || defs) {@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      fputs(", ", html_file);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      if (uses && (!defs || uses->scrap < defs->scrap)) {@\\
\mbox{}\verb@        display_scrap_ref(html_file, uses->scrap);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@        uses = uses->next;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      }@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      else {@\\
\mbox{}\verb@        if (uses && defs->scrap == uses->scrap)@\\
\mbox{}\verb@          uses = uses->next;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@        fputs("<strong>", html_file);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@        display_scrap_ref(html_file, defs->scrap);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@        fputs("</strong>", html_file);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@        defs = defs->next;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      }@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    }@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    fputs(".\n", html_file);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  }@\\
\mbox{}\verb@}@{\NWsep}
\end{list}
\vspace{-1ex}
\footnotesize\addtolength{\baselineskip}{-1ex}
\begin{list}{}{\setlength{\itemsep}{-\parsep}\setlength{\itemindent}{-\leftmargin}}
\item \NWtxtMacroRefIn\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}.
\end{list}
\vspace{-2ex}
\footnotesize\addtolength{\baselineskip}{-1ex}
\begin{list}{}{\setlength{\itemsep}{-\parsep}\setlength{\itemindent}{-\leftmargin}}
\item \NWtxtIdentsUsed\nobreak\  \verb@display_scrap_ref@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}, \verb@fprintf@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}, \verb@fputs@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}, \verb@Scrap_Node@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}.\end{list}
\end{minipage}\\[4ex]
\end{flushleft}

\begin{flushleft} \small

\begin{list}{}{\setlength{\itemsep}{-\parsep}\setlength{\itemindent}{-\leftmargin}}

\vspace{-2ex}
\footnotesize\addtolength{\baselineskip}{-1ex}
\begin{list}{}{\setlength{\itemsep}{-\parsep}\setlength{\itemindent}{-\leftmargin}}
\item \NWtxtIdentsUsed\nobreak\  \verb@Name@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}.\end{list}
\end{minipage}\\[4ex]
\end{flushleft}
We call \verb|tempnam|, causing it to create a file name in the
current directory.  This could cause a problem for \verb|rename| if
the eventual output file will reside on a different file system.

To avoid this, we used to set the environment variable \verb|TMPDIR| 
to \verb|"."| at the beginning of the program, but since we got rid of
tempnam(), we no longer bother.

\begin{flushleft} \small
\begin{minipage}{\linewidth} \label{scrap130}
$\langle\,${\it Avoid rename() problems}\nobreak\ {\footnotesize \NWtarget{nuweb?}{?}}$\,\rangle\equiv$
\vspace{-1ex}
\begin{list}{}{} \item
\mbox{}\verb@@\\
\mbox{}\verb@@{\NWsep}
\end{list}
\vspace{-1ex}
\footnotesize\addtolength{\baselineskip}{-1ex}
\begin{list}{}{\setlength{\itemsep}{-\parsep}\setlength{\itemindent}{-\leftmargin}}
\item \NWtxtMacroRefIn\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}.
\end{list}
\end{minipage}\\[4ex]
\end{flushleft}
Note the call to \verb|remove| before \verb|rename| --
The ANSI/ISO C standard does {\em not}
guarantee that renaming a file to an existing filename 
will overwrite the file. 

Note: I've modified this on 2001-02-15 for compilation
for Win32 with Borland C++ (assuming \verb|MSDOS| is defined). The second
argument to \verb|tempname| cannot be null in that system.
\begin{flushleft} \small
\begin{minipage}{\linewidth} \label{scrap131}
$\langle\,${\it Type declarations}\nobreak\ {\footnotesize \NWtarget{nuweb?}{?}}$\,\rangle\equiv$
\vspace{-1ex}
\begin{list}{}{} \item
\mbox{}\verb@@\\
\mbox{}\verb@#define MAX_INDENT 1500@\\
\mbox{}\verb@@{\NWsep}
\end{list}
\vspace{-1ex}
\footnotesize\addtolength{\baselineskip}{-1ex}
\begin{list}{}{\setlength{\itemsep}{-\parsep}\setlength{\itemindent}{-\leftmargin}}
\item \NWtxtMacroDefBy\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}.
\item \NWtxtMacroRefIn\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}.
\end{list}
\end{minipage}\\[4ex]
\end{flushleft}
\begin{flushleft} \small
\begin{minipage}{\linewidth} \label{scrap132}
$\langle\,${\it Write out \verb|files->spelling|}\nobreak\ {\footnotesize \NWtarget{nuweb?}{?}}$\,\rangle\equiv$
\vspace{-1ex}
\begin{list}{}{} \item
\mbox{}\verb@{@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  static char temp_name[FILENAME_MAX];@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  static char real_name[FILENAME_MAX];@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  static int temp_name_count = 0;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  char indent_chars[MAX_INDENT];@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  int temp_file_fd;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  FILE *temp_file;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  for( temp_name_count = 0; temp_name_count < 10000; temp_name_count++) {@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    sprintf(temp_name,"%s%snw%06d", dirpath, path_sep, temp_name_count);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@#ifdef O_EXCL@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    if (-1 != (temp_file_fd = open(temp_name, O_CREAT|O_WRONLY|O_EXCL))) {@\\
\mbox{}\verb@       temp_file = fdopen(temp_file_fd, "w");@\\
\mbox{}\verb@       break;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    }@\\
\mbox{}\verb@#else@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    if (0 != (temp_file = fopen(temp_name, "a"))) {@\\
\mbox{}\verb@       if ( 0L == ftell(temp_file)) {@\\
\mbox{}\verb@          break;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@       } else {@\\
\mbox{}\verb@          fclose(temp_file);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@          temp_file = 0;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@       }@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    }@\\
\mbox{}\verb@#endif@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  }@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  if (!temp_file) {@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    fprintf(stderr, "%s: can't create %s for a temporary file\n",@\\
\mbox{}\verb@            command_name, temp_name);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    exit(-1);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  }  @\\
\mbox{}\verb@  sprintf(real_name, "%s%s%s", dirpath, path_sep, files->spelling);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  if (verbose_flag)@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    fprintf(stderr, "writing %s [%s]\n", files->spelling, temp_name);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  write_scraps(temp_file, files->spelling, files->defs, 0, indent_chars,@\\
\mbox{}\verb@               files->debug_flag, files->tab_flag, files->indent_flag, 0);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  fclose(temp_file);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  if (compare_flag)@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    @\hbox{$\langle\,${\it Compare the temp file and the old file}\nobreak\ {\footnotesize \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}}$\,\rangle$}\verb@@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  else {@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    remove(real_name);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    if (rename(temp_name, real_name)==-1)@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      remove(temp_name);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  }@\\
\mbox{}\verb@}@{\NWsep}
\end{list}
\vspace{-1ex}
\footnotesize\addtolength{\baselineskip}{-1ex}
\begin{list}{}{\setlength{\itemsep}{-\parsep}\setlength{\itemindent}{-\leftmargin}}
\item \NWtxtMacroRefIn\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}.
\end{list}
\vspace{-2ex}
\footnotesize\addtolength{\baselineskip}{-1ex}
\begin{list}{}{\setlength{\itemsep}{-\parsep}\setlength{\itemindent}{-\leftmargin}}
\item \NWtxtIdentsUsed\nobreak\  \verb@command_name@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}, \verb@compare_flag@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}, \verb@exit@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}, \verb@fclose@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}, \verb@FILE@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}, \verb@fopen@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}, \verb@fprintf@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}, \verb@remove@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}, \verb@stderr@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}, \verb@verbose_flag@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}, \verb@write_scraps@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}.\end{list}
\end{minipage}\\[4ex]
\end{flushleft}
Again, we use a call to \verb|remove| before \verb|rename|.
\begin{flushleft} \small
\begin{minipage}{\linewidth} \label{scrap133}
$\langle\,${\it Compare the temp file and the old file}\nobreak\ {\footnotesize \NWtarget{nuweb?}{?}}$\,\rangle\equiv$
\vspace{-1ex}
\begin{list}{}{} \item
\mbox{}\verb@{@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  FILE *old_file = fopen(real_name, "r");@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  if (old_file) {@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    int x, y;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    temp_file = fopen(temp_name, "r");@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    do {@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      x = getc(old_file);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      y = getc(temp_file);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    } while (x == y && x != EOF);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    fclose(old_file);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    fclose(temp_file);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    if (x == y)@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      remove(temp_name);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    else {@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      remove(real_name);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      if (rename(temp_name, real_name)==-1)@\\
\mbox{}\verb@        remove(temp_name);      @\\
\mbox{}\verb@    }@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  }@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  else {@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    if (rename(temp_name, real_name)==-1)@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      remove(temp_name);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  }@\\
\mbox{}\verb@}@{\NWsep}
\end{list}
\vspace{-1ex}
\footnotesize\addtolength{\baselineskip}{-1ex}
\begin{list}{}{\setlength{\itemsep}{-\parsep}\setlength{\itemindent}{-\leftmargin}}
\item \NWtxtMacroRefIn\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}.
\end{list}
\vspace{-2ex}
\footnotesize\addtolength{\baselineskip}{-1ex}
\begin{list}{}{\setlength{\itemsep}{-\parsep}\setlength{\itemindent}{-\leftmargin}}
\item \NWtxtIdentsUsed\nobreak\  \verb@fclose@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}, \verb@FILE@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}, \verb@fopen@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}, \verb@getc@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}, \verb@remove@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}.\end{list}
\end{minipage}\\[4ex]
\end{flushleft}

\subsection{Local Declarations}


\begin{flushleft} \small

\item \NWtxtFileDefBy\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}.

\footnotesize\addtolength{\baselineskip}{-1ex}
\begin{list}{}{\setlength{\itemsep}{-\parsep}\setlength{\itemindent}{-\leftmargin}}
\item \NWtxtIdentsDefed\nobreak\  \verb@double_at@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}, \verb@include_depth@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}, \verb@source_file@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}, \verb@source_peek@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}.\end{list}
\vspace{-2ex}
\footnotesize\addtolength{\baselineskip}{-1ex}
\begin{list}{}{\setlength{\itemsep}{-\parsep}\setlength{\itemindent}{-\leftmargin}}
\item \NWtxtIdentsUsed\nobreak\  \verb@FILE@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}.\end{list}
\end{minipage}\\[4ex]
\end{flushleft}
\begin{flushleft} \small
\begin{minipage}{\linewidth} \label{scrap138}
\verb@"input.c"@\nobreak\ {\footnotesize \NWtarget{nuweb?}{?} }$\equiv$
\vspace{-1ex}
\begin{list}{}{} \item
\mbox{}\verb@static struct {@\\

\mbox{}\verb@  char *name;@\\
