\subsection{Reading a File}

The routine \verb|source_get| returns the next character from the
current source file. It notices newlines and keeps the line counter 
\verb|source_line| up to date. It also catches \verb|EOF| and watches
for \verb|@|~characters. All other characters are immediately returned.
We define \verb|source_last| to let us tell which type of scrap we
are defining.
\begin{flushleft} \small
\begin{minipage}{\linewidth} \label{scrap139}
\verb@"input.c"@\nobreak\ {\footnotesize \NWtarget{nuweb?}{?} }$\equiv$
\vspace{-1ex}
\begin{list}{}{} \item
\mbox{}\verb@@\\
\mbox{}\verb@int source_last;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@int source_get()@\\
\mbox{}\verb@{@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  int c;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  source_last = c = source_peek;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  switch (c) {@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    case EOF:  @\hbox{$\langle\,${\it Handle \verb|EOF|}\nobreak\ {\footnotesize \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}}$\,\rangle$}\verb@@\\
\mbox{}\verb@               return c;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    case '\n': source_line++;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    default:@\\
\mbox{}\verb@           if (c==nw_char)@\\
\mbox{}\verb@             {@\\
\mbox{}\verb@               @\hbox{$\langle\,${\it Handle an ``at'' character}\nobreak\ {\footnotesize \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}}$\,\rangle$}\verb@@\\
\mbox{}\verb@               return c;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@             }@\\
\mbox{}\verb@           source_peek = getc(source_file);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@               return c;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  }@\\
\mbox{}\verb@}@\\
\mbox{}\verb@@{\NWsep}
\end{list}
\vspace{-1ex}
\footnotesize\addtolength{\baselineskip}{-1ex}
\begin{list}{}{\setlength{\itemsep}{-\parsep}\setlength{\itemindent}{-\leftmargin}}
\item \NWtxtFileDefBy\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}.
\end{list}
\vspace{-2ex}
\footnotesize\addtolength{\baselineskip}{-1ex}
\begin{list}{}{\setlength{\itemsep}{-\parsep}\setlength{\itemindent}{-\leftmargin}}
\item \NWtxtIdentsDefed\nobreak\  \verb@source_get@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}, \verb@source_last@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}.\end{list}
\vspace{-2ex}
\footnotesize\addtolength{\baselineskip}{-1ex}
\begin{list}{}{\setlength{\itemsep}{-\parsep}\setlength{\itemindent}{-\leftmargin}}
\item \NWtxtIdentsUsed\nobreak\  \verb@getc@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}, \verb@nw_char@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}, \verb@source_file@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}, \verb@source_line@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}, \verb@source_peek@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}.\end{list}
\end{minipage}\\[4ex]
\end{flushleft}
\verb|source_ungetc| pushes a read character back to the \verb|source_file|.
\begin{flushleft} \small
\begin{minipage}{\linewidth} \label{scrap140}
\verb@"input.c"@\nobreak\ {\footnotesize \NWtarget{nuweb?}{?} }$\equiv$
\vspace{-1ex}
\begin{list}{}{} \item
\mbox{}\verb@int source_ungetc(int *c)@\\
\mbox{}\verb@{       @\\
\mbox{}\verb@        ungetc(source_peek, source_file);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@        if(*c == '\n') @\\
\mbox{}\verb@                source_line--;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@   source_peek=*c;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@}@\\
\mbox{}\verb@@{\NWsep}
\end{list}
\vspace{-1ex}
\footnotesize\addtolength{\baselineskip}{-1ex}
\begin{list}{}{\setlength{\itemsep}{-\parsep}\setlength{\itemindent}{-\leftmargin}}
\item \NWtxtFileDefBy\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}.
\end{list}
\vspace{-2ex}
\footnotesize\addtolength{\baselineskip}{-1ex}
\begin{list}{}{\setlength{\itemsep}{-\parsep}\setlength{\itemindent}{-\leftmargin}}
\item \NWtxtIdentsDefed\nobreak\  \verb@source_ungetc@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}.\end{list}
\vspace{-2ex}
\footnotesize\addtolength{\baselineskip}{-1ex}
\begin{list}{}{\setlength{\itemsep}{-\parsep}\setlength{\itemindent}{-\leftmargin}}
\item \NWtxtIdentsUsed\nobreak\  \verb@source_file@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}, \verb@source_line@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}, \verb@source_peek@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}.\end{list}
\end{minipage}\\[4ex]
\end{flushleft}
This whole \verb|@|~character handling mess is pretty annoying.
I want to recognize \verb|@i| so I can handle include files correctly.
At the same time, it makes sense to recognize illegal \verb|@|~sequences
and complain; this avoids ever having to check anywhere else.
Unfortunately, I need to avoid tripping over the \verb|@@|~sequence;
hence this whole unsatisfactory \verb|double_at| business.
\begin{flushleft} \small
\begin{minipage}{\linewidth} \label{scrap141}
$\langle\,${\it Handle an ``at'' character}\nobreak\ {\footnotesize \NWtarget{nuweb?}{?}}$\,\rangle\equiv$
\vspace{-1ex}
\begin{list}{}{} \item
\mbox{}\verb@{@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  c = getc(source_file);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  if (double_at) {@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    source_peek = c;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    double_at = FALSE;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    c = nw_char;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  }@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  else@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    switch (c) {@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      case 'i': @\hbox{$\langle\,${\it Open an include file}\nobreak\ {\footnotesize \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}}$\,\rangle$}\verb@@\\
\mbox{}\verb@                break;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      case '#': case 'f': case 'm': case 'u':@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      case 'd': case 'o': case 'D': case 'O': case 's':@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      case '+':@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      case '-':@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      case '{': case '}': case '<': case '>': case '|':@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      case '(': case ')': case '[': case ']':@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      case '%': case '_':@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      case ':': case ',': case 'x':@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      case '1': case '2': case '3': case '4': case '5': @\\
\mbox{}\verb@      case '6': case '7': case '8': case '9': @\\
\mbox{}\verb@      case 'r':@\\
\mbox{}\verb@                source_peek = c;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@                c = nw_char;        @\\
\mbox{}\verb@                break;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      default:  @\\
\mbox{}\verb@            if (c==nw_char)@\\
\mbox{}\verb@              {@\\
\mbox{}\verb@                source_peek = c;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@                double_at = TRUE;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@                break;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@              }@\\
\mbox{}\verb@             fprintf(stderr, "%s: bad %c sequence %c[%d] (%s, line %d)\n",@\\
\mbox{}\verb@                     command_name, nw_char, c, c, source_name, source_line);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@             exit(-1);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    }@\\
\mbox{}\verb@}@{\NWsep}
\end{list}
\vspace{-1ex}
\footnotesize\addtolength{\baselineskip}{-1ex}
\begin{list}{}{\setlength{\itemsep}{-\parsep}\setlength{\itemindent}{-\leftmargin}}
\item \NWtxtMacroRefIn\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}.
\end{list}
\vspace{-2ex}
\footnotesize\addtolength{\baselineskip}{-1ex}
\begin{list}{}{\setlength{\itemsep}{-\parsep}\setlength{\itemindent}{-\leftmargin}}
\item \NWtxtIdentsUsed\nobreak\  \verb@command_name@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}, \verb@double_at@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}, \verb@exit@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}, \verb@FALSE@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}, \verb@fprintf@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}, \verb@getc@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}, \verb@nw_char@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}, \verb@source_file@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}, \verb@source_line@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}, \verb@source_name@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}, \verb@source_peek@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}, \verb@stderr@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}, \verb@TRUE@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}.\end{list}
\end{minipage}\\[4ex]
\end{flushleft}
\begin{flushleft} \small
\begin{minipage}{\linewidth} \label{scrap142}
$\langle\,${\it Open an include file}\nobreak\ {\footnotesize \NWtarget{nuweb?}{?}}$\,\rangle\equiv$
\vspace{-1ex}
\begin{list}{}{} \item
\mbox{}\verb@{@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  char name[100];@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  if (include_depth >= 10) {@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    fprintf(stderr, "%s: include nesting too deep (%s, %d)\n",@\\
\mbox{}\verb@            command_name, source_name, source_line);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    exit(-1);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  }@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  @\hbox{$\langle\,${\it Collect include-file name}\nobreak\ {\footnotesize \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}}$\,\rangle$}\verb@@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  stack[include_depth].name = source_name;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  stack[include_depth].file = source_file;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  stack[include_depth].line = source_line + 1;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  include_depth++;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  source_line = 1;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  source_name = save_string(name);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  source_file = fopen(source_name, "r");@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  if (!source_file) {@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    fprintf(stderr, "%s: can't open include file %s\n",@\\
\mbox{}\verb@     command_name, source_name);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    exit(-1);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  }@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  source_peek = getc(source_file);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  c = source_get();@\\
\mbox{}\verb@}@{\NWsep}
\end{list}
\vspace{-1ex}
\footnotesize\addtolength{\baselineskip}{-1ex}
\begin{list}{}{\setlength{\itemsep}{-\parsep}\setlength{\itemindent}{-\leftmargin}}
\item \NWtxtMacroRefIn\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}.
\end{list}
\vspace{-2ex}
\footnotesize\addtolength{\baselineskip}{-1ex}
\begin{list}{}{\setlength{\itemsep}{-\parsep}\setlength{\itemindent}{-\leftmargin}}
\item \NWtxtIdentsUsed\nobreak\  \verb@command_name@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}, \verb@exit@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}, \verb@fopen@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}, \verb@fprintf@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}, \verb@getc@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}, \verb@include_depth@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}, \verb@save_string@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}, \verb@source_file@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}, \verb@source_get@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}, \verb@source_line@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}, \verb@source_name@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}, \verb@source_peek@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}, \verb@stack@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}, \verb@stderr@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}.\end{list}
\end{minipage}\\[4ex]
\end{flushleft}
\begin{flushleft} \small
\begin{minipage}{\linewidth} \label{scrap143}
$\langle\,${\it Collect include-file name}\nobreak\ {\footnotesize \NWtarget{nuweb?}{?}}$\,\rangle\equiv$
\vspace{-1ex}
\begin{list}{}{} \item
\mbox{}\verb@{@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    char *p = name;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    do @\\
\mbox{}\verb@      c = getc(source_file);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    while (c == ' ' || c == '\t');@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    while (isgraph(c)) {@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      *p++ = c;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      c = getc(source_file);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    }@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    *p = '\0';@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    if (c != '\n') {@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      fprintf(stderr, "%s: unexpected characters after file name (%s, %d)\n",@\\
\mbox{}\verb@              command_name, source_name, source_line);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      exit(-1);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    }@\\
\mbox{}\verb@}@{\NWsep}
\end{list}
\vspace{-1ex}
\footnotesize\addtolength{\baselineskip}{-1ex}
\begin{list}{}{\setlength{\itemsep}{-\parsep}\setlength{\itemindent}{-\leftmargin}}
\item \NWtxtMacroRefIn\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}.
\end{list}
\vspace{-2ex}
\footnotesize\addtolength{\baselineskip}{-1ex}
\begin{list}{}{\setlength{\itemsep}{-\parsep}\setlength{\itemindent}{-\leftmargin}}
\item \NWtxtIdentsUsed\nobreak\  \verb@command_name@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}, \verb@exit@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}, \verb@fprintf@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}, \verb@getc@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}, \verb@isgraph@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}, \verb@source_file@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}, \verb@source_line@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}, \verb@source_name@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}, \verb@stderr@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}.\end{list}
\end{minipage}\\[4ex]
\end{flushleft}
If an \verb|EOF| is discovered, the current file must be closed and
input from the next stacked file must be resumed. If no more files are
on the stack, the \verb|EOF| is returned.
\begin{flushleft} \small
\begin{minipage}{\linewidth} \label{scrap144}
$\langle\,${\it Handle \verb|EOF|}\nobreak\ {\footnotesize \NWtarget{nuweb?}{?}}$\,\rangle\equiv$
\vspace{-1ex}
\begin{list}{}{} \item
\mbox{}\verb@{@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  fclose(source_file);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  if (include_depth) {@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    include_depth--;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    source_file = stack[include_depth].file;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    source_line = stack[include_depth].line;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    source_name = stack[include_depth].name;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    source_peek = getc(source_file);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    c = source_get();@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  }@\\
\mbox{}\verb@}@{\NWsep}
\end{list}
\vspace{-1ex}
\footnotesize\addtolength{\baselineskip}{-1ex}
\begin{list}{}{\setlength{\itemsep}{-\parsep}\setlength{\itemindent}{-\leftmargin}}
\item \NWtxtMacroRefIn\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}.
\end{list}
\vspace{-2ex}
\footnotesize\addtolength{\baselineskip}{-1ex}
\begin{list}{}{\setlength{\itemsep}{-\parsep}\setlength{\itemindent}{-\leftmargin}}
\item \NWtxtIdentsUsed\nobreak\  \verb@fclose@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}, \verb@getc@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}, \verb@include_depth@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}, \verb@source_file@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}, \verb@source_get@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}, \verb@source_line@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}, \verb@source_name@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}, \verb@source_peek@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}, \verb@stack@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}.\end{list}
\end{minipage}\\[4ex]
\end{flushleft}
\subsection{Opening a File}

The routine \verb|source_open| takes a file name and tries to open the
file. If unsuccessful, it complains and halts. Otherwise, it sets 
\verb|source_name|, \verb|source_line|, and \verb|double_at|.
\begin{flushleft} \small
\begin{minipage}{\linewidth} \label{scrap145}
\verb@"input.c"@\nobreak\ {\footnotesize \NWtarget{nuweb?}{?} }$\equiv$
\vspace{-1ex}
\begin{list}{}{} \item
\mbox{}\verb@void source_open(name)@\\
\mbox{}\verb@     char *name;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@{@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  source_file = fopen(name, "r");@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  if (!source_file) {@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    fprintf(stderr, "%s: couldn't open %s\n", command_name, name);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    exit(-1);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  }@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  nw_char = '@{\tt @}\verb@';@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  source_name = name;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  source_line = 1;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  source_peek = getc(source_file);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  double_at = FALSE;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  include_depth = 0;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@}@\\
\mbox{}\verb@@{\NWsep}
\end{list}
\vspace{-1ex}
\footnotesize\addtolength{\baselineskip}{-1ex}
\begin{list}{}{\setlength{\itemsep}{-\parsep}\setlength{\itemindent}{-\leftmargin}}
\item \NWtxtFileDefBy\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}.
\end{list}
\vspace{-2ex}
\footnotesize\addtolength{\baselineskip}{-1ex}
\begin{list}{}{\setlength{\itemsep}{-\parsep}\setlength{\itemindent}{-\leftmargin}}
\item \NWtxtIdentsDefed\nobreak\  \verb@source_open@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}.\end{list}
\vspace{-2ex}
\footnotesize\addtolength{\baselineskip}{-1ex}
\begin{list}{}{\setlength{\itemsep}{-\parsep}\setlength{\itemindent}{-\leftmargin}}
\item \NWtxtIdentsUsed\nobreak\  \verb@command_name@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}, \verb@double_at@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}, \verb@exit@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}, \verb@FALSE@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}, \verb@fopen@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}, \verb@fprintf@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}, \verb@getc@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}, \verb@include_depth@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}, \verb@nw_char@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}, \verb@source_file@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}, \verb@source_line@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}, \verb@source_name@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}, \verb@source_peek@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}, \verb@stderr@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}.\end{list}
\end{minipage}\\[4ex]
\end{flushleft}
\section{Scraps} \label{scraps}


\begin{flushleft} \small
\begin{minipage}{\linewidth} \label{scrap146}
\verb@"scraps.c"@\nobreak\ {\footnotesize \NWtarget{nuweb?}{?} }$\equiv$
\vspace{-1ex}
\begin{list}{}{} \item
\mbox{}\verb@#define SLAB_SIZE 500@\\
\mbox{}\verb@@\\
\mbox{}\verb@typedef struct slab {@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  struct slab *next;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  char chars[SLAB_SIZE];@\\
\mbox{}\verb@} Slab;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@@{\NWsep}
\end{list}
\vspace{-1ex}

\begin{minipage}{\linewidth} \label{scrap151}
\verb@"scraps.c"@\nobreak\ {\footnotesize \NWtarget{nuweb?}{?} }$\equiv$
\vspace{-1ex}
\begin{list}{}{} \item
\mbox{}\verb@void write_scrap_ref(file, num, first, page)@\\
\mbox{}\verb@     FILE *file;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@     int num;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@     int first;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@     int *page;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@{@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  if (scrap_array(num).page >= 0) {@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    if (first!=0)@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      fprintf(file, "%d", scrap_array(num).page);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    else if (scrap_array(num).page != *page)@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      fprintf(file, ", %d", scrap_array(num).page);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    if (scrap_array(num).letter > 0)@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      fputc(scrap_array(num).letter, file);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  }@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  else {@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    if (first!=0)@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      putc('?', file);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    else@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      fputs(", ?", file);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    @\hbox{$\langle\,${\it Warn (only once) about needing to rerun after Latex}\nobreak\ {\footnotesize \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}}$\,\rangle$}\verb@@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  }@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  if (first>=0)@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  *page = scrap_array(num).page;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@}@\\
\mbox{}\verb@@{\NWsep}
\end{list}

\mbox{}\verb@  scrap->chars[index++] = c;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  if (index == SLAB_SIZE) {@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    Slab *new = (Slab *) arena_getmem(sizeof(Slab));@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    scrap->next = new;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    manager->scrap = new;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    index = 0;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  }@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  manager->index = index;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@}@\\
\mbox{}\verb@@{\NWsep}

\mbox{}\verb@        if (c==nw_char)@\\
\mbox{}\verb@          {@\\
\mbox{}\verb@            @\hbox{$\langle\,${\it Handle at-sign during scrap accumulation}\nobreak\ {\footnotesize \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}}$\,\rangle$}\verb@@\\
\mbox{}\verb@                break;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@          }@\\
\mbox{}\verb@        push(c, &writer);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@                c = source_get();@\\

\mbox{}\verb@    }@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  }@\\
\mbox{}\verb@}@{\NWsep}

\begin{flushleft} \small
\begin{minipage}{\linewidth} \label{scrap162}
$\langle\,${\it Handle at-sign during scrap accumulation}\nobreak\ {\footnotesize \NWtarget{nuweb?}{?}}$\,\rangle\equiv$
\vspace{-1ex}
\begin{list}{}{} \item
\mbox{}\verb@{@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  c = source_get();@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  switch (c) {@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    case '(':@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    case '[':@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    case '{': depth++;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@              break;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    case '+':@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    case '-':@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    case '|': @\hbox{$\langle\,${\it Collect user-specified index entries}\nobreak\ {\footnotesize \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}}$\,\rangle$}\verb@@\\
\mbox{}\verb@              /* Fall through */@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    case ')':@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    case ']':@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    case '}': if (--depth > 0)@\\
\mbox{}\verb@                break;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@              /* else fall through */@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    case ',':@\\
\mbox{}\verb@              push('\0', &writer);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@              scrap_ended_with = c;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@              return current_scrap;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    case '<': @\hbox{$\langle\,${\it Handle macro invocation in scrap}\nobreak\ {\footnotesize \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}}$\,\rangle$}\verb@@\\
\mbox{}\verb@              break;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    case '%': @\hbox{$\langle\,${\it Skip commented-out code}\nobreak\ {\footnotesize \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}}$\,\rangle$}\verb@@\\
\mbox{}\verb@              /* emit line break to the output file to keep #line in sync. */@\\
\mbox{}\verb@              push('\n', &writer); @\\
\mbox{}\verb@              c = source_get();@\\
\mbox{}\verb@              break;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    case 'x': @\hbox{$\langle\,${\it Get label while collecting scrap}\nobreak\ {\footnotesize \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}}$\,\rangle$}\verb@@\\
\mbox{}\verb@              break;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    case '1': case '2': case '3':@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    case '4': case '5': case '6':@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    case '7': case '8': case '9':@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    case 'f': case '#':@\\
\mbox{}\verb@              push(nw_char, &writer);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@              break;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    case '_': c = source_get();@\\
\mbox{}\verb@              break;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    default : @\\
\mbox{}\verb@          if (c==nw_char)@\\
\mbox{}\verb@            {@\\
\mbox{}\verb@              push(nw_char, &writer);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@              push(nw_char, &writer);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@              c = source_get();@\\
\mbox{}\verb@              break;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@            }@\\
\mbox{}\verb@          fprintf(stderr, "%s: unexpected %c%c in scrap (%s, %d)\n",@\\
\mbox{}\verb@                      command_name, nw_char, c, source_name, source_line);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@              exit(-1);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  }@\\
\mbox{}\verb@}@{\NWsep}
\end{list}

\begin{flushleft} \small
\begin{minipage}{\linewidth} \label{scrap165}
$\langle\,${\it Collect user-specified index entries}\nobreak\ {\footnotesize \NWtarget{nuweb?}{?}}$\,\rangle\equiv$
\vspace{-1ex}
\begin{list}{}{} \item
\mbox{}\verb@{@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  do {@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    int type = c;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    do {@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    char new_name[100];@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    char *p = new_name;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      unsigned int sector = 0;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    do @\\
\mbox{}\verb@      c = source_get();@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    while (isspace(c));@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    if (c != nw_char) {@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      Name *name;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      do {@\\
\mbox{}\verb@        *p++ = c;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@        c = source_get();@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      } while (c != nw_char && !isspace(c));@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      *p = '\0';@\\
\mbox{}\verb@        switch (type) {@\\
\mbox{}\verb@        case '-':@\\
\mbox{}\verb@           @\hbox{$\langle\,${\it Add user identifier use}\nobreak\ {\footnotesize \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}}$\,\rangle$}\verb@@\\
\mbox{}\verb@           /* Fall through */@\\
\mbox{}\verb@        case '|': sector = current_sector;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@           /* Fall through */@\\
\mbox{}\verb@        case '+':@\\
\mbox{}\verb@           @\hbox{$\langle\,${\it Add user identifier definition}\nobreak\ {\footnotesize \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}}$\,\rangle$}\verb@@\\
\mbox{}\verb@           break;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      }@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    }@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  } while (c != nw_char);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  c = source_get();@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  }while (c == '+' || c == '-' || c == '|');@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  if (c != '}' && c != ']' && c != ')') {@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    fprintf(stderr, "%s: unexpected %c%c in index entry (%s, %d)\n",@\\
\mbox{}\verb@            command_name, nw_char, c, source_name, source_line);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    exit(-1);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  }@\\
\mbox{}\verb@}@{\NWsep}
\end{list}

\verb@"scraps.c"@\nobreak\ {\footnotesize \NWtarget{nuweb?}{?} }$\equiv$
\vspace{-1ex}
\begin{list}{}{} \item
\mbox{}\verb@static char pop(manager)@\\
\mbox{}\verb@     Manager *manager;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@{@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  Slab *scrap = manager->scrap;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  int index = manager->index;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  char c = scrap->chars[index++];@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  if (index == SLAB_SIZE) {@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    manager->prev = scrap;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    manager->scrap = scrap->next;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    index = 0;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  }@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  manager->index = index;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  return c;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@}@\\
\mbox{}\verb@@{\NWsep}
\end{list}
\vspace{-1ex}

\mbox{}\verb@{@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  Slab *scrap = manager->scrap;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  int index = manager->index;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  if (n > index@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      && manager->prev != NULL)@\\

\mbox{}\verb@     manager->scrap = manager->prev;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@     manager->prev = NULL;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@     index += SLAB_SIZE;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  }@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  manager->index = (n <= index ? index - n : 0);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@}@\\
\mbox{}\verb@@{\NWsep}
\end{list}

\begin{minipage}{\linewidth} \label{scrap174}
$\langle\,${\it Check for end of scrap name and return}\nobreak\ {\footnotesize \NWtarget{nuweb?}{?}}$\,\rangle\equiv$
\vspace{-1ex}
\begin{list}{}{} \item
\mbox{}\verb@{@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  Name *pn;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  c = pop(manager);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  if (c == nw_char) {@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    *p++ = c;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    c = pop(manager);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  }@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  @\hbox{$\langle\,${\it Check for macro parameters}\nobreak\ {\footnotesize \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}}$\,\rangle$}\verb@@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  if (c == '>') {@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    if (p - name > 3 && p[-1] == '.' && p[-2] == '.' && p[-3] == '.') {@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      p[-3] = ' ';@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      p -= 2;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    }@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    *p = '\0';@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    pn = prefix_add(&macro_names, name, sector);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    return pn;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  }@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  else {@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    fprintf(stderr, "%s: found an internal problem (1)\n", command_name);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    exit(-1);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  }@\\
\mbox{}\verb@}@{\NWsep}
\end{list}

\mbox{}\verb@{@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  char c;@\\

\mbox{}\verb@  reader.index = 0;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  @\hbox{$\langle\,${\it Insert debugging information if required}\nobreak\ {\footnotesize \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}}$\,\rangle$}\verb@@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  if (delayed_indent)@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  {@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    @\hbox{$\langle\,${\it Insert appropriate indentation}\nobreak\ {\footnotesize \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}}$\,\rangle$}\verb@@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    delayed_indent--;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  }@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  c = pop(&reader);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  while (c) {@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    switch (c) {@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      case '\n': putc(c, file);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@                 line_number++;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@                 @\hbox{$\langle\,${\it Insert appropriate indentation}\nobreak\ {\footnotesize \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}}$\,\rangle$}\verb@@\\
\mbox{}\verb@                 break;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      case '\t': @\hbox{$\langle\,${\it Handle tab characters on output}\nobreak\ {\footnotesize \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}}$\,\rangle$}\verb@@\\
\mbox{}\verb@                 break;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      default:@\\
\mbox{}\verb@         if (c==nw_char)@\\
\mbox{}\verb@           {@\\
\mbox{}\verb@             @\hbox{$\langle\,${\it Check for macro invocation in scrap}\nobreak\ {\footnotesize \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}}$\,\rangle$}\verb@@\\
\mbox{}\verb@             break;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@           }         @\\
\mbox{}\verb@          putc(c, file);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@          if (global_indent + indent < MAX_INDENT) {@\\
\mbox{}\verb@             indent_chars[global_indent + indent] = ' ';@\\
\mbox{}\verb@             indent++;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@          }@\\
\mbox{}\verb@          break;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    }@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    c = pop(&reader);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  }@\\
\mbox{}\verb@}@{\NWsep}
\end{list}

\begin{flushleft} \small
\begin{minipage}{\linewidth} \label{scrap179}
$\langle\,${\it Insert appropriate indentation}\nobreak\ {\footnotesize \NWtarget{nuweb?}{?}}$\,\rangle\equiv$
\vspace{-1ex}
\begin{list}{}{} \item
\mbox{}\verb@{@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  char c1 = pop(&reader);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  char c2 = pop(&reader);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  if (indent_flag && !(@\hbox{$\langle\,${\it Indent suppressed}\nobreak\ {\footnotesize \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}}$\,\rangle$}\verb@)) {@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    if (tab_flag)@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      for (indent=0; indent<global_indent; indent++)@\\
\mbox{}\verb@        putc(' ', file);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    else@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      for (indent=0; indent<global_indent; indent++)@\\
\mbox{}\verb@        putc(indent_chars[indent], file);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  }@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  indent = 0;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  backup(2, &reader);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@}@{\NWsep}
\end{list}
\vspace{-1ex}
\footnotesize\addtolength{\baselineskip}{-1ex}
\begin{list}{}{\setlength{\itemsep}{-\parsep}\setlength{\itemindent}{-\leftmargin}}
\item \NWtxtMacroRefIn\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}.
\end{list}
\vspace{-2ex}
\footnotesize\addtolength{\baselineskip}{-1ex}
\begin{list}{}{\setlength{\itemsep}{-\parsep}\setlength{\itemindent}{-\leftmargin}}
\item \NWtxtIdentsUsed\nobreak\  \verb@backup@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}, \verb@pop@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}, \verb@putc@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}.\end{list}
\end{minipage}\\[4ex]
\end{flushleft}
Indent will be suppressed if the next character is a newline or
if the next two characters are \verb|@#|. If the next two characters
are \verb|@<|, we suppress the indent for now but mark that it
may be needed when the next macro is started.

\begin{flushleft} \small
\begin{minipage}{\linewidth} \label{scrap180}
$\langle\,${\it Indent suppressed}\nobreak\ {\footnotesize \NWtarget{nuweb?}{?}}$\,\rangle\equiv$
\vspace{-1ex}
\begin{list}{}{} \item
\mbox{}\verb@c1 == '\n'@\\
\mbox{}\verb@|| c1 == nw_char && (c2 == '#' || (delayed_indent += (c2 == '<')))@{\NWsep}
\end{list}
\vspace{-1ex}
\footnotesize\addtolength{\baselineskip}{-1ex}
\begin{list}{}{\setlength{\itemsep}{-\parsep}\setlength{\itemindent}{-\leftmargin}}
\item \NWtxtMacroRefIn\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}.
\end{list}
\vspace{-2ex}
\footnotesize\addtolength{\baselineskip}{-1ex}
\begin{list}{}{\setlength{\itemsep}{-\parsep}\setlength{\itemindent}{-\leftmargin}}
\item \NWtxtIdentsUsed\nobreak\  \verb@delayed_indent@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}, \verb@nw_char@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}.\end{list}
\end{minipage}\\[4ex]
\end{flushleft}
\begin{flushleft} \small
\begin{minipage}{\linewidth} \label{scrap181}

\mbox{}\verb@  else {@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    putc('\t', file);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    if (global_indent + indent < MAX_INDENT) {@\\
\mbox{}\verb@        indent_chars[global_indent + indent] = '\t';@\\

\mbox{}\verb@    }@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  }@\\

\mbox{}\verb@              break;@\\

\mbox{}\verb@  }@\\

\mbox{}\verb@    fprintf(stderr, "%s: recursive macro discovered involving <%s>\n",@\\

\mbox{}\verb@    exit(-1);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  }@\\

\mbox{}\verb@    indent -= global_indent;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    name->mark = FALSE;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  }@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  else@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  {@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    if (undefined_flag) {    @\\
\mbox{}\verb@      int ln = fprintf(file, "%c<%s%c>",  nw_char, name->spelling, nw_char);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      for (; --ln >= 0;)@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      {@\\
\mbox{}\verb@        indent_chars[global_indent + indent] = ' ';@\\
\mbox{}\verb@        indent++;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      }@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    }@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    if (!tex_flag)@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    fprintf(stderr, "%s: macro never defined <%s>\n",@\\
\mbox{}\verb@            command_name, name->spelling);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  }@\\
\mbox{}\verb@}@{\NWsep}
\end{list}

\subsection{Collecting Page Numbers}

\begin{flushleft} \small
\begin{minipage}{\linewidth} \label{scrap187}
$\langle\,${\it Function prototypes}\nobreak\ {\footnotesize \NWtarget{nuweb?}{?}}$\,\rangle\equiv$
\vspace{-1ex}
\begin{list}{}{} \item

\mbox{}\verb@@{\NWsep}
\end{list}
\vspace{-1ex}
\footnotesize\addtolength{\baselineskip}{-1ex}
\begin{list}{}{\setlength{\itemsep}{-\parsep}\setlength{\itemindent}{-\leftmargin}}
\item \NWtxtMacroDefBy\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}.
\item \NWtxtMacroRefIn\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}.
\end{list}
\vspace{-2ex}
\footnotesize\addtolength{\baselineskip}{-1ex}
\begin{list}{}{\setlength{\itemsep}{-\parsep}\setlength{\itemindent}{-\leftmargin}}
\item \NWtxtIdentsUsed\nobreak\  \verb@collect_numbers@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}.\end{list}
\end{minipage}\\[4ex]
\end{flushleft}
\begin{flushleft} \small
\begin{minipage}{\linewidth} \label{scrap188}
\verb@"scraps.c"@\nobreak\ {\footnotesize \NWtarget{nuweb?}{?} }$\equiv$
\vspace{-1ex}
\begin{list}{}{} \item
\mbox{}\verb@void collect_numbers(aux_name)@\\
\mbox{}\verb@     char *aux_name;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@{@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  if (number_flag) {@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    int i;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    for (i=1; i<scraps; i++)@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      scrap_array(i).page = i;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  }@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  else {@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    FILE *aux_file = fopen(aux_name, "r");@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    already_warned = FALSE;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    if (aux_file) {@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      char aux_line[500];@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      while (fgets(aux_line, 500, aux_file)) {@\\
\mbox{}\verb@        int scrap_number;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@        int page_number;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@        char dummy[50];@\\
\mbox{}\verb@        if (3 == sscanf(aux_line, "\\newlabel{scrap%d}{%[^}]}{%d}",@\\
\mbox{}\verb@                        &scrap_number, dummy, &page_number)) {@\\
\mbox{}\verb@          if (scrap_number < scraps)@\\
\mbox{}\verb@            scrap_array(scrap_number).page = page_number;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@          else@\\
\mbox{}\verb@            @\hbox{$\langle\,${\it Warn (only once) about needing to rerun after Latex}\nobreak\ {\footnotesize \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}}$\,\rangle$}\verb@@\\
\mbox{}\verb@        }@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      }@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      fclose(aux_file);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      @\hbox{$\langle\,${\it Add letters to scraps with duplicate page numbers}\nobreak\ {\footnotesize \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}}$\,\rangle$}\verb@@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    }@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  }@\\
\mbox{}\verb@}@\\
\mbox{}\verb@@{\NWsep}
\end{list}
\vspace{-1ex}
\footnotesize\addtolength{\baselineskip}{-1ex}
\begin{list}{}{\setlength{\itemsep}{-\parsep}\setlength{\itemindent}{-\leftmargin}}
\item \NWtxtFileDefBy\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}.
\end{list}
\vspace{-2ex}
\footnotesize\addtolength{\baselineskip}{-1ex}
\begin{list}{}{\setlength{\itemsep}{-\parsep}\setlength{\itemindent}{-\leftmargin}}
\item \NWtxtIdentsDefed\nobreak\  \verb@collect_numbers@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}.\end{list}
\vspace{-2ex}

\begin{flushleft} \small
\begin{minipage}{\linewidth} \label{scrap195}
\verb@"names.c"@\nobreak\ {\footnotesize \NWtarget{nuweb?}{?} }$\equiv$
\vspace{-1ex}
\begin{list}{}{} \item
\mbox{}\verb@enum { LESS, GREATER, EQUAL, PREFIX, EXTENSION };@\\
\mbox{}\verb@@\\
\mbox{}\verb@static int compare(x, y)@\\
\mbox{}\verb@     char *x;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@     char *y;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@{@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  int len, result;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  int xl = strlen(x);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  int yl = strlen(y);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  int xp = x[xl - 1] == ' ';@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  int yp = y[yl - 1] == ' ';@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  if (xp) xl--;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  if (yp) yl--;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  len = xl < yl ? xl : yl;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  result = strncmp(x, y, len);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  if (result < 0) return GREATER;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  else if (result > 0) return LESS;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  else if (xl < yl) {@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    if (xp) return EXTENSION;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    else return LESS;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  }@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  else if (xl > yl) {@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    if (yp) return PREFIX;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    else return GREATER;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  }@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  else return EQUAL;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@}@\\
\mbox{}\verb@@{\NWsep}
\end{list}
\vspace{-1ex}
\footnotesize\addtolength{\baselineskip}{-1ex}
\begin{list}{}{\setlength{\itemsep}{-\parsep}\setlength{\itemindent}{-\leftmargin}}
\item \NWtxtFileDefBy\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}.
\end{list}
\vspace{-2ex}
\footnotesize\addtolength{\baselineskip}{-1ex}
\begin{list}{}{\setlength{\itemsep}{-\parsep}\setlength{\itemindent}{-\leftmargin}}
\item \NWtxtIdentsDefed\nobreak\  \verb@compare@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}, \verb@EQUAL@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}, \verb@EXTENSION@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}, \verb@GREATER@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}, \verb@LESS@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}, \verb@PREFIX@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}.\end{list}

\begin{flushleft} \small
\begin{minipage}{\linewidth} \label{scrap197}
\verb@"names.c"@\nobreak\ {\footnotesize \NWtarget{nuweb?}{?} }$\equiv$
\vspace{-1ex}
\begin{list}{}{} \item
\mbox{}\verb@static int ambiguous_prefix();@\\
\mbox{}\verb@@\\
\mbox{}\verb@static char * found_name = NULL;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@@\\
\mbox{}\verb@Name *prefix_add(rt, spelling, sector)@\\
\mbox{}\verb@     Name **rt;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@     char *spelling;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@     unsigned char sector;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@{@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  Name *node = *rt;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  int cmp;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  while (node) {@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    switch ((cmp = compare(node->spelling, spelling))) {@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    case GREATER:   rt = &node->rlink;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@                    break;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    case LESS:      rt = &node->llink;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@                    break;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    case EQUAL:@\\
\mbox{}\verb@                    found_name = node->spelling;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    case EXTENSION: if (node->sector > sector) {@\\
\mbox{}\verb@                       rt = &node->rlink;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@                       break;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@                    }@\\
\mbox{}\verb@                    else if (node->sector < sector) {@\\
\mbox{}\verb@                       rt = &node->llink;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@                       break;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@                    }@\\
\mbox{}\verb@                    if (cmp == EXTENSION)@\\
\mbox{}\verb@                       node->spelling = save_string(spelling);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@                    return node;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    case PREFIX:    @\hbox{$\langle\,${\it Check for ambiguous prefix}\nobreak\ {\footnotesize \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}}$\,\rangle$}\verb@@\\
\mbox{}\verb@                    return node;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    }@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    node = *rt;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  }@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  @\hbox{$\langle\,${\it Create new name entry}\nobreak\ {\footnotesize \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}}$\,\rangle$}\verb@@\\
\mbox{}\verb@}@\\
\mbox{}\verb@@{\NWsep}
\end{list}
\vspace{-1ex}
\footnotesize\addtolength{\baselineskip}{-1ex}
\begin{list}{}{\setlength{\itemsep}{-\parsep}\setlength{\itemindent}{-\leftmargin}}
\item \NWtxtFileDefBy\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}.
\end{list}
\vspace{-2ex}
\footnotesize\addtolength{\baselineskip}{-1ex}
\begin{list}{}{\setlength{\itemsep}{-\parsep}\setlength{\itemindent}{-\leftmargin}}
\item \NWtxtIdentsDefed\nobreak\  \verb@prefix_add@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}.\end{list}
\vspace{-2ex}
\footnotesize\addtolength{\baselineskip}{-1ex}
\begin{list}{}{\setlength{\itemsep}{-\parsep}\setlength{\itemindent}{-\leftmargin}}
\item \NWtxtIdentsUsed\nobreak\  \verb@compare@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}, \verb@EQUAL@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}, \verb@EXTENSION@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}, \verb@GREATER@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}, \verb@LESS@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}, \verb@Name@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}, \verb@PREFIX@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}, \verb@save_string@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}.\end{list}
\end{minipage}\\[4ex]
\end{flushleft}
Since a very short prefix might match more than one macro name, I need
to check for other matches to avoid mistakes. Basically, I simply
continue the search down {\em both\/} branches of the tree.

\begin{flushleft} \small
\begin{minipage}{\linewidth} \label{scrap198}
$\langle\,${\it Check for ambiguous prefix}\nobreak\ {\footnotesize \NWtarget{nuweb?}{?}}$\,\rangle\equiv$
\vspace{-1ex}
\begin{list}{}{} \item
\mbox{}\verb@{@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  if (ambiguous_prefix(node->llink, spelling, sector) ||@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      ambiguous_prefix(node->rlink, spelling, sector))@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    fprintf(stderr,@\\
\mbox{}\verb@            "%s: ambiguous prefix %c<%s...%c> (%s, line %d)\n",@\\
\mbox{}\verb@            command_name, nw_char, spelling, nw_char, source_name, source_line);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@}@{\NWsep}
\end{list}
\vspace{-1ex}
\footnotesize\addtolength{\baselineskip}{-1ex}
\begin{list}{}{\setlength{\itemsep}{-\parsep}\setlength{\itemindent}{-\leftmargin}}
\item \NWtxtMacroRefIn\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}.
\end{list}
\vspace{-2ex}
\footnotesize\addtolength{\baselineskip}{-1ex}
\begin{list}{}{\setlength{\itemsep}{-\parsep}\setlength{\itemindent}{-\leftmargin}}
\item \NWtxtIdentsUsed\nobreak\  \verb@command_name@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}, \verb@fprintf@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}, \verb@nw_char@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}, \verb@source_line@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}, \verb@source_name@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}, \verb@stderr@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}.\end{list}
\end{minipage}\\[4ex]
\end{flushleft}
\begin{flushleft} \small
\begin{minipage}{\linewidth} \label{scrap199}
\verb@"names.c"@\nobreak\ {\footnotesize \NWtarget{nuweb?}{?} }$\equiv$
\vspace{-1ex}
\begin{list}{}{} \item
\mbox{}\verb@static int ambiguous_prefix(node, spelling, sector)@\\
\mbox{}\verb@     Name *node;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@     char *spelling;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@     unsigned char sector;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@{@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  while (node) {@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    switch (compare(node->spelling, spelling)) {@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    case GREATER:   node = node->rlink;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@                    break;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    case LESS:      node = node->llink;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@                    break;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    case EXTENSION:@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    case PREFIX:@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    case EQUAL:     if (node->sector > sector) {@\\
\mbox{}\verb@                       node = node->rlink;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@                       break;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@                    }@\\
\mbox{}\verb@                    else if (node->sector < sector) {@\\
\mbox{}\verb@                       node = node->llink;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@                       break;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@                    }@\\
\mbox{}\verb@                    return TRUE;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    }@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  }@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  return FALSE;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@}@\\
\mbox{}\verb@@{\NWsep}
\end{list}
\vspace{-1ex}
\footnotesize\addtolength{\baselineskip}{-1ex}
\begin{list}{}{\setlength{\itemsep}{-\parsep}\setlength{\itemindent}{-\leftmargin}}
\item \NWtxtFileDefBy\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}.
\end{list}

\footnotesize\addtolength{\baselineskip}{-1ex}

\end{flushleft}
Rob Shillingsburg suggested that I organize the index of
user-specified identifiers more traditionally; that is, not relying on
strict {\small ASCII} comparisons via \verb|strcmp|. Ideally, we'd like
to see the index ordered like this:
\begin{quote}
\begin{flushleft}
aardvark \\
Adam \\
atom \\
Atomic \\
atoms
\end{flushleft}
\end{quote}
The function \verb|robs_strcmp| implements the desired predicate.

\begin{flushleft} \small
\begin{minipage}{\linewidth} \label{scrap200}
\verb@"names.c"@\nobreak\ {\footnotesize \NWtarget{nuweb?}{?} }$\equiv$
\vspace{-1ex}
\begin{list}{}{} \item
\mbox{}\verb@int robs_strcmp(x, y)@\\
\mbox{}\verb@     char *x;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@     char *y;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@{@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  char *xx = x;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  char *yy = y;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  int xc = toupper(*xx);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  int yc = toupper(*yy);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  while (xc == yc && xc) {@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    xx++;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    yy++;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    xc = toupper(*xx);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    yc = toupper(*yy);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  }@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  if (xc != yc) return xc - yc;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  xc = *x;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  yc = *y;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  while (xc == yc && xc) {@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    x++;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    y++;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    xc = *x;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    yc = *y;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  }@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  if (isupper(xc) && islower(yc))@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    return xc * 2 - (toupper(yc) * 2 + 1);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  if (islower(xc) && isupper(yc))@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    return toupper(xc) * 2 + 1 - yc * 2;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  return xc - yc;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@}@\\
\mbox{}\verb@@{\NWsep}
\end{list}
\vspace{-1ex}
\footnotesize\addtolength{\baselineskip}{-1ex}
\begin{list}{}{\setlength{\itemsep}{-\parsep}\setlength{\itemindent}{-\leftmargin}}
\item \NWtxtFileDefBy\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}.
\end{list}
\vspace{-2ex}
\footnotesize\addtolength{\baselineskip}{-1ex}
\begin{list}{}{\setlength{\itemsep}{-\parsep}\setlength{\itemindent}{-\leftmargin}}
\item \NWtxtIdentsDefed\nobreak\  \verb@robs_strcmp@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}.\end{list}
\vspace{-2ex}
\footnotesize\addtolength{\baselineskip}{-1ex}
\begin{list}{}{\setlength{\itemsep}{-\parsep}\setlength{\itemindent}{-\leftmargin}}
\item \NWtxtIdentsUsed\nobreak\  \verb@islower@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}, \verb@isupper@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}, \verb@toupper@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}.\end{list}
\end{minipage}\\[4ex]
\end{flushleft}
\begin{flushleft} \small
\begin{minipage}{\linewidth} \label{scrap201}
\verb@"names.c"@\nobreak\ {\footnotesize \NWtarget{nuweb?}{?} }$\equiv$
\vspace{-1ex}
\begin{list}{}{} \item
\mbox{}\verb@Name *name_add(rt, spelling, sector)@\\
\mbox{}\verb@     Name **rt;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@     char *spelling;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@     unsigned char sector;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@{@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  Name *node = *rt;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  while (node) {@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    int result = robs_strcmp(node->spelling, spelling);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    if (result > 0)@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      rt = &node->llink;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    else if (result < 0)@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      rt = &node->rlink;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    else@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    {@\\
\mbox{}\verb@       found_name = node->spelling;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@       if (node->sector > sector)@\\
\mbox{}\verb@         rt = &node->llink;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@       else if (node->sector < sector)@\\
\mbox{}\verb@         rt = &node->rlink;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    else@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      return node;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    }@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    node = *rt;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  }@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  @\hbox{$\langle\,${\it Create new name entry}\nobreak\ {\footnotesize \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}}$\,\rangle$}\verb@@\\
\mbox{}\verb@}@\\
\mbox{}\verb@@{\NWsep}
\end{list}
\vspace{-1ex}
\footnotesize\addtolength{\baselineskip}{-1ex}
\begin{list}{}{\setlength{\itemsep}{-\parsep}\setlength{\itemindent}{-\leftmargin}}

\end{list}

\begin{flushleft} \small
\begin{minipage}{\linewidth} \label{scrap202}
$\langle\,${\it Create new name entry}\nobreak\ {\footnotesize \NWtarget{nuweb?}{?}}$\,\rangle\equiv$
\vspace{-1ex}
\begin{list}{}{} \item
\mbox{}\verb@{@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  node = (Name *) arena_getmem(sizeof(Name));@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  if (found_name && robs_strcmp(found_name, spelling) == 0)@\\
\mbox{}\verb@     node->spelling = found_name;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  else@\\
\mbox{}\verb@     node->spelling = save_string(spelling);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  node->mark = FALSE;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  node->llink = NULL;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  node->rlink = NULL;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  node->uses = NULL;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  node->defs = NULL;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  node->tab_flag = TRUE;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  node->indent_flag = TRUE;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  node->debug_flag = FALSE;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  node->sector = sector;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  *rt = node;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  return node;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@}@{\NWsep}
\end{list}
\vspace{-1ex}
\footnotesize\addtolength{\baselineskip}{-1ex}
\begin{list}{}{\setlength{\itemsep}{-\parsep}\setlength{\itemindent}{-\leftmargin}}
\item \NWtxtMacroRefIn\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}.
\end{list}
\vspace{-2ex}
\footnotesize\addtolength{\baselineskip}{-1ex}
\begin{list}{}{\setlength{\itemsep}{-\parsep}\setlength{\itemindent}{-\leftmargin}}

\end{flushleft}
Name terminated by whitespace.  Also check for ``per-file'' flags. Keep
skipping white space until we reach scrap.
\begin{flushleft} \small
\begin{minipage}{\linewidth} \label{scrap203}
\verb@"names.c"@\nobreak\ {\footnotesize \NWtarget{nuweb?}{?} }$\equiv$
\vspace{-1ex}
\begin{list}{}{} \item
\mbox{}\verb@Name *collect_file_name()@\\
\mbox{}\verb@{@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  Name *new_name;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  char name[100];@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  char *p = name;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  int start_line = source_line;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  int c = source_get(), c2;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  while (isspace(c))@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    c = source_get();@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  while (isgraph(c)) {@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    *p++ = c;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    c = source_get();@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  }@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  if (p == name) {@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    fprintf(stderr, "%s: expected file name (%s, %d)\n",@\\
\mbox{}\verb@            command_name, source_name, start_line);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    exit(-1);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  }@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  *p = '\0';@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  /* File names are always global. */@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  new_name = name_add(&file_names, name, 0);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  @\hbox{$\langle\,${\it Handle optional per-file flags}\nobreak\ {\footnotesize \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}}$\,\rangle$}\verb@@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  c2 = source_get();@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  if (c != nw_char || (c2 != '{' && c2 != '(' && c2 != '[')) {@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    fprintf(stderr, "%s: expected %c{, %c[, or %c( after file name (%s, %d)\n",@\\
\mbox{}\verb@            command_name, nw_char, nw_char, nw_char, source_name, start_line);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    exit(-1);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  }@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  return new_name;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@}@\\
\mbox{}\verb@@{\NWsep}
\end{list}
\vspace{-1ex}
\footnotesize\addtolength{\baselineskip}{-1ex}
\begin{list}{}{\setlength{\itemsep}{-\parsep}\setlength{\itemindent}{-\leftmargin}}
\item \NWtxtFileDefBy\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}.
\end{list}
\vspace{-2ex}
\footnotesize\addtolength{\baselineskip}{-1ex}
\begin{list}{}{\setlength{\itemsep}{-\parsep}\setlength{\itemindent}{-\leftmargin}}
\item \NWtxtIdentsDefed\nobreak\  \verb@collect_file_name@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}.\end{list}
\vspace{-2ex}
\footnotesize\addtolength{\baselineskip}{-1ex}
\begin{list}{}{\setlength{\itemsep}{-\parsep}\setlength{\itemindent}{-\leftmargin}}
\item \NWtxtIdentsUsed\nobreak\  \verb@command_name@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}, \verb@exit@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}, \verb@file_names@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}, \verb@fprintf@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}, \verb@isgraph@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}, \verb@isspace@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}, \verb@Name@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}, \verb@name_add@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}, \verb@nw_char@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}, \verb@source_get@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}, \verb@source_line@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}, \verb@source_name@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}, \verb@stderr@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}.\end{list}
\end{minipage}\\[4ex]
\end{flushleft}
\begin{flushleft} \small
\begin{minipage}{\linewidth} \label{scrap204}
$\langle\,${\it Handle optional per-file flags}\nobreak\ {\footnotesize \NWtarget{nuweb?}{?}}$\,\rangle\equiv$
\vspace{-1ex}
\begin{list}{}{} \item
\mbox{}\verb@{@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  while (1) {@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    while (isspace(c))@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      c = source_get();@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    if (c == '-') {@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      c = source_get();@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      do {@\\
\mbox{}\verb@        switch (c) {@\\
\mbox{}\verb@          case 't': new_name->tab_flag = FALSE;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@                    break;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@          case 'd': new_name->debug_flag = TRUE;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@                    break;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@          case 'i': new_name->indent_flag = FALSE;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@                    break;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@          default : fprintf(stderr, "%s: unexpected per-file flag (%s, %d)\n",@\\
\mbox{}\verb@                            command_name, source_name, source_line);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@                    break;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@        }@\\
\mbox{}\verb@        c = source_get();@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      } while (!isspace(c));@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    }@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    else break;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  }@\\
\mbox{}\verb@}@{\NWsep}
\end{list}
\vspace{-1ex}
\footnotesize\addtolength{\baselineskip}{-1ex}
\begin{list}{}{\setlength{\itemsep}{-\parsep}\setlength{\itemindent}{-\leftmargin}}
\item \NWtxtMacroRefIn\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}.
\end{list}
\vspace{-2ex}
\footnotesize\addtolength{\baselineskip}{-1ex}
\begin{list}{}{\setlength{\itemsep}{-\parsep}\setlength{\itemindent}{-\leftmargin}}
\item \NWtxtIdentsUsed\nobreak\  \verb@command_name@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}, \verb@FALSE@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}, \verb@fprintf@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}, \verb@isspace@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}, \verb@source_get@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}, \verb@source_line@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}, \verb@stderr@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}, \verb@TRUE@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}.\end{list}
\end{minipage}\\[4ex]
\end{flushleft}
Name terminated by \verb+\n+ or \verb+@{+; but keep skipping until \verb+@{+
\begin{flushleft} \small
\begin{minipage}{\linewidth} \label{scrap205}
\verb@"names.c"@\nobreak\ {\footnotesize \NWtarget{nuweb?}{?} }$\equiv$
\vspace{-1ex}
\begin{list}{}{} \item
\mbox{}\verb@Name *collect_macro_name()@\\
\mbox{}\verb@{@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  char name[100];@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  char *p = name;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  int start_line = source_line;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  int c = source_get(), c2;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  unsigned char sector = current_sector;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  if (c == '+') {@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    sector = 0;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    c = source_get();@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  }@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  while (isspace(c))@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    c = source_get();@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  while (c != EOF) {@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    switch (c) {@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      case '\t':@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      case ' ':  *p++ = ' ';@\\
\mbox{}\verb@                 do@\\
\mbox{}\verb@                   c = source_get();@\\
\mbox{}\verb@                 while (c == ' ' || c == '\t');@\\
\mbox{}\verb@                 break;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      case '\n': @\hbox{$\langle\,${\it Skip until scrap begins, then return name}\nobreak\ {\footnotesize \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}}$\,\rangle$}\verb@@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      default:   @\\
\mbox{}\verb@         if (c==nw_char)@\\
\mbox{}\verb@           {@\\
\mbox{}\verb@             @\hbox{$\langle\,${\it Check for terminating at-sequence and return name}\nobreak\ {\footnotesize \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}}$\,\rangle$}\verb@@\\
\mbox{}\verb@             break;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@           }@\\
\mbox{}\verb@         *p++ = c;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@                 c = source_get();@\\
\mbox{}\verb@                 break;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    }@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  }@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  fprintf(stderr, "%s: expected macro name (%s, %d)\n",@\\
\mbox{}\verb@          command_name, source_name, start_line);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  exit(-1);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  return NULL;  /* unreachable return to avoid warnings on some compilers */@\\
\mbox{}\verb@}@\\
\mbox{}\verb@@{\NWsep}
\end{list}
\vspace{-1ex}
\footnotesize\addtolength{\baselineskip}{-1ex}
\begin{list}{}{\setlength{\itemsep}{-\parsep}\setlength{\itemindent}{-\leftmargin}}
\item \NWtxtFileDefBy\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}.
\end{list}
\vspace{-2ex}
\footnotesize\addtolength{\baselineskip}{-1ex}
\begin{list}{}{\setlength{\itemsep}{-\parsep}\setlength{\itemindent}{-\leftmargin}}
\item \NWtxtIdentsDefed\nobreak\  \verb@collect_macro_name@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}.\end{list}
\vspace{-2ex}
\footnotesize\addtolength{\baselineskip}{-1ex}
\begin{list}{}{\setlength{\itemsep}{-\parsep}\setlength{\itemindent}{-\leftmargin}}
\item \NWtxtIdentsUsed\nobreak\  \verb@command_name@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}, \verb@current_sector@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}, \verb@exit@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}, \verb@fprintf@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}, \verb@isspace@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}, \verb@Name@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}, \verb@nw_char@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}, \verb@source_get@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}, \verb@source_line@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}, \verb@source_name@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}, \verb@stderr@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}.\end{list}
\end{minipage}\\[4ex]
\end{flushleft}
\begin{flushleft} \small
\begin{minipage}{\linewidth} \label{scrap206}
$\langle\,${\it Check for terminating at-sequence and return name}\nobreak\ {\footnotesize \NWtarget{nuweb?}{?}}$\,\rangle\equiv$
\vspace{-1ex}
\begin{list}{}{} \item
\mbox{}\verb@{@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  c = source_get();@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  switch (c) {@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    case '(':@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    case '[':@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    case '{': @\hbox{$\langle\,${\it Cleanup and install name}\nobreak\ {\footnotesize \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}}$\,\rangle$}\verb@@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    default:  @\\
\mbox{}\verb@          if (c==nw_char)@\\
\mbox{}\verb@            {@\\
\mbox{}\verb@              *p++ = c;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@              break;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@            }@\\
\mbox{}\verb@          fprintf(stderr,@\\
\mbox{}\verb@                      "%s: unexpected %c%c in macro definition name (%s, %d)\n",@\\
\mbox{}\verb@                      command_name, nw_char, c, source_name, start_line);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@              exit(-1);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  }@\\
\mbox{}\verb@}@{\NWsep}
\end{list}
\vspace{-1ex}

\begin{flushleft} \small
\begin{minipage}{\linewidth} \label{scrap207}
$\langle\,${\it Cleanup and install name}\nobreak\ {\footnotesize \NWtarget{nuweb?}{?}}$\,\rangle\equiv$
\vspace{-1ex}
\begin{list}{}{} \item
\mbox{}\verb@{@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  if (p > name && p[-1] == ' ')@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    p--;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  if (p - name > 3 && p[-1] == '.' && p[-2] == '.' && p[-3] == '.') {@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    p[-3] = ' ';@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    p -= 2;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  }@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  if (p == name || name[0] == ' ') {@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    fprintf(stderr, "%s: empty name (%s, %d)\n",@\\
\mbox{}\verb@            command_name, source_name, source_line);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    exit(-1);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  }@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  *p = '\0';@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  return prefix_add(&macro_names, name, sector);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@}@{\NWsep}
\end{list}
\vspace{-1ex}
\footnotesize\addtolength{\baselineskip}{-1ex}

\mbox{}\verb@  }@\\

Terminated by \verb+@>+
\begin{flushleft} \small
\begin{minipage}{\linewidth} \label{scrap209}
\verb@"names.c"@\nobreak\ {\footnotesize \NWtarget{nuweb?}{?} }$\equiv$
\vspace{-1ex}
\begin{list}{}{} \item
\mbox{}\verb@Name *collect_scrap_name()@\\
\mbox{}\verb@{@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  char name[100];@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  char *p = name;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  int c = source_get();@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  unsigned char sector = current_sector;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  if (c == '+')@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  {@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    sector = 0;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    c = source_get();@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  }@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  while (c == ' ' || c == '\t')@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    c = source_get();@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  while (c != EOF) {@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    switch (c) {@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      case '\t':@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      case ' ':  *p++ = ' ';@\\
\mbox{}\verb@                 do@\\
\mbox{}\verb@                   c = source_get();@\\
\mbox{}\verb@                 while (c == ' ' || c == '\t');@\\
\mbox{}\verb@                 break;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      default:   @\\
\mbox{}\verb@         if (c==nw_char)@\\
\mbox{}\verb@           {@\\
\mbox{}\verb@             @\hbox{$\langle\,${\it Look for end of scrap name and return}\nobreak\ {\footnotesize \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}}$\,\rangle$}\verb@@\\
\mbox{}\verb@             break;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@           }@\\
\mbox{}\verb@         if (!isgraph(c)) {@\\
\mbox{}\verb@                   fprintf(stderr,@\\
\mbox{}\verb@                           "%s: unexpected character in macro name (%s, %d)\n",@\\
\mbox{}\verb@                           command_name, source_name, source_line);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@                   exit(-1);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@                 }@\\
\mbox{}\verb@                 *p++ = c;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@                 c = source_get();@\\
\mbox{}\verb@                 break;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    }@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  }@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  fprintf(stderr, "%s: unexpected end of file (%s, %d)\n",@\\
\mbox{}\verb@          command_name, source_name, source_line);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  exit(-1);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  return NULL;  /* unreachable return to avoid warnings on some compilers */@\\
\mbox{}\verb@}@\\
\mbox{}\verb@@{\NWsep}
\end{list}

\mbox{}\verb@        @\hbox{$\langle\,${\it Cleanup and install name}\nobreak\ {\footnotesize \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}}$\,\rangle$}\verb@@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    case '>': @\\
\mbox{}\verb@        scrap_name_has_parameters = 0;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@        @\hbox{$\langle\,${\it Cleanup and install name}\nobreak\ {\footnotesize \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}}$\,\rangle$}\verb@@\\
\mbox{}\verb@@\\

\mbox{}\verb@  }@\\

Just for fun, here's a non-recursive version of the traditional list
reversal code. Note that it reverses the list in place; that is, it
does no new allocations.
\begin{flushleft} \small
\begin{minipage}{\linewidth} \label{scrap212}
\verb@"names.c"@\nobreak\ {\footnotesize \NWtarget{nuweb?}{?} }$\equiv$
\vspace{-1ex}
\begin{list}{}{} \item
\mbox{}\verb@static Scrap_Node *reverse(a)@\\
\mbox{}\verb@     Scrap_Node *a;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@{@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  if (a) {@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    Scrap_Node *b = a->next;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    a->next = NULL;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    while (b) {@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      Scrap_Node *c = b->next;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      b->next = a;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      a = b;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      b = c;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    }@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  }@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  return a;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@}@\\
\mbox{}\verb@@{\NWsep}
\end{list}
\vspace{-1ex}
\footnotesize\addtolength{\baselineskip}{-1ex}
\begin{list}{}{\setlength{\itemsep}{-\parsep}\setlength{\itemindent}{-\leftmargin}}
\item \NWtxtFileDefBy\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}.
\end{list}
\vspace{-2ex}
\footnotesize\addtolength{\baselineskip}{-1ex}
\begin{list}{}{\setlength{\itemsep}{-\parsep}\setlength{\itemindent}{-\leftmargin}}
\item \NWtxtIdentsDefed\nobreak\  \verb@reverse@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}.\end{list}
\vspace{-2ex}
\footnotesize\addtolength{\baselineskip}{-1ex}
\begin{list}{}{\setlength{\itemsep}{-\parsep}\setlength{\itemindent}{-\leftmargin}}
\item \NWtxtIdentsUsed\nobreak\  \verb@Scrap_Node@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}.\end{list}
\end{minipage}\\[4ex]
\end{flushleft}
\section{Searching for Index Entries} \label{search}

Given the array of scraps and a set of index entries, we need to
search all the scraps for occurrences of each entry. The obvious
approach to this problem would be quite expensive for large documents;
however, there is an interesting  paper describing an efficient
solution~\cite{aho:75}.


\begin{flushleft} \small
\begin{minipage}{\linewidth} \label{scrap213}
\verb@"scraps.c"@\nobreak\ {\footnotesize \NWtarget{nuweb?}{?} }$\equiv$
\vspace{-1ex}
\begin{list}{}{} \item
\mbox{}\verb@typedef struct name_node {@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  struct name_node *next;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  Name *name;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@} Name_Node;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@@{\NWsep}
\end{list}
\vspace{-1ex}
\footnotesize\addtolength{\baselineskip}{-1ex}
\begin{list}{}{\setlength{\itemsep}{-\parsep}\setlength{\itemindent}{-\leftmargin}}
\item \NWtxtFileDefBy\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}.

\vspace{-2ex}

\begin{flushleft} \small
\begin{minipage}{\linewidth} \label{scrap221}
$\langle\,${\it Extend goto graph with \verb|tree->spelling|}\nobreak\ {\footnotesize \NWtarget{nuweb?}{?}}$\,\rangle\equiv$
\vspace{-1ex}
\begin{list}{}{} \item
\mbox{}\verb@{@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  int depth = 2;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  char *p = tree->spelling;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  char c = *p++;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  Goto_Node *q = root[c];@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  Name_Node * last;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  if (!q) {@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    q = (Goto_Node *) arena_getmem(sizeof(Goto_Node));@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    root[c] = q;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    q->moves = NULL;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    q->fail = NULL;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    q->moves = NULL;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    q->output = NULL;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    q->next = depths[1];@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    depths[1] = q;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  }@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  while (c = *p++) {@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    Goto_Node *new = goto_lookup(c, q);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    if (!new) {@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      Move_Node *new_move = (Move_Node *) arena_getmem(sizeof(Move_Node));@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      new = (Goto_Node *) arena_getmem(sizeof(Goto_Node));@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      new->moves = NULL;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      new->fail = NULL;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      new->moves = NULL;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      new->output = NULL;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      new_move->state = new;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      new_move->c = c;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      new_move->next = q->moves;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      q->moves = new_move;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      if (depth == max_depth) {@\\
\mbox{}\verb@        int i;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@        Goto_Node **new_depths =@\\
\mbox{}\verb@            (Goto_Node **) arena_getmem(2*depth*sizeof(Goto_Node *));@\\
\mbox{}\verb@        max_depth = 2 * depth;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@        for (i=0; i<depth; i++)@\\
\mbox{}\verb@          new_depths[i] = depths[i];@\\
\mbox{}\verb@        depths = new_depths;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@        for (i=depth; i<max_depth; i++)@\\
\mbox{}\verb@          depths[i] = NULL;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      }@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      new->next = depths[depth];@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      depths[depth] = new;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    }@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    q = new;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    depth++;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  }@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  last = q->output;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  q->output = (Name_Node *) arena_getmem(sizeof(Name_Node));@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  q->output->next = last;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  q->output->name = tree;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@}@{\NWsep}
\end{list}
\vspace{-1ex}
\footnotesize\addtolength{\baselineskip}{-1ex}
\begin{list}{}{\setlength{\itemsep}{-\parsep}\setlength{\itemindent}{-\leftmargin}}
\item \NWtxtMacroRefIn\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}.
\end{list}
\vspace{-2ex}
\footnotesize\addtolength{\baselineskip}{-1ex}
\begin{list}{}{\setlength{\itemsep}{-\parsep}\setlength{\itemindent}{-\leftmargin}}
\item \NWtxtIdentsUsed\nobreak\  \verb@arena_getmem@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}, \verb@depths@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}, \verb@goto_lookup@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}, \verb@Goto_Node@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}, \verb@max_depth@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}, \verb@Move_Node@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}, \verb@Name_Node@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}, \verb@root@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}.\end{list}
\end{minipage}\\[4ex]
\end{flushleft}
\begin{flushleft} \small
\begin{minipage}{\linewidth} \label{scrap222}
$\langle\,${\it Build failure functions}\nobreak\ {\footnotesize \NWtarget{nuweb?}{?}}$\,\rangle\equiv$
\vspace{-1ex}
\begin{list}{}{} \item
\mbox{}\verb@{@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  int depth;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  for (depth=1; depth<max_depth; depth++) {@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    Goto_Node *r = depths[depth];@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    while (r) {@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      Move_Node *m = r->moves;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      while (m) {@\\
\mbox{}\verb@        char a = m->c;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@        Goto_Node *s = m->state;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@        Goto_Node *state = r->fail;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@        while (state && !goto_lookup(a, state))@\\
\mbox{}\verb@          state = state->fail;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@        if (state)@\\
\mbox{}\verb@          s->fail = goto_lookup(a, state);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@        else@\\
\mbox{}\verb@          s->fail = root[a];@\\
\mbox{}\verb@        if (s->fail) {@\\
\mbox{}\verb@          Name_Node *p = s->fail->output;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@          while (p) {@\\
\mbox{}\verb@            Name_Node *q = (Name_Node *) arena_getmem(sizeof(Name_Node));@\\
\mbox{}\verb@            q->name = p->name;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@            q->next = s->output;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@            s->output = q;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@            p = p->next;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@          }@\\
\mbox{}\verb@        }@\\
\mbox{}\verb@        m = m->next;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      }@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      r = r->next;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    }@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  }@\\
\mbox{}\verb@}@{\NWsep}
\end{list}
\vspace{-1ex}
\footnotesize\addtolength{\baselineskip}{-1ex}
\begin{list}{}{\setlength{\itemsep}{-\parsep}\setlength{\itemindent}{-\leftmargin}}
\item \NWtxtMacroRefIn\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}.
\end{list}
\vspace{-2ex}
\footnotesize\addtolength{\baselineskip}{-1ex}
\begin{list}{}{\setlength{\itemsep}{-\parsep}\setlength{\itemindent}{-\leftmargin}}
\item \NWtxtIdentsUsed\nobreak\  \verb@arena_getmem@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}, \verb@depths@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}, \verb@goto_lookup@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}, \verb@Goto_Node@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}, \verb@max_depth@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}, \verb@Move_Node@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}, \verb@Name_Node@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}, \verb@root@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}.\end{list}
\end{minipage}\\[4ex]
\end{flushleft}
\subsection{Searching the Scraps}

\begin{flushleft} \small
\begin{minipage}{\linewidth} \label{scrap223}
$\langle\,${\it Search scraps}\nobreak\ {\footnotesize \NWtarget{nuweb?}{?}}$\,\rangle\equiv$
\vspace{-1ex}
\begin{list}{}{} \item
\mbox{}\verb@{@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  for (i=1; i<scraps; i++) {@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    signed char c, last = '\0';@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    Manager reader;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    Goto_Node *state = NULL;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    reader.prev = NULL;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    reader.scrap = scrap_array(i).slab;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    reader.index = 0;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    c = pop(&reader);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    while (c) {@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      while (state && !goto_lookup(c, state))@\\
\mbox{}\verb@        state = state->fail;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      if (state)@\\
\mbox{}\verb@        state = goto_lookup(c, state);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      else@\\
\mbox{}\verb@        state = root[c];@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      @\hbox{$\langle\,${\it Skip over a scrap use}\nobreak\ {\footnotesize \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}}$\,\rangle$}\verb@@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      c = pop(&reader);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      if (state && state->output) {@\\
\mbox{}\verb@        Name_Node *p = state->output;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@        do {@\\
\mbox{}\verb@          Name *name = p->name;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@          if (!reject_match(name, c, &reader) &&@\\
\mbox{}\verb@              scrap_array(i).sector == name->sector &&@\\
\mbox{}\verb@              (!name->uses || name->uses->scrap != i)) {@\\
\mbox{}\verb@            Scrap_Node *new_use =@\\
\mbox{}\verb@                (Scrap_Node *) arena_getmem(sizeof(Scrap_Node));@\\
\mbox{}\verb@            new_use->scrap = i;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@            new_use->next = name->uses;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@            name->uses = new_use;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@            if (!scrap_is_in(name->defs, i))@\\
\mbox{}\verb@              add_uses(&(scrap_array(i).uses), name);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@          }@\\
\mbox{}\verb@          p = p->next;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@        } while (p);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      }@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    }@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  }@\\
\mbox{}\verb@}@{\NWsep}
\end{list}
\vspace{-1ex}
\footnotesize\addtolength{\baselineskip}{-1ex}
\begin{list}{}{\setlength{\itemsep}{-\parsep}\setlength{\itemindent}{-\leftmargin}}
\item \NWtxtMacroRefIn\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}.
\end{list}
\vspace{-2ex}
\footnotesize\addtolength{\baselineskip}{-1ex}
\begin{list}{}{\setlength{\itemsep}{-\parsep}\setlength{\itemindent}{-\leftmargin}}
\item \NWtxtIdentsUsed\nobreak\  \verb@add_uses@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}, \verb@arena_getmem@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}, \verb@goto_lookup@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}, \verb@Goto_Node@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}, \verb@Manager@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}, \verb@Name@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}, \verb@Name_Node@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}, \verb@pop@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}, \verb@reject_match@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}, \verb@root@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}, \verb@scraps@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}, \verb@scrap_array@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}, \verb@scrap_is_in@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}, \verb@Scrap_Node@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}.\end{list}
\end{minipage}\\[4ex]
\end{flushleft}
\begin{flushleft} \small
\begin{minipage}{\linewidth} \label{scrap224}
$\langle\,${\it Skip over a scrap use}\nobreak\ {\footnotesize \NWtarget{nuweb?}{?}}$\,\rangle\equiv$
\vspace{-1ex}
\begin{list}{}{} \item
\mbox{}\verb@if (last == nw_char && c == '<')@\\
\mbox{}\verb@{@\\
\mbox{}\verb@   int n = 1;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@   c = pop(&reader);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@   do {@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      last = c;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      c = pop(&reader);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      if (last == nw_char)@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      {@\\
\mbox{}\verb@         if (c == '>')@\\
\mbox{}\verb@            n--;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@         else if (c == '<')@\\
\mbox{}\verb@            n++;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      }@\\
\mbox{}\verb@   }while (n > 0);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@}@\\
\mbox{}\verb@last = c;@{\NWsep}
\end{list}
\vspace{-1ex}
\footnotesize\addtolength{\baselineskip}{-1ex}
\begin{list}{}{\setlength{\itemsep}{-\parsep}\setlength{\itemindent}{-\leftmargin}}
\item \NWtxtMacroRefIn\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}.
\end{list}
\vspace{-2ex}
\footnotesize\addtolength{\baselineskip}{-1ex}
\begin{list}{}{\setlength{\itemsep}{-\parsep}\setlength{\itemindent}{-\leftmargin}}
\item \NWtxtIdentsUsed\nobreak\  \verb@nw_char@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}\NWlink{nuweb?}{, ?}, \verb@pop@\nobreak\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}.\end{list}
\end{minipage}\\[4ex]
\end{flushleft}

\begin{minipage}{\linewidth} \label{scrap227}
\verb@"scraps.c"@\nobreak\ {\footnotesize \NWtarget{nuweb?}{?} }$\equiv$
\vspace{-1ex}
\begin{list}{}{} \item
\mbox{}\verb@@\\
\mbox{}\verb@static void add_uses(Uses * * root, Name *name)@\\
\mbox{}\verb@{@\\
\mbox{}\verb@   int cmp;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@   Uses *p, **q = root;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@@\\
\mbox{}\verb@   while ((p = *q, p != NULL)@\\
\mbox{}\verb@          && (cmp = robs_strcmp(p->defn->spelling, name->spelling)) < 0)@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      q = &(p->next);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@   if (p == NULL || cmp > 0)@\\
\mbox{}\verb@   {@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      Uses *new = arena_getmem(sizeof(Uses));@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      new->next = p;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      new->defn = name;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@      *q = new;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@   }@\\
\mbox{}\verb@}@\\
\mbox{}\verb@@{\NWsep}
\end{list}

\begin{flushleft} \small
\begin{minipage}{\linewidth} \label{scrap235}
$\langle\,${\it Write one def reference}\nobreak\ {\footnotesize \NWtarget{nuweb?}{?}}$\,\rangle\equiv$
\vspace{-1ex}
\begin{list}{}{} \item
\mbox{}\verb@Name * name = p->defn;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@Scrap_Node *defs = name->uses;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@int first = TRUE, page = -1;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@fprintf(tex_file,@\\
\mbox{}\verb@        "%c \\verb%c%s%c\\nobreak\\ ",@\\
\mbox{}\verb@        join, nw_char, name->spelling, nw_char);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@if (defs == NULL@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    || (defs->scrap == scrap && defs->next == NULL)) {@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  fputs("\\NWtxtIdentsNotUsed", tex_file);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@}@\\
\mbox{}\verb@else {@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  do {@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    if (defs->scrap != scrap) {@\\
\mbox{}\verb@       @\hbox{$\langle\,${\it Write one referenced scrap}\nobreak\ {\footnotesize \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}}$\,\rangle$}\verb@@\\
\mbox{}\verb@       first = FALSE;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    }@\\
\mbox{}\verb@    defs = defs->next;@\\
\mbox{}\verb@  }while (defs!= NULL);@\\
\mbox{}\verb@}@\\
\mbox{}\verb@@{\NWsep}
\end{list}
\vspace{-1ex}
\footnotesize\addtolength{\baselineskip}{-1ex}
\begin{list}{}{\setlength{\itemsep}{-\parsep}\setlength{\itemindent}{-\leftmargin}}
\item \NWtxtMacroRefIn\ \NWlink{nuweb?}{?}.
\end{list}
\vspace{-2ex}
\footnotesize\addtolength{\baselineskip}{-1ex}
\begin{list}{}{\setlength{\itemsep}{-\parsep}\setlength{\itemindent}{-\leftmargin}}
